# math.SP [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [A reverse Faber--Krahn inequality for the Robin Laplacian with negative boundary parameter: small coupling in all dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24341)
*Nunzia Gavitone,David Krejcirik,Gloria Paoli*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文证明了 Bareket (1977) 关于弱边界耦合条件下凸域第一特征值的猜想：在边界参数足够接近零时，球体在所有固定体积的有界凸域中最大化第一特征值。证明依赖于通过平行坐标法（parallel coordinates）构造具有组合 Neumann-Robin 边界条件的球壳比较，以及对相应径向问题的细致分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证 Bareket 于 1977 年提出的关于凸域特征值优化问题的猜想，该猜想在所有维度下、弱边界耦合（weak boundary coupling）情形下尚未得到严格证明。

Method: 采用平行坐标法（method of parallel coordinates）构造具有组合 Neumann-Robin 边界条件（combined Neumann-Robin boundary conditions）的球壳比较对象，并结合对相应径向问题（radial problem）的细致分析来完成证明。

Result: 在所有维度下，对于受到负边界条件（negative boundary conditions）的拉普拉斯算子（Laplace operator），当边界参数足够接近零时，球体（ball）在固定体积的所有有界凸域（bounded convex domains）中最大化第一特征值（maximises the first eigenvalue）。该小量条件仅依赖于体积和维度。

Conclusion: 成功证实了 Bareket 猜想在弱边界耦合情形下对所有维度的凸域成立，并为类似特征值优化问题提供了一种基于平行坐标法和径向分析的证明框架。

Abstract: We establish Bareket's conjecture from 1977 for convex domains in all dimensions in the regime of weak boundary coupling. In other words, we consider the Laplace operator, subject to negative boundary conditions, and show that the ball maximises the first eigenvalue among all bounded convex domains of fixed volume, provided that the boundary parameter is sufficiently close to zero. The smallness depends on the volume and dimension only. The proof relies on a comparison with spherical shells with combined Neumann--Robin boundary conditions obtained via the method of parallel coordinates, which we manage to extend to all dimensions, and on a careful analysis of the corresponding radial problem.

</details>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Universal Dynamical Response to Slow Driving in Chaotic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23810)
*Nachiket Karve,Nathan Rose,David Campbell,Anatoli Polkovnikov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于慢驱动下稳态稳定性来统一刻画经典混沌（classical chaos）与量子混沌（quantum chaos）的理论框架。通过引入“速度-费舍信息”（speed-Fisher information）作为敏感度探针，并将其与不可逆熵产生（irreversible entropy production）相联系，证明混沌动力学表现为该信息量随协议时间发散，且该响应由扰动的低频谱权重控制。该框架同时适用于经典和量子哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian systems），并可自然推广至非哈密顿经典流（non-Hamiltonian classical flows）。(70词)


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典混沌与量子混沌长期缺乏统一的理论描述，现有方法往往局限于特定系统类型或动力学框架。本文旨在建立一种普适的判别准则，能够跨越经典与量子、哈密顿与非哈密顿系统的界限，从统计力学的基本概念出发统一理解混沌的本质。

Method: 论文提出以系统在慢驱动（slow driving）下稳态的稳定性作为混沌判据，通过定义“速度-费舍信息”（speed-Fisher information）来量化系统对平均协议速度的敏感度，并将该敏感度与不可逆熵产生（irreversible entropy production）建立关联。通过分析该信息量在协议时间尺度上的发散行为，以及扰动低频谱权重（low-frequency spectral weight）的控制作用，构建统一的混沌诊断方法。

Result: 混沌动力学表现为速度-费舍信息随协议时间发散；该发散响应受扰动低频谱权重控制。该框架在经典与量子哈密顿系统的简单示例中均得到了验证，并且在非哈密顿经典流中也定性地观察到类似的低频谱行为。

Conclusion: 该研究为经典与量子混沌提供了一种统一的理论视角，其核心机制——慢驱动下的稳定性与低频谱响应——不仅适用于哈密顿系统，还能自然延伸至非哈密顿经典流，暗示了一种超越具体系统类型的混沌普适刻画方式。

Abstract: We propose a unified perspective on classical and quantum chaos based on the stability of a system's stationary states under slow driving. We probe this sensitivity via the system's susceptibility to the average protocol speed, which we call the ``speed-Fisher information," and relate it to irreversible entropy production in the system. We show that chaotic dynamics manifests as a divergence of the speed-Fisher information with the protocol time, and that this response is controlled by the perturbation's low-frequency spectral weight. This approach to chaos applies to both classical and quantum Hamiltonian systems, and naturally extends to non-Hamiltonian classical flows. We illustrate this framework with simple classical and quantum examples, along with a non-Hamiltonian flow that qualitatively exhibits analogous low-frequency spectral behavior.

</details>


### [3] [Pareto-optimal control strategies in intrinsically nonequilibrium systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23828)
*Gustavo A. L. Forão,Carlos E. Fiore,Jonas Berx*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个多目标热力学控制（multi-objective thermodynamic control）的通用框架，能够绘制出本质非平衡系统中最优控制策略的完整帕累托前沿（Pareto front），并发现了一个单一内在尺度（intrinsic scale）统一支配了目标间的权衡、生成了整个前沿并定义了控制等价类（control equivalence classes）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热力学控制（thermodynamic control）通常被表述为单一目标的优化问题，然而实际系统中相互竞争的成本很少能同时达到最优，因此单目标控制只能捕获可达性能空间的一个角落。作者旨在发展一个适用于多目标情形的通用框架。

Method: 通过构建一个通用理论框架，将多目标热力学控制映射为完整的帕累托前沿（Pareto front）。作者从数学上证明了帕累托最优协议（Pareto-optimal protocols）通常由光滑分支和边界跳跃（boundary jumps）组成，且各目标的相对权重与物理参数合并为一个单一内在尺度（intrinsic scale），该尺度单独支配整个权衡关系。

Result: 该内在尺度具有双重作用：它参数化了一个单一函数形式，从而生成整个帕累托前沿；同时它定义了控制等价类，使得具有不同物理参数但相同内在尺度的系统共享完全相同的最优策略。作者将框架应用于两个实验上可实现的范式系统——谐振阱中的活性粒子（active particle in a harmonic trap）和循环量子点引擎（cyclic quantum-dot engine），并得到了两者的帕累托前沿和最优策略的闭式解（closed form）。

Conclusion: 多目标热力学控制的通用框架为本质非平衡系统提供了完整的最优控制图谱，并揭示了内在尺度作为核心控制参数的重要作用，为不同系统间的控制策略等价性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Thermodynamic control is typically formulated as the optimisation of a single objective, yet competing costs rarely admit a common optimum, so single-objective control captures only one corner of the achievable performance space. We develop a general framework for multi-objective thermodynamic control of intrinsically nonequilibrium systems that maps out the full Pareto front of optimal control strategies. We show that Pareto-optimal protocols generically consist of smooth branches connected by boundary jumps, and that the relative weights of the objectives combine with the physical parameters into a single intrinsic scale that alone governs the trade-off. Remarkably, this scale plays a double role: it parametrizes a single functional form that generates the entire front, and it defines control equivalence classes, in which systems with different parameters but the same scale share identical optimal strategies. We illustrate the framework for two paradigmatic systems that are experimentally accessible: transport of an active particle in a harmonic trap, and a cyclic quantum-dot engine. For both, we obtain the Pareto front and optimal strategies in closed form.

</details>


### [4] [Two-Dimensional Phase Transitions in Classical Systems: 60 Years after the Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24091)
*Ruijian Zhu,Yanting Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该综述系统梳理了二维系统熔化问题的研究进展，包括被动系统中BKT理论（BKT theory）的应用与最新理论计算成果，以及非平衡活性物质（active matter）体系中偏离Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner定理的涌现现象，最后展望了预测二维熔化场景和理解非平衡性质的若干方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维熔化机制尚未被完全理解，而近年来主动物质领域的新现象进一步偏离了经典理论框架，亟需系统综述以梳理进展并指明未来方向。

Method: 采用综述（review）形式，首先聚焦被动系统中关于二维熔化问题的理论与计算最新进展，继而总结非平衡体系中的启发性结果。

Result: 综述指出，被动系统中BKT理论作为二维熔化的重要应用，其机制仍未完全阐明；非平衡活性物质体系则展现了偏离Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner定理的新奇现象。

Conclusion: 文章对预测二维熔化场景和理解二维活性物质体系的非平衡本质提出了若干有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: In 1966, Hohenberg, Mermin and Wagner proved that long-wavelength fluctuations destabilize the long-range order of continuous symmetry in two-dimensional (2D) systems. Later in the 1970s, Berezinskii, Kosterlitz and Thouless developed the BKT theory describing an unconventional phase transition between quasi-long-range and short-range order in 2D systems driven by the binding-unbinding of topological defects, which has become a fundamental topic in statistical mechanics, condensed matter physics, and soft matter physics. One of the most important applications of the BKT theory is the melting of 2D crystals, whose mechanisms are not yet fully understood. Recently, this topic has been extended to the area of active matter, where the non-equilibrium nature leads to novel phenomena that deviate from the Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner theorem. In this review, we first focus on the recent theoretical and computational progress in the 2D melting problem in passive systems, and then summarize the inspiring results obtained from non-equilibrium systems. The review closes with comments on several promising directions for predicting 2D melting scenarios and for understanding the non-equilibrium nature in 2D active matter systems.

</details>


### [5] [Evaluating the solution performance of the augmented Lagrangian function on Ising machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24241)
*Shunsuke Awai,Takuro Itoh,Keita Takahashi,Kotaro Tanahashi,Shu Tanaka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出将增广拉格朗日函数（augmented Lagrangian function, ALF）作为伊辛机（Ising machines）的一种求解公式化方法，并通过时间-ε（time-to-epsilon, TTε）指标评估其性能。以二次背包问题（quadratic knapsack problem）为基准，实验表明ALF相比惩罚函数法（penalty function formulation）可将TTε降低约一个数量级，并在保持μ较小的情况下获得可行解和高精度解，证明ALF是一种提升伊辛机求解性能的有效方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伊辛机（Ising machines）在求解组合优化问题时，如何选择合适的公式化方法（formulation）以提升求解效率和精度是关键问题。惩罚函数法（penalty function formulation）虽被广泛使用，但存在数值不稳定性和收敛性不足的局限，亟需更优的替代方案。

Method: 采用增广拉格朗日函数（augmented Lagrangian function, ALF）作为伊辛机的公式化方法，以二次背包问题（quadratic knapsack problem）为基准测试，通过时间-ε（time-to-epsilon, TTε）指标评估性能，并分析超参数μ和λ对TTε的影响。

Result: 相比惩罚函数法（penalty function formulation），增广拉格朗日函数公式化方法可将TTε降低约一个数量级（roughly an order of magnitude），同时能在保持μ较小的情况下获得可行解，并在代表性参数设置下更早达到高精度解。

Conclusion: 增广拉格朗日函数（augmented Lagrangian function）是一种有前景的伊辛机公式化方法，能够有效提升求解性能，在数值稳定性、收敛性和求解精度方面优于传统惩罚函数法。

Abstract: We apply the augmented Lagrangian function (ALF) as a formulation for Ising machines and evaluate its performance by time-to-epsilon (\mathrm{TT\varepsilon}). The ALF has been well studied in continuous optimization for its numerical stability and convergence, and its advantage over the penalty function formulation is demonstrated here through the following results. Using the quadratic knapsack problem as a benchmark, we examine the dependence of \mathrm{TT\varepsilon} on the hyperparameters μand λ. The augmented Lagrangian formulation reduces \mathrm{TT\varepsilon} by roughly an order of magnitude compared with the penalty function formulation, keeping μsmall while obtaining feasible solutions and, for representative parameter settings, reaching high-precision solutions earlier in the search. These findings indicate that the augmented Lagrangian function is a promising formulation for improving the solution performance of Ising machines.

</details>


### [6] [Universal Extraction of Quantum Critical Exponents and Phase Transitions via Tailored Hilbert Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24312)
*Ye Xiong*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的希尔伯特空间裁剪方案，用于探测量子临界现象。在仅含50个元胞的晶格上精确重构了1D XY模型的二阶量子相变（QPT）临界点与临界指数；在仅12个格点的1D XXZ链中恢复了Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变的临界参数。该方法为多体晶格系统中量子相变的普适表征提供了一条高效替代路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）与重整化群（renormalization group）是分析量子相变（quantum phase transitions, QPTs）的核心工具。现有方法通常需要较大系统尺寸才能准确提取临界参数；本文旨在开发一种更高效的希尔伯特空间裁剪方案，以在极小晶格上实现量子临界现象的精确探测。

Method: 提出一种新型希尔伯特空间裁剪方案（Hilbert-space tailoring scheme），在保证关键物理信息的前提下对系统希尔伯特空间进行有效裁剪，从而在极小系统尺寸下仍能准确提取临界行为。

Result: 将该方法应用于一维（1D）XY模型的二阶量子相变，在仅含50个元胞的晶格上得到精确的临界点和临界指数；进一步应用于一维XXZ链的Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变，在仅12个格点的小系统上恢复了临界参数。

Conclusion: 该裁剪方案可能开辟一条替代性的高效路径，用于在多种多体晶格系统中普适地表征量子相变（QPT）。

Abstract: Finite-size scaling and the renormalization group form the central toolkit
  for analyzing quantum phase transitions (QPTs). In this Letter, we introduce
  a novel Hilbert-space tailoring scheme to probe quantum critical phenomena.
  Applied to the second-order QPT of the one-dimensional (1D) XY model, our method
  yields precise critical points and exponents on lattices containing merely 50
  unit cells. We further establish the universal applicability of this
  framework via investigations of the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless
  transition in the 1D XXZ chain: critical parameters are recovered
  with as few as 12 lattice sites. This technique may open an alternative,
  efficient route to universally characterize QPT across many-body lattice systems.

</details>


### [7] [Out-of-equilibrium scaling of the particle density in quantum fermionic wires after a critical quenching of the chemical potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24395)
*H. Panagopoulos,E. Vicari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子费米子Kitaev链在瞬时量子淬火（quantum quench）后的非平衡标度行为，发现淬火后粒子密度与临界值之差满足动态标度函数，并在小标度变量极限下表现出奇异性，为先前关于非平衡动态标度的猜想提供了解析证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基态粒子密度在Ising型量子相变处的临界标度被正则项和对数项所掩盖，呈现次主导行为；本文旨在探究化学势瞬时量子淬火后的非平衡动力学中，粒子密度是否展现出与平衡态不同的、可解析描述的标度行为。

Method: 采用解析分析方法，研究一维量子费米子Kitaev线（Kitaev wires）在化学势瞬时量子淬火后的非平衡动力学；淬火从临界区域内的基态出发，将化学势瞬间淬火到临界点，分析淬火后粒子密度随动态标度变量θ∼t/ξ^z（t为淬火后时间，ξ为初始态长度标度，z为动态临界指数）的演化行为。

Result: 淬火后粒子密度与临界值之差在θ→0极限下表现出奇异的标度行为，该奇异性与淬火起点处粒子密度异常的平衡标度行为相关；该动态标度行为为先前基于数值有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analyses）提出的猜想提供了解析证据。

Conclusion: 非平衡动态标度（out-of-equilibrium dynamic scaling）在淬火后的粒子密度中普遍存在，与受非普适贡献主导的平衡标度行为形成对比；该解析结果支持了关于减除粒子密度（subtracted particle density）在量子淬火后会出现动态标度行为的早期猜想。

Abstract: We study the out-of-equilibrium scaling behavior of the particle density in quantum fermionic Kitaev wires, after instantaneous quantum quenches (QQs) of the chemical potential within their quantum critical region. The critical scaling of the ground-state particle density is known to be subleading at its Ising-like quantum transition, hidden by regular and logarithmic terms arising from peculiar mixings with the identity operator. This situation changes along the out-of-equilibrium dynamics arising from QQs of the chemical potential to the critical point, starting from the ground state for Hamiltonian parameters within the critical region. We analytically show that the difference between the post-QQ particle density and its critical value develops an out-of-equilibrium scaling behavior, in terms of the dynamic scaling variable $θ\sim t/ξ^z$ (where $t>0$ is the post-QQ time, $ξ$ is the length scale of the initial state, and $z$ is the dynamic critical exponent) associated with the post-QQ time evolution. The scaling function turns out to have a peculiar singular behavior in the $θ\to 0$ limit, apparently related to the anomalous equilibrium scaling behavior of the particle density at the starting point of the QQ protocol. This provides analytical evidence of earlier conjectures on the general emergence of post-QQ dynamic scaling behaviors of the subtracted particle density (supported by numerical finite-size scaling analyses), unlike their equilibrium counterpart which turns out to be dominated by nonuniversal contributions.

</details>


### [8] [The impact of population heterogeneity on the redundancy principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24411)
*Sergei Fedotov,Daniel Fears,Daniel Han*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了生物信号传导中，群体异质性（population heterogeneity）会显著改变极值首次通过时间（extreme first passage time）的统计特性，使得异质性群体的模态和最小首次通过时间比同质群体小一个数量级，表明异质性是可被生物利用的参数而非噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物的快速信号响应常依赖极值统计——由一群搜索者中的最快几个来完成。虽然极端首次通过时间（extreme first passage time, FPT）理论在同质系综（homogeneous ensembles）中已很成熟，但其对群体异质性（population heterogeneity）的敏感性尚未明确。

Method: 通过理论分析，对异质无记忆随机游走者（memoryless random walkers）群体进行系综平均，推导出异质性导致的系综自强化（ensemble self-reinforcement）效应，并精确计算了异质与同质群体在FPT和最小FPT密度上的差异。

Result: 异质性群体的模态首次通过时间和最小首次通过时间均比具有相同平均速率（mean rates）的同质群体小一个数量级。

Conclusion: 精确的解析预测表明，群体异质性是一个生物学可以利用的参数，而不仅仅是需要被平均掉的噪声。

Abstract: Biological signaling is often governed by extreme value statistics, where a rapid response relies on the fastest few out of a large redundant group of searchers. While extreme first passage time (FPT) theory is well established for homogeneous ensembles, its sensitivity to population heterogeneity remains open. We show that averaging over a heterogeneous population of memoryless random walkers gives rise to ensemble self-reinforcement. This heterogeneity drastically changes both the FPT and minimum FPT densities relative to a homogeneous ensemble with identical mean rates. The modal and minimum FPTs are an order of magnitude smaller for heterogeneous populations relative to homogeneous ones. Our exact analytical predictions establish that population heterogeneity is a parameter that biology can exploit and not merely noise to be averaged away.

</details>


### [9] [From Continuous-Time Random Walks to Laplace Tails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24451)
*Omer Hamdi,Stanislav Burov,Eli Barkai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在连续时间随机行走（CTRW）框架下，系统研究了拉普拉斯尾巴（Laplace tails）的产生机制，通过分析有限时间内的更新次数概率 $Q_t(n)$，建立了速率函数（rate function）类框架，证明指数尾巴源于 $Q_t(n)$ 的指数行为，并与数值模拟和大偏差速率函数（large deviation rate functions）结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布朗运动（Brownian motion）中位移分布通常服从正态分布，符合中心极限定理（central limit theorem），但在玻璃、活细胞和胶体悬浮液等复杂介质中的单粒子追踪实验中，观测到位移分布呈现显著的指数衰减（即拉普拉斯尾巴）。此前仅有简要通讯报道过该现象在连续时间随机行走（CTRW）框架中的出现，缺乏详细的互补性研究。

Method: 通过探索 $Q_t(n)$（时间 $t$ 内恰好发生 $n$ 次更新（renewal）的概率）的行为，发展了一个适用于有限时间 $t$ 的类速率函数（rate function-like）分析框架，将 $Q_t(n)$ 的指数尾巴与位置概率密度函数 $P(x,t)$ 的指数尾巴联系起来。

Result: 证明 $Q_t(n)$ 呈现指数尾巴（exponential tails），并由此导致位置概率密度函数 $P(x,t)$ 也呈现指数尾巴。结果与有限时间数值模拟（finite-time numerical simulations）以及渐近大偏差速率函数（asymptotic large deviation rate functions）的对比验证良好，表明结果在广泛的时间范围内成立。

Conclusion: 本文在CTRW框架下为拉普拉斯尾巴的出现提供了完整且详细的理论解释，所建立的有限时间速率函数框架在广泛时间范围内与数值模拟和大偏差理论结果一致，加深了对复杂介质中反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）机理的理解。

Abstract: During Brownian motion, the displacement is normally distributed, a classical fact aligned with the central limit theorem. However, single particle tracking in complex media such as glasses, living cells, and colloidal suspensions often reveals pronounced exponential decay of the displacement distribution, known as Laplace tails. In a short letter, two of us presented the emergence of Laplace tails in the continuous time random walk (CTRW) framework. Here, a detailed complementary study is presented. By exploring the behavior of $Q_t(n)$, the probability that exactly $n$ renewals occur during time $t$, we develop a rate function-like framework for this quantity, valid for finite $t$. We show that $Q_t(n)$ exhibits exponential tails, which in turn give rise to exponential tails of the positional probability density function $P(x,t)$. Favorable comparison to finite-time numerical simulations and asymptotic large deviation rate functions establishes the validity of our results over a wide temporal range.

</details>


### [10] [Anomalous Floquet Heating from Sparse Long-Range Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24541)
*Chenyue Guo,Andrea Pizzi,Hongzheng Zhao*

TL;DR: 本文发现，在周期性驱动下，具有稀疏无限程相互作用的量子多体系统会出现反常加热行为，其加热率γ ∼ exp(-O(√ω))，比常规指数压制(exp(-O(ω)))更慢，根源在于网络配位数(coordination number)的宽分布导致加热由高配位位点主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常规周期驱动晶格系统中加热率随驱动频率ω指数压制(γ ∼ exp(-O(ω)))，但稀疏无限程相互作用——这一在量子模拟器中新近可实现的相互作用形式——是否会导致不同的加热行为尚不清楚，需要理论探索。

Method: 通过解析理论分析小世界网络(small-world networks)中的加热行为，并结合大规模数值模拟进行验证；通过分析配位数的宽分布来解释反常加热的起源。

Result: 发现反常加热率γ ∼ exp(-O(√ω))，比常规指数压制更慢；加热由高配位位点主导，使局域能量尺度随频率增长；解析理论与大规模数值结果高度吻合；揭示了网络拓扑可作为调控非平衡物质相的控制手段。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了Floquet加热的新机制，并为在具有可编程相互作用网络的驱动系统中稳定非平衡相(nonequilibrium phases)提供了新路径。

Abstract: Regular lattices of interacting particles under a periodic drive typically heat with rate $γ\sim e^{-\mathcal{O}(ω)}$ which is exponentially suppressed in drive frequency $ω$. Here, we show that sparse infinite-range interactions, which have recently become accessible in quantum simulators, can lead to anomalous heating with rate $γ\sim e^{-\mathcal{O}(\sqrtω)}$. This anomaly originates from the broad distribution of coordination numbers across the network: as the driving frequency increases, heating becomes dominated by sites with larger coordination numbers, making the characteristic local energy scale relevant for heating grow with frequency. For small-world networks, we develop an analytic theory that thoroughly matches our large scale numerics. Finally, we discuss how network topology can serve as a control knob for engineering non-equilibrium phases of matter. Our results uncover a new mechanism for Floquet heating and suggest new routes toward stabilizing nonequilibrium phases in driven systems with programmable interaction networks.

### [11] [Exact log-odds representation and mean-field criticality of a growing social group model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24818)
*Xingfu Ke,Fanyuan Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对一个无哈密顿量的社会群体增长模型进行了精确解析重整，将其表述为对数时间上的梯度流，归结为一个自洽方程 arctanh(φ*) = m·arctanh(αφ*)，揭示了该动力学等价于一个平均场自洽推断过程，并建立了包含Landau-like有效势、临界性分析和RG-like标度流的三层框架，系统比较了与平均场Ising模型的异同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社会群体增长是一个无哈密顿量（Hamiltonian-free）的非平衡过程，现有工具难以对其固定点结构和临界行为进行精确解析刻画。本文旨在为该类增长驱动集体行为提供一个可解析求解的最小模型，并考察平衡临界工具箱中的哪些元素——经适当重新解释后——能在无哈密顿量的体系中存活。

Method: 将群体增长模型重新表述为对数时间（logarithmic time）上的梯度流（gradient flow），推导出极化（polarization）φ的自洽方程 arctanh(φ*) = m·arctanh(αφ*)，其中α为评估可靠性（evaluation reliability），m为评估者数量。构建三层分析框架：核心理论层（Landau-like有效势、与平均场Ising模型的比较及无平衡对应特征）、数学基础层（相关判据下的临界性、Pólya-urn鞅收敛、以群体大小为尺度的RG-like流），以及不可逆性与信息几何的互补视角。使用冻结N下的Freidlin–Wentzell拟势给出亚稳态的Kramers逃逸估计，并进行蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟验证。

Result: 自洽方程具有直接的log-odds解释：每个判决贡献对数似然比（log-likelihood ratio）2arctanh(αφ)；一致同意累积m个独立证据。动力学构成精确的平均场自洽推断理论，当集体增益mα克服增长稀释时发生有序化。与平均场Ising模型共享临界指数（critical exponents），但具有增长模型独有的嵌套arctanh结构。蒙特卡洛模拟在对数时间上塌缩为一条无参数确定主曲线。

Conclusion: 本文提供了增长驱动集体行为最小模型的详细解析刻画，揭示了在无哈密顿量条件下，平衡临界工具箱中的哪些元素——经适当重新解释——依然可以保留，而哪些特征（如嵌套arctanh结构）则是增长过程所独有的。

Abstract: We present an exact analytical reformulation of a growing social group model -- a Hamiltonian-free nonequilibrium process in which a group grows by noisy, consensus-driven admission. Cast as a gradient flow on logarithmic time, the fixed-point structure collapses to a single self-consistent equation: $\arctanh(φ^*) = m \cdot \arctanh(αφ^*)$, where $φ$ is the polarization, $α=1-2η$ the evaluation reliability, and $m$ the number of evaluators. The equation has a direct log-odds interpretation: each verdict contributes log-likelihood ratio $2\arctanh(αφ)$; unanimity accumulates $m$ independent evidence pieces. The dynamics thus constitutes an exact mean-field theory of self-consistent inference, ordering when the collective gain $mα$ overcomes the dilution of growth. We develop a systematic three-layer framework: core theory (Landau-like effective potential, comparison with the mean-field Ising model, and features without equilibrium counterpart), mathematical foundations (criticality from correlated verdicts, Pólya-urn martingale convergence, and an RG-like flow with group size as scale), and complementary perspectives on irreversibility and information geometry. A frozen-$N$ Freidlin--Wentzell quasipotential yields Kramers-type escape estimates for metastable states, while Monte Carlo simulations collapse onto a parameter-free deterministic master curve on logarithmic time. Systematic comparison with the mean-field Ising model reveals shared critical exponents but a nested arctanh structure unique to growth. These results provide a detailed analytical characterization of a minimal model of growth-driven collective behavior and map which elements of the equilibrium critical toolbox -- suitably reinterpreted -- survive without a Hamiltonian.

</details>


### [12] [First-Order Recoverability Collapse in Self-Referential Information Decoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24861)
*Pieter van Rooyen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从热力学统计力学（statistical mechanics）视角研究了非平衡驱动下自适应系统（adaptive systems）中推理与不可逆动作的耦合，提出了有限容量解码器（finite-capacity decoders）模型，证明了在持续过载下可恢复性丧失和稳定性诊断发散是容量饱和的结构性后果，并揭示了从连续相变到一级相变的转变、滞后恢复行为以及级联（cascade）大小的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡驱动下自适应系统中推理与不可逆动作之间的耦合机制，特别是当信息处理作为热力学负载（thermodynamic load）时，系统如何在持续过载条件下失去可恢复性，以及这种失效的结构性起源是什么。

Method: 将自适应系统建模为有限容量解码器（finite-capacity decoders），其不可逆承诺消除反事实选项；通过可行性裕度（feasibility margin）和稳定性诊断（stability diagnostic）刻画可恢复操作；引入显式反馈机制，使每个未经认证的承诺平均产生alpha个新候选，分析相变行为；采用级联统计分析与事件驱动模拟（event-driven simulations）验证理论预测。

Result: 持续过载下可恢复性丧失和稳定性诊断发散是容量饱和的结构性后果，与优化目标、控制策略或基底无关；单纯增加容量无法恢复可恢复性，且更高通量加速不可恢复损失；显式反馈将连续转变变为一级相变，明澈态（lucid state）与崩溃态（collapsed state）共存于尖点组织（cusp-organized）双稳区；级联大小由输入中有根分数（grounded fraction）限定，远离开边界时恢复均场指数tau=3/2，每个级联携带兰道尔定价（Landauer-priced）的合成熵爆发。

Conclusion: 可恢复耗散（recoverable dissipation）是高通量通量（high-flux regimes）下解码器稳定性的必要条件；本分析基于约束且与基底无关，为分布式系统中常见的亚稳态失效（metastable failures）提供了统计力学基础；高通量人工智能（high-throughput AI）是具体应用实例。

Abstract: We study adaptive systems coupling inference to irreversible action under sustained nonequilibrium driving. Treating information processing as a thermodynamic load, we model them as finite-capacity decoders whose irreversible commitments eliminate counterfactual options, and characterize recoverable operation by a feasibility margin and a stability diagnostic fixing when irreversible action is admissible. Under sustained overload -- induced flux exceeding effective integrative capacity -- loss of recoverability and divergence of the diagnostic arise as structural consequences of capacity saturation, independent of optimization objective, control policy, or substrate. Added capacity alone does not restore recoverability: absent certification or gating, higher throughput accelerates non-recoverable loss, with high-throughput AI a concrete application. Making the feedback explicit -- each uncertified commitment spawning on average alpha new candidates -- turns the continuous transition first-order: lucid and collapsed states coexist in a cusp-organized bistable region with closed-form spinodals, collapse pre-empts the continuous divergence at finite stability ratio, recovery is hysteretic, and for alpha >= 1 load reduction alone cannot restore operation. Cascade sizes are bounded by the grounded fraction of input: a genealogy-times-congestion factorization sets a cutoff that grows as grounding shrinks, with the mean-field exponent tau = 3/2 recovered away from the boundary and each cascade carrying a Landauer-priced burst of synthetic entropy; event-driven simulations confirm the cutoff law and phase structure. This supplies the statistical mechanics of the metastable failures seen in distributed systems. The analysis is constraint-based and substrate-agnostic, establishing recoverable dissipation as a necessary criterion for decoder stability in high-flux regimes.

</details>

### [13] [Connecting Quantum Tomography and Quantum Retrodiction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23777)
*Sebastian Murk,Ian Tan,Fabian Müller,Dominik Šafránek*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明量子断层扫描（quantum tomography）与量子回溯推断（quantum retrodiction）遵循相同原理：与测量通道（measurement channel）关联的Petz恢复映射（Petz recovery map）等价于最大似然断层扫描中使用的对数似然梯度更新，重复应用该映射可单调递增似然；进一步将Petz映射非对易推广至任意量子通道（quantum channel），建立回溯推断、恢复映射与统计推断之间的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上量子断层扫描与量子回溯推断被视为两种独立的推断任务，前者从测量数据重建量子态，后者从观测结果反推过去量子态，二者之间缺乏统一的数学联系。

Method: 通过对测量通道的梯度分析，证明Petz恢复映射等价于最大似然断层扫描中的对数似然梯度更新；在此基础上，从任意量子通道的广义似然梯度出发，推导出Petz映射的非对易（noncommutative）推广形式。

Result: 重复应用Petz映射可单调递增似然函数；所提出的迭代过程能够最大化似然，为量子断层扫描提供了一个通用框架。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了量子回溯推断、恢复映射与统计推断之间的直接桥梁，揭示了量子断层扫描与量子回溯推断本质上是同一底层原理的两种体现。

Abstract: Quantum tomography and quantum retrodiction are traditionally viewed as separate inference tasks: tomography reconstructs quantum states from measurement data, whereas retrodiction infers past quantum states from observed outcomes. We show that the two are manifestations of the same underlying principle. We prove that the Petz recovery map associated with a measurement channel is precisely the gradient update of the log-likelihood used in maximum-likelihood tomography. Consequently, repeated applications of the Petz map monotonically increase the likelihood. Extending beyond measurement channels, we derive a noncommutative generalization of the Petz map from the gradient of a generalized likelihood for arbitrary quantum channels. The resulting iterative procedure maximizes the likelihood and provides a general framework for quantum tomography, establishing a direct bridge between retrodiction, recovery maps, and statistical inference.

### [14] [Wavelet Matrix Product States for Quantum Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23823)
*Molly Kaplan,Antoine Tilloy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种变分方法（variational method），利用基于Daubechies小波（Daubechies wavelets）的矩阵乘积态（wMPS）来求解连续量子模型，能够在任意精细尺度上迭代逼近，并在Lieb-Liniger模型上验证了其计算能量密度和关联函数的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续量子模型（continuum quantum models）的数值求解在传统框架下通常受限于离散格点近似或自由理论（free theories），缺乏一种能够灵活处理连续场论（field theory）且可系统提高精度的张量网络方法。

Method: 采用基于正则性充分高（$N\geq 6$）的Daubechies尺度函数构建小波矩阵乘积态（wavelet matrix product states, wMPS），该状态直接定义在连续场论Fock空间（Fock space）中，具有有限能量密度，并可通过标准算法优化，不局限于自由理论。利用小波内置的多分辨率分析（multi-resolution analysis）及其量子电路描述，可迭代细化wMPS以获得任意精细长度尺度下的准确近似。

Result: 在Lieb-Liniger模型上，该方法成功计算了能量密度（energy density）和关联函数（correlation functions），展示了其数值效率。

Conclusion: wMPS方法为连续量子多体系统（continuous quantum many-body systems）提供了一种兼具张量网络可优化性与小波多尺度精化能力的通用变分框架。

Abstract: We introduce a variational method to solve continuum quantum models with discrete tensor network techniques. The method leverages wavelet matrix product states (wMPS): matrix product states built on top of sufficiently regular ($N\geq 6$) Daubechies scaling functions. These states live in the continuum field theory Fock space, have finite energy density, and can be optimized with standard algorithms, without restriction to free theories. Further, exploiting the multi-resolution analysis built into wavelets, and its quantum circuit description, we can iteratively refine wMPS to obtain accurate approximations at arbitrarily fine length-scales. We showcase the efficiency of the method on the Lieb-Liniger model, computing energy density and correlation functions.

### [15] [The Vector and Canonical Components of the Momentum Operator in 3D Euclidean Space Spanned by General Curvilinear Coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24572)
*M. S. Shikakhwa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种统一且自然的方法，在三维欧氏空间的广义曲线坐标（GCC）中构造动量算符的厄米矢量分量和正则分量。该方法将动量算符识别为质量乘以速度算符，通过海森堡运动方程（Heisenberg equation of motion）计算速度算符，得到梯度算符加上一个零值和，将其分配到梯度各分量后得到GCC中的厄米矢量分量；再对每个矢量分量在相应的基矢量上进行对称化处理，即得到正则分量。文中首先以极坐标（polar coordinates）为例展示形式体系，再推广至一般GCC情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义曲线坐标中，动量算符的厄米矢量分量和正则分量的构造长期以来缺乏统一、简单且自然的方法，现有推导往往依赖于特定坐标系的非对称操作。

Method: 采用基于动量算符定义为质量乘以速度算符的物理识别方法；利用海森堡运动方程计算速度算符，得到梯度算符加一个零值和；将该零值和分配到梯度各分量以构造厄米矢量分量；通过对每个厄米矢量分量在相应基矢量上进行对称化处理，得到正则分量。先以极坐标为例进行形式体系展示，再推广至一般GCC。

Result: 成功在广义曲线坐标中构造了动量算符的厄米矢量分量和正则分量，并证明了一种简单、统一且自然的推导路径。

Conclusion: 该统一方法使更广泛的受众（包括初学者）能够理解和应用广义曲线坐标下的动量算符构造，降低了传统推导的复杂性和形式化门槛。

Abstract: We construct the Hermitian vector and canonical components of the momentum operator in 3D Euclidean space spanned by general curvilinear coordinates (GCC's) using a simple, natural and unified approach based on identifying the momentum operator in any coordinate system as mass times the velocity operator. When this latter is calculated by applying the Heisenberg equation of motion, it returns ($-i\hbar$ times) the gradient operator plus an additional zero-valued sum, which when distributed among the components of the gradient, it makes each the Hermitian vector component of the momentum operator in GCC's. The canonical components follow immediately upon symmetrizing each of these vector components in the corresponding base vector. For accessability by wider audiences, we first develop the formalism for the simple polar coordinates and then we develop the case for GCC's.

### [16] [Infinite-Level Hierarchy of Solvable Quantum Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23803)
*Michael A. Rampp,Suhail A. Rather,Pieter W. Claeys*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套无限层次的严格可解性条件（solvability conditions），以弥补广义对偶幺正层级（generalized dual-unitary hierarchy）在超出第二层后在全体时空（whole spacetime）中不再可解的缺陷。该新层级可与广义对偶幺正层级结合，使得关联函数和纠缠动力学在全体时空中精确可解，并证明每一层都存在非平凡解，从而系统地将对偶幺正性（dual unitarity）推广至更一般的严格可解非可积系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对偶幺正电路（dual-unitary circuits）已成为严格可解但非可积量子动力学（non-integrable quantum dynamics）的范式。近期提出的广义对偶幺正层级（generalized dual-unitary hierarchy）试图扩展严格可解电路的现像范围，但在第二层之后，该层级在全体时空中不再可解，因此亟需一套新的可解性条件来恢复并维持全域的可解性。

Method: 提出一套无限层次的严格可解性条件（solvability conditions），将其与广义对偶幺正层级（generalized dual-unitary hierarchy）相结合，从而在全体时空中实现关联函数（correlation functions）和纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics）的精确解析。

Result: 该新层级在每一层都拥有非平凡解（non-trivial solutions），证明了可以在保持可解性的前提下系统性地扩展对偶幺正性（dual unitarity）。

Conclusion: 该工作表明对偶幺正性能够被系统地扩展同时保留严格可解性，为研究具有更一般性质的严格可解非可积系统（exactly solvable non-integrable systems）开辟了新的方向。

Abstract: Dual-unitary circuits have emerged as a paradigm of exactly solvable yet non-integrable quantum dynamics. Recently, a generalization of dual unitarity attempting to extend the phenomenology of exactly solvable circuits has been introduced through a hierarchy of conditions, with dual unitarity as the first level. However, beyond the second level the proposed generalized dual-unitary hierarchy ceases to be solvable in the whole spacetime. We present an infinite hierarchy of solvability conditions remedying this problem. These new conditions can be combined with the generalized dual-unitary hierarchy to obtain circuits for which correlation functions and entanglement dynamics can be analyzed exactly in the whole spacetime. We show that this novel hierarchy possesses non-trivial solutions at every level. Our results demonstrate that dual unitarity can be systematically extended while preserving solvability, opening up investigations of exactly solvable non-integrable systems with more general properties.

### [17] [Augmenting Imaginary-Time Evolution with Local Geometric Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23934)
*Carlos L. Benavides-Riveros,Prachi Sharma,Fedor Šimkovic*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种增强型虚时演化（augmented imaginary-time evolution, AITE）框架，通过利用瞬时能量分布的高阶统计结构识别局部最优方向，替代标准虚时演化的梯度流。AITE在整个演化过程中严格优于标准ITE，展现出超线性收敛和有限虚时内误差精确消失的灭绝（extinction）两个定性不同的阶段，而标准ITE仅表现为渐近指数衰减。标准ITE在AITE的零偏度（zero-skewness）极限下被恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准虚时演化（imaginary-time evolution, ITE）在基态制备中收敛速度仅呈渐近指数衰减，受限于瞬时态的能量方差（energy variance），无法在有限时间内精确到达基态。本文旨在克服这一根本性局限，设计一种加速收敛的新框架。

Method: 提出增强型虚时演化（AITE）框架，摒弃标准能量景观（energy landscape）上的梯度流，转而沿由瞬时能量分布的高阶统计结构（higher-order statistical structure）确定的局部最优方向（locally optimal directions）进行几何信息引导的下降（geometrically informed descent）。

Result: AITE在整个演化过程中严格优于标准ITE，展现出两种不同收敛阶段：超线性收敛（superlinear convergence）阶段和灭绝（extinction）阶段——后者在有限虚时（finite imaginary time）内能量误差精确消失。标准ITE仅在零偏度（zero-skewness）极限下作为AITE的特例被恢复。

Conclusion: AITE框架以统一的加速形式涵盖并扩展了更广泛的ITE算法家族，为量子模拟和量子多体物理中的基态制备提供了性能严格更优的理论基础。

Abstract: Imaginary-time evolution (ITE) underpins a broad family of algorithms for ground-state preparation in quantum simulation and quantum many-body physics. In these methods, convergence is governed by the energy variance of the instantaneous state, causing the flow to approach the ground state only asymptotically. We introduce an augmented imaginary-time evolution (AITE) framework that replaces the standard gradient flow on the energy landscape with a geometrically informed descent along locally optimal directions, which are identified by exploiting the higher-order statistical structure of the instantaneous energy distribution. The resulting flow strictly outperforms standard ITE throughout the entire evolution and exhibits two qualitatively distinct regimes: a superlinear convergence regime, followed by an extinction regime in which the energy error vanishes exactly at a finite imaginary time, in sharp contrast to the asymptotic exponential decay of ITE. Standard ITE is recovered in the zero-skewness limit of AITE, implying that the acceleration extends naturally across the broader ITE algorithmic family.

</details>


### [18] [Initial-state-dependent dephasing effect in non-Hermitian Su-Schrieffer-Heeger models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24185)
*Tao Min,Junjie Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究纯退相干（pure dephasing）对有限大小非厄米SSH晶格模型中迹距离（trace distance）动力学演化的影响，发现退相干效应在很大程度上不依赖于非厄米对称性（symmetry-independent），而是依赖于初态（initial-state dependent）。通过改变初始态，增强退相干强度可以加速迹距离衰减或使其稳定，并揭示了强退相干极限下的两种稳定化机制：部分稳定化和完全稳定化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外部额外耗散（external dissipation）下非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）的动力学演化至关重要，但退相干（dephasing）这一主要的现实耗散机制对非厄米系统的影响尚缺乏探索。

Method: 聚焦于实空间中具有交替增益和损耗的有限大小非厄米Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）晶格模型，通过调节系统参数使模型支持具有宇称-时间对称性（parity-time symmetry）或反宇称-时间对称性（anti-parity-time symmetry）的相，并计算纯退相干下迹距离的动力学演化。

Result: 迹距离在不同非厄米相中表现出不同的动力学行为，但对退相干的响应不依赖于对称性而是依赖于初态。增大退相干强度可加速迹距离衰减或使其稳定。在强退相干极限下观察到两种稳定化：部分稳定化（trace distance趋近于小于初值的有限值）和完全稳定化（trace distance在演化中始终等于初值）。在反宇称-时间对称性未破缺相中，退相干强度增大会连续抑制原本无退相干时迹距离的指数衰减。

Conclusion: 初态依赖的退相干效应归因于系统中交替的增益和损耗，且在厄米对应系统中不存在该效应。该发现揭示了退相干在非厄米系统中具有不同于传统认知的、依赖初态的稳定化作用。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamical evolution of non-Hermitian systems under extra external dissipation is essential. Dephasing, a major realistic dissipation, is conventionally considered detrimental to information processing. However, its impact on non-Hermitian systems remains largely unexplored. Here, we focus on finite-sized non-Hermitian Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) lattice models with alternating gain and loss in real space and examine the dynamical evolution of the trace distance under pure dephasing. By tuning system parameters, this model supports phases with either parity-time or anti-parity-time symmetries, enabling us to explore the interplay between dephasing and different non-Hermitian symmetries. While the trace distance exhibits distinct dynamical behaviors across the different phases in the absence of dephasing, its response to dephasing is largely symmetry-independent but instead initial-state dependent. By varying initial states, we observe that increasing the dephasing strength can either merely accelerate the decay of the trace distance or stabilize it. Interestingly, we reveal two kinds of dephasing-induced stabilization that differ in the strong dephasing limit: a partial stabilization, where the trace distance approaches a finite value smaller than its initial value in the long-time limit, and a complete stabilization, where the trace distance remains at its initial value throughout the entire evolution. By analyzing the equation of motion, we attribute the initial-state dependent dephasing effect to the alternating gain and loss in the system and confirm its absence in Hermitian counterparts. Furthermore, in the anti-parity-time symmetry unbroken phase, we identify a continuous suppression-upon increasing the dephasing strength-of the otherwise exponential decay of the trace distance seen in the absence of dephasing.

### [19] [Quantum-enabled active matter at the atomic scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24615)
*Sabrina Burgardt,Julian Feß,Alexander Guthmann,Silvia Hiebel,Aritra K. Mukhopadhyay,Sangyun Lee,Michael te Vrugt,Benno Liebchen,Hartmut Löwen,Raphael Wittkowski,Artur Widera*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该实验首次在单个铯-133原子尺度实现活性物质，通过量子自旋交换从超冷铷-87原子浴中提取能量并转化为运动，建立了无参数活性朗之万模型，开启了活性、量子物理与非平衡热力学交叉研究的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性物质（active matter）研究已从微米尺度推进至纳米尺度，但在单个原子这一量子效应显著的基本尺度上实现活性仍是一个开放挑战。本文旨在实验演示并解释单个原子层面的量子活性机制。

Method: 将单个Cs-133原子束缚于光学偶极阱（optical dipole trap）中，通过与超冷Rb-87原子浴的量子力学自旋相互作用（quantum-mechanical spin interactions）提取能量并转化为活性运动。采用基于动理论（kinetic theory）的无参数活性朗之万模型（parameter-free active Langevin model）定量重现动力学过程，并用事件驱动蒙特卡罗碰撞模拟（event-driven Monte Carlo collision simulations）加以验证。

Result: 实验观察到单个Cs-133原子从Rb-87原子浴中提取能量并产生活性运动。量子自旋交换（quantum spin exchange）被确认为活性的微观起源，它将离散的内部自旋能量转移为动能。无参数活性朗之万模型与模拟结果均与实验定量吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了在单个原子这一尺寸极限下实现活性物质的量子路径，为探索活性、量子物理（quantum physics）与介观非平衡热力学（mesoscopic non-equilibrium thermodynamics）之间的相互作用开辟了新前景。

Abstract: Active matter comprises particles that extract energy from their local environment and convert it into motion. Although active particles have been miniaturized down to the nanoscale, realizing activity at the fundamentally smaller scale of individual atoms remains an open challenge, where quantum effects become increasingly relevant. Here, we experimentally demonstrate that individual Cs-133 atoms confined in an optical dipole trap extract energy from an ultracold bath of Rb-87 atoms via quantum-mechanical spin interactions and convert it into active motion. We quantitatively reproduce the resulting dynamics using a parameter-free active Langevin model derived from kinetic theory and support it with event-driven Monte Carlo collision simulations. The microscopic origin of activity is identified as quantum spin exchange, which transfers discrete internal spin energy into kinetic motion. Our work establishes a quantum-enabled route to active matter at the fundamental size limit of single atoms and opens perspectives for exploring the interplay of activity, quantum physics, and mesoscopic non-equilibrium thermodynamics.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将平均场交互粒子系统推广到状态空间包含空间变量与测度值分量的情形，并建立相应的强解理论、混沌传播与收敛性质。

Method: 采用局部Lipschitz且满足线性增长条件的漂移算子，空间分量由布朗扩散驱动，测度值分量由Arens–Eells空间中的投影柱噪声扰动；利用Wasserstein–1距离刻画经验测度的收敛。

Result: 在局部Lipschitz与线性增长假设下，证明了$N$粒子系统及非线性McKean–Vlasov方程的强解存在唯一性；当$N\to\infty$时，经验测度在期望意义下依Wasserstein–1距离收敛到唯一McKean–Vlasov解；非线性McKean–Vlasov动力学指数收敛到唯一不变测度。

Abstract: We study a stochastic mean-field interacting particle system whose state space is $\Y = \Tt^d \times \cP(U)$, where the first component represents a spatial variable and the second one is a probability measure over a compact metric space $U$. We first establish existence and uniqueness of strong solutions for both the $N$-particle system and the associated nonlinear McKean--Vlasov equation under locally Lipschitz and linear growth assumptions on the drift coefficients. We then prove propagation of chaos: as $N\to\infty$, the empirical measure converges in expectation in Wasserstein--1 distance towards the unique McKean--Vlasov solution. Further, we investigate exponential convergence of the nonlinear McKean--Vlasov dynamics towards a unique invariant measure.

### [21] [Toeplitz Determinants and Admissible Correlation Intervals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24603)
*Thomas Erben*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Using the classical Desnanot--Jacobi determinant identity, I derive a simple determinantal representation for the widths of admissible correlation intervals.
  As an immediate consequence, I recover the product expressions for admissible interval widths previously stated by Schneider & Hartlap (2009). The argument places these relations into the general framework of classical Toeplitz determinant theory.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 sine-Gordon (sG) 方程在光锥坐标系下 quarter plane 上初始边值 (IBV) 问题的适定性，并揭示左右半平面边界条件需求的差异。

Method: 采用 Riemann-Hilbert (RH) 问题框架，分别处理右半平面 ($x>0$) 和左半平面 ($x<0$) 上的 IBV 问题，并在 $x\to\pm\infty$ 方向上施加适当的衰减条件。

Result: 右半平面问题（$x\ge 0$）的解仅由初始数据 $u(x,0)$ 唯一确定；左半平面问题（$x\le 0$）除初始数据外，还必须给定边界数据 $u(0,t)$ 才能保证适定性。

Abstract: In this work, we study the initial boundary value (IBV) problems for the sine-Gordon (sG) equation in the light-cone coordinates $u_{xt}=\sin u$ in the quarter planes $x> 0$, $t>0$ and $x< 0$, $t>0$ assuming a suitable decay as $x\to +\infty$ or as $x\to -\infty$. Employing the Riemann--Hilbert (RH) problem framework, we demonstrate that these two IBV problems differ significantly with respect to the boundary data required for well-posedness. Specifically, the solution of the ``right problem'' ($x\ge 0$) is uniquely determined by the initial data $u(x,0)$, $x\ge 0$ alone whereas for the ``left problem'' ($x\le 0$), the boundary data $u(0,t)$ has to be prescribed in addition to the initial data in order to obtain a well-posed problem.

### [23] [Recursive behavior in a diatomic FPUT lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24280)
*Guo Deng,Andrea Pezzi,Genghong Lin,Miguel Onorato*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 研究了具有立方非简谐势的双原子费米-帕斯塔-乌拉姆（FPUT）晶格，发现两类回复行为：经典的FPUT回复以及仅存在于双原子体系的光学-声学-声学共振回复。通过约化傅里叶空间模型、数值模拟（双原子Toda晶格和颗粒链）以及连续极限下的可积三耦合偏微分方程（PDE）系统，验证了结果的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对双原子FPUT晶格（含立方非简谐势）的解析分析，证明光学-声学-声学共振相互作用存在；构建约化傅里叶空间动力学模型以复现相同的回复行为；通过数值模拟验证双原子Toda晶格和双原子颗粒链中的回复现象；在连续极限下从双原子模型推导出三耦合PDE系统。

Result: 发现两类回复：（1）经典FPUT回复，其回复周期与非线性强度的关系类似于单原子情形；（2）双原子体系特有的光学-声学-声学三傅里叶模态共振相互作用导致的回复。约化傅里叶空间模型成功复现了回复行为。数值模拟在Toda晶格和颗粒链中均观察到相同回复现象。连续极限下导出已知可积的三耦合PDE系统。

Conclusion: 双原子FPUT晶格中存在两种不同类型的回复行为，其中光学-声学-声学共振回复是单原子体系所不具备的新现象；该现象在多种双原子非线性晶格模型中具有普适性，并在连续极限下关联到可积偏微分方程系统。

Abstract: We study the diatomic FPUT lattice with cubic anharmonic potential, and analyze the recurrent behaviour of its solutions. We find that two distinct types of recurrence occur. One type is the classic FPUT recurrence; for such recurrence, we find that the relation between recurrence period and nonlinear strength is similar to that in the monatomic case. The other type, which cannot exist in the monatomic lattice, is the recurrence due to the interactions between modes in the two branches of the dispersion relation. Indeed, we prove the existence of the optical-acoustical-acoustical resonant interaction between three Fourier modes for which a recurrent behavior in the distribution of the energy is observed. In addition, we develop a reduced Fourier-space dynamical model that reproduces the same recurrent behavior. We assess the robustness of our results through numerical simulations of the diatomic Toda lattice and the diatomic granular chain; in both cases, the same recursive behavior is observed. Finally, in the continuous limit, we derive from the diatomic model a system of three coupled PDEs which are known to be integrable.

### [25] [Arithmetic Supports of Lax Difference Hierarchies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24273)
*Sylvain Carpentier*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文完整分类了具有独立系数的单式有限带标量差分算子，证明了其存在无穷多个支持保持流的充要条件是支持构成算术数列（arithmetic progression）。由此得到由三个整数(N,p,m)标定的有限带标量Lax层级分类，该框架统一了多个经典可积格点系统并生成无穷多新例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对具有独立系数的单式有限带标量差分算子进行分类，刻画其支持（support）上能够承载无穷多个保支持流（support-preserving flows）的算子结构，从而建立有限带标量Lax层级（Lax hierarchies）的完整分类理论。

Method: 通过推导支持上指数必须形成算术数列这一算术条件（arithmetic condition），建立算子可积性的充要刻画；并证明每个算术支持均可构造一个无穷局部Lax流层级（infinite hierarchy of local Lax flows），进而使用三个整数(N,p,m)完成分类。

Result: 有限带标量Lax层级由三个整数(N,p,m)完全分类，分别对应领头阶（leading order）、支持的公差（common difference）和生成元个数（number of generators）。该分类恢复了Toda、Volterra、Narita–Itoh–Bogoyavlensky和Blaszak-Marciniak格点（lattices），并产生无穷多新例子。特别地，支持(-1,1,m)给出了Beffa-Wang层级的标量差分Lax表示，而m=2时对应于其Belov-Chaltikian约化。

Conclusion: 该工作为有限带标量差分算子的可积性提供了基于支持算术性质的完整分类标准，统一了多个经典可积系统并揭示了新的可积结构。

Abstract: We classify monic finite-band scalar difference operators with independent coefficients admitting infinitely many support-preserving flows. We prove that such operators are completely characterized by an arithmetic condition on their support: the exponents must form an arithmetic progression. Conversely, every arithmetic support gives rise to an infinite hierarchy of local Lax flows. As a consequence, finite-band scalar Lax hierarchies with independent coefficients are classified by three integers (N,p,m), corresponding respectively to the leading order, the common difference of the support, and the number of generators. This framework recovers several classical systems, including the Toda, Volterra, Narita--Itoh--Bogoyavlensky, and Blaszak-Marciniak lattices, while simultaneously producing infinitely many additional examples. In particular, the support (-1,1,m) yields a scalar difference Lax representation of the Beffa-Wang hierarchy, and its Belov-Chaltikian reduction in the case m=2.

</details>

### [26] [Red vs. Blue: How metallicity shapes black hole dynamics and mergers in dense star clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23788)
*Saloni Agrawal,Kyle Kremer,Michael Zevin,Cailin Plunkett,Elena González Prieto,Fulya Kıroğlu,Christopher E. O'Connor,Frederic A. Rasio,Claire S. Ye*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过一套新的蒙特卡罗星团模拟（Monte Carlo star cluster simulations），精细覆盖了较高金属丰度（[Fe/H]≥-1）参数空间，揭示了高金属丰度环境对黑洞质量函数、并合率、留存率及延迟时间分布的关键影响，并成功解释了GW241011和GW241110等低质量引力波事件可能源于高金属丰度球状星团的动力学起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）观测到的引力波事件（如GW241011和GW241110）具有较低的质量，与经典的低金属丰度球状星团模型（low-metallicity globular cluster models）所预测的较大质量黑洞存在矛盾，暗示这些事件可能起源于高金属丰度环境。为验证这一假设，需系统性研究金属丰度对星团动力学及黑洞并合的影响。

Method: 作者开展了一套新的蒙特卡罗星团模拟（Monte Carlo star cluster simulations），在金属丰度参数上进行了精细化覆盖，重点关注[Fe/H]≥-1的范围，即大多数星系中“红色”球状星团亚群（red globular cluster subpopulation）对应的金属丰度区间。

Result: 模拟显示，金属丰度显著影响黑洞质量函数（mass function of black holes）、黑洞并合总数、黑洞因新生冲走（natal kicks）的留存率、黑洞驱动星团动力学质量分层时间（mass segregation time）以及并合延迟时间分布（merger delay time distribution）。高金属丰度模型产生的低质量层级式并合（low-mass hierarchical mergers）与GW241011和GW241110的质量比和成分质量一致。

Conclusion: 高金属丰度球状星团在产生当前LVK观测到的低质量引力波事件中扮演重要角色，未来LVK星表的物理解释应充分考虑高金属丰度星团的贡献。

Abstract: Dense star clusters are a well-established environment for the formation of gravitational wave sources through dynamical interactions. Recent LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) events such as GW241011 and GW241110 provide some of the best evidence yet for a dynamical origin. However, their relatively low component masses are in tension with predictions from low-metallicity globular cluster models (which typically produce more massive black holes), hinting that these events may have originated in higher-metallicity environments. Here we present a new set of Monte Carlo star cluster simulations with refined coverage in metallicity, focusing specifically on clusters with [Fe/H] $\geq-1$, similar to the ''red'' globular cluster subpopulation observed in most galaxies. We show that metallicity has a significant effect on the mass function of black holes and black hole mergers, the total number of black hole mergers per cluster, black hole retention from natal kicks, the mass segregation time for black-hole-driven cluster dynamics, and the merger delay time distribution. We also show that high-metallicity cluster models produce low-mass hierarchical mergers consistent with the mass ratios and component masses of GW241011 and GW241110, motivating the importance of high-metallicity clusters in the astrophysical interpretation of future LVK catalogs.

### [28] [On Chen-Teo geometries with cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24761)
*Bernardo Araneda*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究带有非零宇宙学常数的爱因斯坦度量推广，证明在陈-陶几何（Chen-Teo geometry）框架下，解要么是带λ的Plebański-Demiański度量，要么具有反自偶Weyl张量（anti-self-dual Weyl tensor），并详细分析了后者在λ<0时的结构、共形边界、类ALE标量平坦Kähler度量的全局共形性、不同拓扑的引力瞬子构造，以及四极解（4-pole solution）分类归属。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 陈-陶几何（Chen-Teo geometry）是首个反驳欧几里得黑洞唯一性猜想（Euclidean black hole uniqueness conjecture）的AF引力瞬子（gravitational instanton），其带宇宙学常数λ的爱因斯坦度量推广问题尚未解决，本文旨在系统构造并分类这类推广。

Method: 采用微分几何与广义相对论中的度量构造方法，通过分析Weyl张量的自偶性（self-duality）条件进行分类讨论；对λ<0情形，利用共形变换构造全局共形（globally conformal）关系，并借助Calderbank-Pedersen分类（Calderbank-Pedersen classification）识别几何结构。

Result: 得到两类解：Plebański-Demiański度量（Plebański-Demiański metric）带λ，或具有反自偶Weyl张量（anti-self-dual Weyl tensor）的解。后者在λ<0时存在分隔两个渐近双曲度量（asymptotically hyperbolic metrics）的共形无穷远（conformal infinity）；其中之一全局共形于一个ALE标量平坦Kähler度量（ALE scalar-flat Kähler metric）；构造了不同拓扑的引力瞬子；该几何属于Calderbank-Pedersen分类中的四极解。

Conclusion: 成功建立了带宇宙学常数的陈-陶几何推广的严格分类框架，揭示了其与ALE Kähler几何、共形无穷远结构及引力瞬子拓扑多样性的深层联系，为理解非零λ下引力瞬子的唯一性问题提供了新视角。

Abstract: The Chen-Teo geometry is a Riemannian, Ricci-flat ALF 4-manifold, containing an AF gravitational instanton that gives the first counterexample to the Euclidean black hole uniqueness conjecture. We investigate the problem of constructing an Einstein analogue with a non-zero cosmological constant $λ$. We show that the solution is either the Plebański-Demiański metric with $λ$, or it has an anti-self-dual Weyl tensor. We study the latter case in detail: we prove that for $λ<0$, there is a conformal infinity separating two asymptotically hyperbolic metrics; we show that one of them is globally conformal to an ALE scalar-flat Kähler metric; we construct gravitational instantons with different topologies; and we show that the geometry is a 4-pole solution in the Calderbank-Pedersen classification.

</details>

### [29] [Dual-isotope narrow-line MOT of dysprosium by phase modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23958)
*M. Dürbeck,L. Reihs,J. Seifert,B. Choudhari,J. P. Marulanda-Serna,N. Werum,M. De Pas,G. Meijer,G. Valtolina*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种窄线磁光阱（narrow-line MOT）中同时装载和囚禁镝（Dy）原子两种不同同位素的方法。通过高功率自由空间电光调制器（EOM）在421 nm减速跃迁和626 nm MOT跃迁上产生光学边带，并利用模块化谐振电子电路匹配边带分离量与同位素频移，实现了164Dy-162Dy和162Dy-160Dy玻色同位素混合物。通过调节EOM驱动频率控制辐射力与重力的相互作用，实现了两同位素空间位置的全控，为窄线MOT中原子混合物的操控提供了经济有效的新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现窄线磁光阱（narrow-line MOT）中多种同位素的同时装载与囚禁，并发展一种无需复杂激光系统即可控制同位素混合物的经济有效方法。

Method: 采用高功率自由空间电光调制器（EOM）在421 nm和626 nm两条跃迁线上产生光学边带，通过模块化谐振电子电路将边带分离量精确匹配至目标同位素的同位素频移（isotope shift），并利用EOM驱动频率调控窄线MOT中辐射力（radiation force）与重力（gravity）的相互作用，从而控制两种同位素的空间位置。

Result: 成功实现了玻色同位素164Dy-162Dy和162Dy-160Dy的混合物囚禁，并能通过调节EOM驱动频率完全控制同位素混合物的组成及空间分布。

Conclusion: 该方法为窄线MOT中多种原子物种混合物的控制提供了一种新颖且经济高效的途径。

Abstract: We report on the characterization of a narrow-line magneto-optical trap (MOT), where two different isotopes of the dysprosium (Dy) atom can be simultaneously loaded and trapped. We rely on phase modulation via high-power, free-space electro-optic modulators (EOMs) to generate optical sidebands at the correct detuning for two different isotopes. This technique is applied on the slowing transition at 421 nm and the MOT transition at 626 nm. Using modular resonant electronic circuits, we match the sideband separation to the isotope shift among the two target isotopes, realizing mixtures of the bosonic isotopes 164Dy -162Dy and 162Dy -160Dy. We exploit the interplay between radiation forces and gravity in the narrow-line MOT to control the spatial position of the two isotopes with the EOM drive frequency. We demonstrate full control of the isotopic mixture with the EOM drive, offering new and cost-effective capabilities for controlling mixtures of atomic species that can be trapped in a narrow-line MOT.

### [30] [Learning to Trigger: Reinforcement Learning at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23993)
*Zixin Ding,Shaghayegh Emam,Giovanna Salvi,Cecilia Tosciri,Abhijith Gandrakota,Jennifer Ngadiuba,Nhan Tran,Christian Herwig,David W. Miller,Yuxin Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将大型强子对撞机（LHC）的在线触发阈值调节（trigger threshold tuning）建模为序贯决策问题，采用强化学习（reinforcement learning）方法，基于分组滤波策略优化（GFPO）框架的两种变体（GFPO-F、GFPO-FR），在模拟和真实CMS碰撞数据上实现了触发系统在容忍带宽内滞留时间比率的显著提升以及信号效率的增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高吞吐量科学设施（如大型强子对撞机）依赖实时事件过滤（触发系统，triggering），但现有触发菜单（trigger menu）多为静态且依赖人工调参，随着探测器条件、堆积（pileup）及本底组成的漂移，性能会逐渐次优。因此，需要一种能够在线自适应调节触发阈值的动态方法。

Method: 将在线阈值调节建模为强化学习序贯决策问题：智能体（agent）读取流式的近期速率和信号敏感特征摘要，并动态更新触发阈值，以最大化信号效率（signal efficiency）的同时将本底率（background rate）控制在目标容忍带内。基于分组滤波策略优化（Group-Filtered Policy Optimization, GFPO）框架进行流式控制适配，提出两种变体：GFPO-F和GFPO-FR，在训练中强制执行本底率可行性约束。

Result: 在模拟数据上，智能体使在容忍时间区间占比提升48%（总横向能量H_T触发）和28%（基于重建损失的异常检测（anomaly-detection, AD）触发），容忍区间内信号效率累积增益最高达2%。在真实CMS碰撞数据（Run 283408）上，无需微调即实现容忍区间占比相比基线提升56%（H_T）和28%（AD），并在两种触发器中均获得进一步信号效率增益。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在真实的大型强子对撞机碰撞数据上实现了基于强化学习的触发控制，证明了RL方法在流式数据场景下在线调节触发阈值的可行性与有效性，为高能物理实验的实时数据过滤提供了自适应调优的新途径。

Abstract: High-throughput scientific facilities such as the Large Hadron Collider depend on real-time event filtering (\textit{triggering}) under tight constraints on bandwidth, latency, and storage. In practice, trigger menus are largely static and hand-tuned and can become suboptimal as detector conditions, pileup, and background composition drift over time. We cast online threshold tuning as a sequential decision-making problem: a reinforcement learning agent ingests streaming summaries of recent rates and signal-sensitive features and updates trigger thresholds to maximize signal efficiency while tracking a target background rate within a tolerance band. We adapt Group-Filtered Policy Optimization (GFPO) to streaming control and introduce two variants (GFPO-F, GFPO-FR) that enforce background rate feasibility during training. On a benchmark that emulates realistic collider operation, we study two representative triggers: a total transverse energy ($H_{T}$) trigger sensitive to pileup variation, and an anomaly-detection (AD) trigger based on reconstruction loss for rare or non-standard signatures. On Monte Carlo streams, our agent increases the fraction of in-tolerance time intervals by 48\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD), with a cumulative gain of up to 2\% in signal efficiency on those in-tolerance intervals. Transferring from simulation to \emph{real} collision data (CMS Run 283408), the same agent, without fine-tuning, achieves a 56\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD) in-tolerance improvement over baselines, with further signal-efficiency gain on both triggers. To our knowledge, this is the \emph{first} demonstration of RL-based trigger control on real Large Hadron Collider collision data. Code is available at https://github.com/Zixind/GFPO\_LHC.

</details>


### [31] [Cyclic Denoising Reveals Ultrastable Memories in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24000)
*Rishabh Sharma,Stefano Martiniani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出循环去噪（cyclic denoising）作为一种针对图像扩散模型的提取攻击方法，通过受控噪声下的反复前向与反向扩散，揭示模型分布中标准采样难以触及的记忆化训练图像。该方法无需梯度、权重检查或提示词，可作为生成景观的物理探针和记忆化审计工具，对隐私、版权合规及模型指纹识别具有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像扩散模型存在记忆化训练数据（memorized training data）的隐私风险，但标准采样方法难以暴露此类记忆化区域。需要一种无梯度、无需提示词或先验知识的攻击方法，以审计模型是否记忆了受版权保护或私密的图像。

Method: 受无序固体中随机组织（random organization in disordered solids）启发，提出循环去噪攻击，即在受控噪声振幅下重复进行前向扩散（加噪）和反向扩散（去噪）过程。该方法仅需采样器级别控制，无需梯度、权重检查、提示词、标题（captions）或训练数据先验知识。主要协议是完全无条件的（fully unconditioned），区别于依赖大规模提示生成与后验相似性或成员推理过滤的生成-过滤攻击（generate-and-filter attacks）。

Result: 在Stable Diffusion v1.4和像素空间DDPM上验证了现象，在潜空间（latent-space）和像素空间（pixel-space）扩散模型上表现一致。最深吸引子（attractors）具有超稳定性（ultrastable）：在近乎完全破坏后仍能再生，并通过数千次加噪-去噪循环持续存在。这些吸引子对应记忆化的训练图像，包括库存照片、品牌水印和网络爬取伪影。在不同噪声振幅下观察到类似屈服（yielding-like）的转变：低振幅循环产生平凡吸收不动点或极限环，高振幅则诱导重排、势阱跳跃（basin hopping）和结构化记忆化吸引子盆中的长期俘获。此外还观察到分层部分吸收（hierarchical partial absorption）、提示稳定化吸引子盆（prompt-stabilized basins）以及恢复吸引子集的跨初始条件普适性（cross-initial-condition universality）。

Conclusion: 循环去噪既是一种受物理学启发的生成景观（generative landscape）探针，也是一种实用的记忆化审计工具，对隐私保护、版权合规和模型指纹识别（model fingerprinting）具有重要启示。

Abstract: We introduce cyclic denoising -- repeated forward and reverse diffusion at controlled noise amplitudes -- as an extraction attack for image diffusion models. Inspired by random organization in disordered solids, cyclic denoising exposes regions of the learned distribution that are largely inaccessible to standard sampling. The dynamics drive samples toward attractors with a broad stability spectrum. The deepest attractors are ultrastable: they regenerate after near-total corruption and persist through thousands of noising-denoising cycles. Many of these attractors correspond to memorized training images, including stock photographs, brand watermarks, and web-crawl artifacts. The attack requires only sampler-level control, with no gradients, weight inspection, prompts, captions, or prior knowledge of the training data. Unlike generate-and-filter attacks, which rely on large-scale prompted generation and post-hoc similarity or membership-inference filtering, our main protocol is fully unconditioned. We demonstrate the phenomenon in Stable Diffusion v1.4 and in a pixel-space DDPM, showing consistent behavior across latent- and pixel-space diffusion models. Across noise amplitudes, we observe a yielding-like transition: low-amplitude cycling produces trivial absorbing fixed points or limit cycles, while larger amplitudes induce rearrangements, basin hopping, and long-lived trapping in structured memorized attractor basins. We also observe hierarchical partial absorption, prompt-stabilized basins, and cross-initial-condition universality of the recovered attractor set. Our results therefore show that cyclic denoising is both a physics-inspired probe of generative landscapes and a practical tool for memorization auditing, with implications for privacy, copyright compliance, and model fingerprinting.

</details>

### [32] [Vertex Superalgebras for Hypertoric Varieties and 3d Abelian Gauge Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24708)
*Tomoyuki Arakawa,Andrea E. V. Ferrari,Sven Möller*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文在光滑超环簇（smooth hypertoric variety）上构造了一个$\hbar$-进（$\hbar$-adic）顶点算子超代数层（sheaf of vertex operator superalgebras），其整体截面对应于3d $\mathcal{N}=4$规范理论的$A$-扭曲边界。该构造证明了大类边界顶点算子超代数的3d Higgs分支猜想（3d Higgs branch conjecture），并指出这些代数是拟光滑（quasi-lisse）的，且是Kuwabara此前定义的非拟光滑超环顶点算子超代数的（费米子）简单流扩充（fermionic simple-current extension），从而将偏西塔函数（partial theta functions）提升为准模形式（quasimodular forms）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超环簇（hypertoric varieties）作为一类辛奇点（symplectic singularities）及其消解，在3d $\mathcal{N}=4$超对称量子场论中作为Higgs分支（Higgs branch）和Coulomb分支（Coulomb branch）出现。此前Kuwabara构造的超环顶点算子超代数（purely even）普遍不是拟光滑（quasi-lisse）的，本文旨在构造一个新的$\hbar$-进顶点算子超代数层，以解决3d Higgs分支猜想并为边界代数建立更完整的结构。

Method: 通过微局域化（microlocalisation）方法，在光滑超环簇上构造一个$\hbar$-进顶点算子超代数层；将其整体截面视为3d规范理论$A$-扭曲边界（$A$-twisted boundary）。通过分析该代数的关联仿射簇（associated affine variety）与奇异超环簇（singular hypertoric variety）的对应关系验证3d Higgs分支猜想。进一步通过与Kuwabara构造的代数进行简单流扩充（simple-current extension）比较，研究其对偶性质（symplectic duality）和特征标（characters）的影响。

Result: 该超环顶点算子超代数的关联仿射簇恢复了奇异超环簇，从而证明了大类边界顶点算子超代数的3d Higgs分支猜想；这些顶点算子超代数是拟光滑的。新构造的顶点算子超代数是Kuwabara代数的（费米子）简单流扩充，后者被提升为从部分（或假）西塔函数（partial/false theta functions）到准模形式的特征标。

Conclusion: 本文证明了大类边界顶点算子超代数满足3d Higgs分支猜想，揭示了其在辛对偶（symplectic duality）框架下的角色，并建立了超环顶点算子超代数与拟模形式（quasimodular forms）之间的新联系。

Abstract: Hypertoric (or toric hyperkähler) varieties are a class of symplectic singularities and their resolutions, obtained as Hamiltonian reductions of a symplectic vector space acted on by a torus. In physics, they appear as Higgs (and Coulomb) branches of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric quantum field theories with abelian gauge group.
  In this work, we construct an $\hbar$-adic (in the sense of microlocalisation) sheaf of vertex operator superalgebras over a given smooth hypertoric variety. Its global sections give the $A$-twisted boundary of the corresponding 3d gauge theory. We use this to prove that the associated affine variety of this hypertoric vertex operator superalgebra recovers the singular hypertoric variety. This proves the 3d Higgs branch conjecture for a large class of boundary vertex operator superalgebras. In particular, these vertex operator superalgebras are quasi-lisse.
  This is in contrast to the (purely even) hypertoric vertex operator superalgebras (and their $\hbar$-adic localisations) constructed previously by Kuwabara as global sections of sheaves on families of universal Poisson deformations of the hypertoric varieties. These are generally not quasi-lisse. We show that the vertex operator superalgebras defined in this paper are (fermionic) simple-current extensions of those defined by Kuwabara, and investigate the consequences for symplectic duality and characters. We observe that the latter are upgraded from partial (or false) theta functions to quasimodular forms.

</details>

### [33] [On the amplitude expansion of gluon correlators in $\textrm{AdS}_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23776)
*Humberto Gomez,Renann Lipinski Jusinskas,Arthur Lipstein,Cristhiam Lopez-Arcos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明$\textrm{AdS}_4$中的树图胶子关联函数（gluon correlators）可以自然地用平直空间散射振幅（flat-space scattering amplitudes）展开，其中每一点关联函数可分解为能量极点之和，其留数对应平直空间振幅；曲率修正则由合并外部数据后的低点振幅捕获，并借助AdS版本的Berends-Giele流递归定义外部极化合并，从而构建出全重数公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在反德西特空间（anti-de Sitter space, AdS）中计算关联函数（correlators）的传统方法依赖于逐个费曼图（Feynman diagram）计算，过程繁琐且缺乏透明性。本文旨在提供一种更优雅、更高效的替代方案，将AdS关联函数与平直空间散射振幅直接联系起来。

Method: 通过在$\textrm{AdS}_4$中引入类似于Berends-Giele流（Berends-Giele currents）的递归结构，定义外部极化的合并规则，从而将$n$点关联函数分解为平直空间振幅在能量极点（energy poles）处的留数之和。曲率修正（curvature corrections）通过合并外部数据后的低点振幅来捕捉，最终构造出适用于任意重数的公式。

Result: 建立了全重数关联函数与平直空间散射振幅之间的显式分解关系，证明了每个$n$点关联函数均可用平直空间振幅的低点组合来表示；该公式通过五点费曼图计算得到验证。

Conclusion: 本文方法在完整关联函数层面而非单个图层面工作，为AdS中树图胶子关联函数的计算提供了一种简洁且透明的全新途径，有望推广到更高阶或更一般的背景。

Abstract: We show that tree-level gluon correlators in $\textrm{AdS}_4$ admit a natural expansion in terms of flat-space scattering amplitudes at all multiplicities. In particular, every $n$-point correlator can be decomposed into a sum over energy poles whose residues are flat-space amplitudes. The $n$-point amplitude encodes the flat-space limit while curvature corrections are captured by lower-point amplitudes with merged external data. The merging of external polarizations is recursively defined via an AdS analogue of the Berends-Giele currents, giving rise to all-multiplicity formulae which we verify against Feynman diagram computations up to five points. Crucially, our approach works at the level of full correlators rather than individual diagrams, providing an elegant and transparent alternative to conventional approaches for computing correlators in anti-de Sitter space.

</details>


### [34] [Excitability of Gaussian states with VEVs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23779)
*Jacqueline Caminiti,Federico Capeccia,Jonathan Sorce*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将arXiv:2604.19861中关于零均值高斯态可激发性的判据推广到非零均值情形（即具有真空期望值的高斯态），证明可激发性等价于连通两点函数满足原判据且真空期望值之差相对于两点函数有界。作为应用，在反德西特时空中证明了真空期望值偏移可从Klein-Gordon真空中被激发当且仅当其边界外推可从对偶共形场论的真空中被激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前工作中针对零均值高斯态的可激发性判据推广到更具一般性的非零均值情形，即包含真空期望值（vacuum expectation values, VEVs）的高斯态，以建立更完整的自由场理论中态激发条件。

Method: 通过数学证明的方式，在广义自由场理论框架下分析非零均值高斯态的可激发性条件；并将结果应用于反德西特时空（anti-de Sitter spacetime），通过边界外推法计算Klein-Gordon真空与对偶共形场论（conformal field theory）真空之间的关系。

Result: 非零均值高斯态可被激发的充要条件为：(i) 连通两点函数满足arXiv:2604.19861中给出的判据，且(ii) 真空期望值之差相对于两点函数有界。在反德西特时空中，真空期望值偏移可从Klein-Gordon真空中被激发当且仅当其边界外推可从对偶共形场论的真空中被激发。

Conclusion: 建立了含真空期望值的高斯态可激发性的完整理论判据，并通过反德西特/共形场论对偶（AdS/CFT duality）给出了一个明确的交叉验证实例，深化了对自由场理论中激发过程的理解。

Abstract: In arXiv:2604.19861, we gave general criteria for when one zero-mean Gaussian state can be excited out of another in a (generalized) free field theory. Here we extend this analysis to the case of nonzero mean, i.e., to Gaussian states with vacuum expectation values (VEVs). We prove that excitability is possible exactly when (i) the connected two-point functions satisfy criteria like those in arXiv:2604.19861, and (ii) the difference of the VEVs is bounded relative to the two-point functions. As an application, we give an explicit computation showing that in anti-de Sitter spacetime, a VEV shift can be excited from the Klein-Gordon vacuum if and only if its boundary extrapolation can be excited from the vacuum of the dual conformal field theory.

</details>


### [35] [Controlled Chaos in 4D SCFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23785)
*Florent Baume,Atakan Çavuşoğlu,Vivek Chakrabhavi,Jonathan J. Heckman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过四维超共形场论（SCFT）中受控子系统的自旋链表示，研究了混沌动力学在量子场论中的出现，并利用膨胀算子（dilatation operator）本征值的统计分布（能级排斥、谱刚性和谱形因子）诊断混沌相变，同时指出Krylov复杂度等诊断工具在某些情况下不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌动力学在多个物理系统中扮演重要角色，其定性标志之一是出现足够“复杂”的能谱，但直接验证相互作用量子场论（quantum field theory）中混沌的出现具有挑战性。本文旨在为四维超共形场论（SCFT）提供一种可控的混沌诊断方案。

Method: 考虑一类由四维$\mathcal{N}=4$超杨-米尔斯理论（Super Yang–Mills theory）的轨形（orbifold）构造得到的SCFT，其中受控子扇区的算子混合由一维有效自旋链（spin chain）描述，近邻相互作用通过SCFT的边缘耦合（marginal coupling）调节。通过分析膨胀算子本征值的统计分布（能级排斥、谱刚性、谱形因子）来诊断混沌的出现，并考察Krylov复杂度等替代诊断方案的有效性。

Result: 调节边缘耦合可使自旋链进入混沌谱（chaotic spectrum），而通常情况下自旋链表现为安德森局域化（Anderson localization）。Krylov复杂度有时并不能可靠地捕捉混沌信息。该结构在弦论实现的目标空间中定义了一个混沌台球系统（chaotic billiard）。在大$N$全息对偶（holographic dual）描述中，单自旋链近似需补充多迹（multi-trace）动力学，即多条自旋链的分裂与合并。

Conclusion: 该方法为量子场论中混沌的定量诊断提供了有效工具，揭示了混沌谱与局域化相变之间的关联，并指出了常见诊断工具的局限性。

Abstract: Chaotic dynamics play an important role in a number of physical systems. One of the qualitative hallmarks of this behavior is the appearance of a sufficiently "complex" spectrum of energy levels. This also makes it challenging to directly verify the onset of chaos in interacting quantum field theories. We present a class of 4D superconformal field theories (SCFTs) given by orbifolds of 4D $\mathcal{N} = 4$ Super Yang--Mills theory in which operator mixing in a controlled subsector is described by an effective spin chain in one spatial dimension with nearest neighbor interactions tuned by the marginal couplings of the SCFT. Tuning the marginal couplings results in a chaotic spectrum, while generically the spin chain exhibits Anderson localization. We diagnose the onset of chaos by analyzing the statistical distribution of eigenvalues of the dilatation operator, in particular properties such as eigenvalue level repulsion, spectral rigidity, and the spectral form factor. We also show that other diagnostics such as Krylov complexity sometimes do not faithfully capture this information. This structure defines a chaotic billiard in the target space of the stringy realization. We also comment on the large $N$ holographic dual description, where the controlled single spin chain approximation must be supplemented by multi-trace dynamics, i.e., the splitting and joining of multiple spin chains.

</details>


### [36] [Towards OSV in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23893)
*Nikolay Bobev,Sunjin Choi,Junho Hong,Valentin Reys*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过超对称局域化（supersymmetric localization）技术，在Cardy-like极限下建立了三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形场论（SCFT）中超共形指标（superconformal index）与压扁三球面配分函数（squashed three-sphere partition function）之间的平方模关系 $Z_{S^1\times S^2} \sim |Z_{S^3_b}|^2$，并进一步推广至拓扑扭变指标（topologically twisted index）。在全息对偶（holography）语境下，该关系联系了超对称渐近AdS$_4$黑洞的配分函数与对偶SCFT的大$N$极限，类似于OSV猜想在平直时空黑洞中的表述。作者利用M2膜SCFT的大$N$结果验证了这一关系，并简要讨论了5d类似情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT中超共形指标与压扁三球面配分函数之间的精确解析关系；并在全息框架下，将这一关系应用于超对称渐近AdS$_4$黑洞的配分函数与对偶场论大$N$极限之间的对应，从而类比并推广平直时空中的OSV猜想。

Method: 采用超对称局域化技术；在Cardy-like极限（small $S^1$ radius and large squashing parameter）下使用鞍点近似（saddle point approximation）推导指标与配分函数之间的平方模关系；并利用M2膜SCFT的大$N$局域化结果进行数值验证。

Result: 建立了超共形指标与压扁三球面配分函数之间的平方模关系 $Z_{S^1\times S^2} \sim |Z_{S^3_b}|^2$，以及拓扑扭变指标与压扁球面配分函数之间的类似关系。在全息对偶中，该关系将超对称渐近AdS$_4$黑洞的配分函数与对偶SCFT的大$N$极限（即规范超引力预势（gauged supergravity prepotential））联系起来。M2膜SCFT的大$N$结果验证了该关系。此外，类似的结论在5d SCFT和渐近AdS$_6$黑洞中也得到初步讨论。

Conclusion: 本文揭示三维超共形指标与压扁球面配分函数之间存在一个普适的平方模关系，该关系在全息对偶中扮演类似OSV猜想的角色，为理解渐近AdS黑洞的微观熵提供了新途径；同时该框架可推广至更高维度的SCFT与黑洞系统。

Abstract: We use supersymmetric localization for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs to establish a relation of the form $Z_{S^1\times S^2} \sim |Z_{S^3_b}|^2$ between the superconformal index and the squashed three-sphere partition function. This applies to general 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs and is derived using a saddle point approximation in the Cardy-like limit of small $S^1$ radius and large squashing parameter. We also show a similar relation between the topologically twisted index and the squashed sphere partition function. In the context of holography our results lead to a relation between the partition function of supersymmetric asymptotically AdS$_4$ black holes and the large $N$ limit of $Z_{S^3_b}$ of the dual SCFT. Since the latter encodes the gauged supergravity prepotential, this result is akin to the OSV conjecture for asymptotically flat black holes. We confirm this relation in detail for SCFTs arising from M2-branes using recent large $N$ results from supersymmetric localization. We also briefly discuss a similar relation for 5d SCFTs and its implications for asymptotically AdS$_6$ black holes.

</details>


### [37] [General Lagrangian formulations for mixed-antisymmetric tensor fields on flat backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24008)
*Alexander A. Reshetnyak*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文首次在d维闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski space-time）中，针对满足杨图（Young tableau）$Y[\hat{s}_1,\hat{s}_2,...,\hat{s}_k]$且具有k列约化/非约化整数高自旋（higher-spin）无质量和有质量庞加莱群表示（Poincare group representations），提出了拉格朗日形式（Lagrangian formulations）。通过BRST方法，利用完全与非完全的BRST算符，在度规类形式（metric-like formulation）中用张量场描述粒子，并找到了等价动力学但不同位形空间的无约束与有约束规范拉格朗日表述，同时提出了合理相互作用的构想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高自旋场理论的拉格朗日形式构建是一个长期难题，尤其是针对混合反对称（mixed-antisymmetric）张量表示。本文旨在填补杨图多列整数高自旋庞加莱群表示在d维时空中的拉格朗日形式空白，为后续相互作用研究奠定基础。

Method: 采用BRST程序（BRST procedure），分别使用完全BRST算符$Q$和不完全BRST算符$Q_c$。首先在辅助福克空间（Fock space）中描述玻色子混合反对称高自旋场，并将初始算符约束系统（operator constraint system）转化为第一类算符约束系统（first-class operator constraints）。通过Verma模（Verma module）首次找到约束子代数（constraint subalgebra）的辅助表示，该表示因豪威对偶性（Howe duality）与$so(k,k)$代数同构，并利用新的振荡子变量构成福克模（Fock module）中包含第二类算符（second-class operators）的子系统。

Result: 得到了两种等价的拉格朗日规范形式：一种是无约束形式（使用$Q$），另一种是有约束形式（使用$Q_c$及BRST不变的代数约束）。这两种形式具有不同的位形空间（configuration spaces），但动力学等价。此外，提出了合理相互作用（consistent interactions）的概念性方案。

Conclusion: 本文为d维闵可夫斯基时空中杨图多列整数高自旋粒子（无质量和有质量情况）提供了完整的拉格朗日形式框架，并通过Verma模和豪威对偶性解决了约束系统的转化问题。这项工作为未来研究高自旋场之间的相互作用提供了理论基础和方法路径。

Abstract: Lagrangian formulations for (ir)reducible integer higher-spin massless and massive Poincare group representations subject to Young tableau with $k$ columns $Y[\hat{s}_1,\hat{s}_2,...,\hat{s}_k]$ in $d$-dimensional Minkowski space-time are firstly presented. The particles are described in a metric-like formulation by tensor fields with $k$ groups of antisymmetric Lorentz indices $Φ_{μ^1[{\hat{s}_1}],μ^2[{\hat{s}_2}],..., μ^k[{\hat{s}_k}]}$ by means of the BRST procedure with complete, $Q$, and incomplete, $Q_c$, BRST operators. Starting from a description of bosonic mixed-antisymmetric higher-spin fields in terms of an auxiliary Fock space associated with a special Poincare module, we realize a conversion of the initial operator constraint system into a system of first-class operator constraints. To this aim, we find, in first time, by means of Verma module the auxiliary representations of the constraint subalgebra, to be isomorphic due to Howe duality to $so(k,k)$ algebra, and containing the subsystem of second-class operators in terms of new oscillator variables forming the Fock module. An unconstrained (with $Q$) and constrained (with $Q_c$ and BRST invariant algebraic constraints) gauge Lagrangian formulations with equivalent dynamics, but different configuration spaces are found. Concept of consistent interactions are suggested.

</details>


### [38] [Null limit of large-charge correlators in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ Super-Yang-Mills theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24018)
*Benjamin Basso,Thiago Fleury,Erkan Kaluç,Didina Serban*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个关于平面 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯（Super-Yang-Mills）理论中零极限（null limit）下大电荷关联子（large-charge correlators）的对数双对数行为的猜想，将其推广至任意 n 点函数到全圈阶，并用倾斜尖点反常维度（tilted cusp anomalous dimension）来描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平面 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论中，零极限下大电荷关联子的对数双对数行为尚未被完全理解，作者旨在将此前四点及五点函数的结果推广至一般 n 点函数，并建立与有质量振幅（massive amplitudes）小质量行为的联系。

Method: 作者基于对四点及五点函数早期结果的推广，提出一个猜想性（conjecture）方案，预测了 n 点关联子在零极限下的双对数行为，该行为由倾斜尖点反常维度（tilted cusp anomalous dimension）控制到所有圈阶。

Result: 该猜想成功预测了 n 点函数到全圈阶的双对数行为，并在对偶振幅描述（dual amplitude description）中复现了等质量极限（equal-mass limit）下大质量振幅（massive amplitudes）预期的小质量渐近行为。

Conclusion: 所提出的猜想为平面 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论中零极限下大电荷关联子的双对数行为提供了一个统一的描述，并建立了与有质量振幅小质量行为的对偶联系。

Abstract: We present a conjecture for the double-logarithmic behavior of the logarithm of large-charge correlators in the null limit in planar $\mathcal{N} = 4$ Super-Yang-Mills theory. Generalizing earlier results for four- and five-point functions, our proposal predicts this behavior for $n$-point functions to all loops in terms of the tilted cusp anomalous dimension. In the dual amplitude description, it reproduces the expected small-mass behavior of massive amplitudes in the equal-mass limit.

</details>


### [39] [Equivariant Interpolations in Topological Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24272)
*Jan Troost*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了P¹和P¹×C²上的等变Gromov-Witten理论，引入与球面和两个平面旋转相关的三个等变参数，探讨等变参数空间中的插值行为。研究发现大等变参数区域由纯拓扑引力主导，小等变参数区域等价于巨正则Hurwitz理论；并进一步提出将全等变对应性嵌入弦理论的方案，同时计算了等变上同调环的结构常数，揭示了其正性和整性性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索P¹和P¹×C²上等变Gromov-Witten理论中等变参数空间的不同区域（包括具有已知全息对偶的特殊点）之间的插值行为，并建立与AdS₃/CFT₂对偶、Hurwitz理论及Kontsevich模型之间的深层联系。

Method: 通过引入三个等变参数（equivariant parameters），分别对应球面旋转和两个平面旋转，在等变Gromov-Witten理论的框架下分析参数空间的插值；利用Jack对称多项式（Jack symmetric polynomials）研究从等变上同调环到普通上同调环的缩放极限，并显式计算结构常数。

Result: 大等变参数区域的理论由两个不动点处的纯拓扑引力（pure topological gravity）主导；小等变参数区域等价于巨正则Hurwitz理论（grand canonical Hurwitz theory）；等变上同调环的结构常数展现出显著的正性和整性（positivity and integrality properties）。

Conclusion: P¹×C²上的等变Gromov-Witten理论与等变平面的对称轨形（symmetric orbifold）之间的全等变对应性可嵌入弦理论；该插值变形为AdS₃/CFT₂对偶模空间中的换位耦合插值提供了一个可解类比。

Abstract: We revisit equivariant Gromov-Witten theories on P1 and on P1 x C2. One can introduce three equivariant parameters associated to rotations of the sphere as well as the two planes. A number of points in the parameter space have known holographic duals. These include the symmetric orbifold point dual to the AdS3 x S3 x C2 string theory at string scale radius of curvature, the grand canonical Hurwitz theory and the product of two Kontsevich models. Within this framework, we discuss interpolations in the equivariant parameters. Firstly, we move between the small and large equivariant parameter regimes in Gromov-Witten theory on P1. At large equivariant parameter, the model is dominated by the pure topological gravity theories at the two fixed points while at small equivariant parameter the theory is equivalent to the grand canonical Hurwitz theory. The deformation is a solvable analogue for the interpolation in the transposition coupling in the moduli space of the AdS3/CFT2 duality. Moreover, we propose that the full equivariant correspondence between the Gromov-Witten theory on P1 x C2 and the symmetric orbifold of the equivariant plane can be embedded in string theory. On the boundary side of that correspondence, we analyze the scaling limit from the equivariant to the ordinary cohomology ring for the Hilbert scheme of points on the plane in terms of Jack symmetric polynomials. We explicitly compute several structure constants of the equivariant cohomology ring and point out their intriguing positivity and integrality properties.

</details>

Abstract: We study dark-sector deformations of holographic anisotropic \(p\)-wave superfluids in hyperscaling-violating black-brane backgrounds. In the visible \(SU(2)\) sector, \(b(u)\) fixes the chemical potential and charge density, while \(ω(u)\) condenses and selects a boundary direction, producing anisotropic strip entanglement. The visible critical chemical potential, radial profiles, condensate branch, and strip-entanglement difference vary with dimension and hyperscaling-violating exponents. We then add hidden gauge sectors and hidden dark-scalar portals. Hidden-current mixing gives a solvable example, whereas isotropic dark sources cancel in the strip difference. It is negative in the \(D=4\) and \(D=5\) backgrounds, so the portal weakly suppresses visible strip anisotropy. This has a holographic RG interpretation: the normalizable dark scalar is weighted toward the IR horizon, while narrow strips probe the UV near-boundary RT region. The Euclidean parent CFT gives a finite wavefunction representation, while the Minkowski parent CFT gives a double-time representation that is unitary in the parent-time polarization. This provides a CFT-based framework for reexamining puzzles of dS and double-time QFT.

Method: 采用协变相空间形式体系，通过微扰方式构造系统的解，从而绕过传统正则量子化中因高阶导数微扰带来的动能结构改变问题，并以一个精确可解的二维非相对论带电粒子模型（磁场和谐振势中的运动，动能视为微扰）为例进行说明。
