Abstract: The standard approach to canonical quantization encounters difficulties in dealing with higher-derivative perturbations that alter the kinetic structure of unperturbed theories. We show that the covariant phase space formalism provides a natural and technically efficient way to circumvent this obstruction. We illustrate the method with an exactly solvable model: a two-dimensional non-relativistic charged particle moving in a magnetic field and a harmonic confining potential, with its kinetic energy viewed as a perturbation. We quantize this model with covariant phase space formalism by constructing the solution perturbatively. We then calculate the energy spectrum and the unequal-time commutators of this system, and obtain the results that agree with the expansion of the exact theory. The procedure developed here is intended to serve as a systematic framework for the canonical quantization of more complex theories with higher-derivative perturbations.

### [44] [Multi-dimensional chaos II: String scattering amplitudes, curve repulsion, and RMT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24490)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入与角度导数零点相关的“面积本征值”（area eigenvalue）$A_n$，计算相邻间隔（spacings）$δ_n$及其比值（ratio）$r_n$；利用间隔比分布拟合随机矩阵理论高斯β系综（RMT Gaussian β-ensembles），并计算“面积形式因子”（areas form factor）以识别混沌特征区域。

Result: 散射角相关曲线收敛于GOE（β=1），极化角相关曲线收敛于GUE（β=2）；面积形式因子呈现下降区（decline）、斜坡区（ramp）和平台区（plateau），且斜坡斜率与间隔比分布提取的β值一致。

Conclusion: 高激发态弦散射振幅在角度参数空间中展现出混沌系统的典型统计普适性，表明弦理论中的散射过程可能蕴含多维混沌（multi-dimensional chaos）行为。

Abstract: Multi-dimensional chaos refers to processes described by erratic functions of several dynamical variables. In this letter we analyze the string scattering amplitudes of highly-excited states and ground states. We show that the amplitudes, which depend on a scattering angle and a polarization angle, are characterized by two sets of non-intersecting curves associated with the vanishing of the derivatives with respect to the angles. We introduce the notion of the "area eigenvalue" $A_n$ associated with the $n$-th curve. We compute the spacings $δ_{n}= A_{n+1}-A_n$ and their ratios $r_{n}=\frac{δ_{n+1}}{δ_n}$. We show that the distributions of the spacing ratios take the form of the RMT Gaussian $β$-ensembles. The curves associated with the scattering angle tend to converge to the Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble value of $β=1$ and those related to the polarization angle to the Gaussian Unitary Ensemble $β=2$. We also compute the ``areas form factor" associated with the areas and discover the regions of decline, ramp and plateau which characterize chaotic processes. The slope of the ramp seems to agree with the $β$ values extracted from the distribution of the spacing ratios.

*A. Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了着色纽结多项式（colored knot polynomials）在双标度准经典（Kashaev）极限下的行为，揭示了量子 A-多项式（quantum A-polynomial）分裂为两部分的相结构，并指出双曲体积在该形式论中仅作为积分常数存在，无法被完全确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用双标度准经典（Kashaev）极限，即表示大小 r ∼ ℏ⁻¹，分析非齐次量子 A-多项式分裂为两个部分的现象，并在除 figure-eight 纽结 4₁ 之外的更多实例上进行验证。

Result: 在双标度准经典极限下存在不同相：一相中经典作用量为零，另一相中经典作用量为双曲体积（纽结补空间在 S³ 中的体积）的形变。非齐次量子 A-多项式分裂为两个部分。双曲体积被视为积分常数，在该形式论中未被完全确定且具有歧义性。经典 A-多项式在 L=1 处与 Alexander 多项式成比例，但非齐次量子 A-多项式的多项式性要求可能使得该 A-多项式不是最小多项式。

Abstract: "Colored" knot polynomials satisfy difference equation w.r.t. the highest weights of the underlying representation -- which in the case of symmetrically colored Jones are named "quantum $A$-polynomials". In the double scaling quasiclassical (Kashaev) limit, when representation size $r\sim \hbar^{-1}$, there are different phases -- in one of them the classical action vanishes and in another one it is a deformation of hyperbolic volume (of a knot complement in $S^3$). This corresponds to a splitting of the non-homogeneous version of the quantum $A$-polynomial into two pieces, which we illustrate by more examples than just a figure-eight knot $4_1$ in the original paper. From the point of view of quasiclassics, hyperbolic volume is just an integration constant, which is not fully determined by the $A$-polynomial equation -- and actually remains ambiguous in this formalism. As a byproduct, we expect that classical $A$-polynomial at $L=1$ becomes proportional to Alexander: $A^{\cal K}(1,M)\sim Δ^{\cal K}(M)$ -- this seems true, but $A$ should be consistent with the polynomiality of {\it non-homogeneous quantum} ${\cal A}$-polynomial, what sometime implies that it is not minimal.

### [47] [Symmetric mass generation of interacting chiral fermions on a one-dimensional lattice without fermion doubling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24713)
*V. A. Zakharov,Atsushi Ueda,Frank Verstraete,C. W. J. Beenakker*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在弦理论（string theory）框架下的 AdS/CFT 对偶中，研究了具有分数化晶格动量（fractional lattice momentum）的算子——即扭量算子（twist operators）——的全息关联函数。通过在 AdS 空间中引入拓扑缺陷（topological defect）来对偶边界上的扭量算子，作者计算了扭量算子的两点、三点和四点关联函数，并推导出算子乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）系数。结果表明，全息计算结果与已知的边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theory, BCFT）结果一致，验证了该构造的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦理论中，D膜（D-branes）上的开弦可以带有分数化的晶格动量，对应弦的世界面（worldsheet）上的扭量算子。然而，这类算子在 AdS/CFT 对偶框架下的全息实现尚不清晰，缺乏一个统一的几何构造来对偶边界上的扭量算子。

Method: 通过在 AdS 空间中引入拓扑缺陷，本文建立了一个内插于两个不同 AdS 边界条件的几何构造，用以对偶边界上的扭量算子。基于此构造，利用 AdS/CFT 的字典计算了扭量算子的两点、三点和四点关联函数，并提取了 OPE 系数。

Result: 计算得到的扭量算子关联函数与边界 BCFT 的结果精确匹配，验证了该拓扑缺陷构造的正确性。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，扭量算子在 AdS/CFT 中的全息对偶是拓扑缺陷，为进一步研究分数化激发的全息性质提供了一个简洁而有效的框架。

Abstract: Symmetric mass generation is the interaction-induced opening of a fermion gap without spontaneous symmetry breaking. The anomaly-free 3-4-5-0 model of Wang and Wen provides a minimal one-dimensional setting for this phenomenon, but a direct lattice realization faces two obstacles: fermion doubling for local chiral discretizations and perturbative irrelevance of the six-fermion gapping interaction. We address both obstacles. First, we formulate the model on a strictly one-dimensional tangent-fermion lattice, where a nonlocal hopping produces a single chiral branch without a mirror partner while retaining an efficient tensor-network representation. Second, we add a Hubbard-type density-density interaction (Luttinger parameter $K$) that reduces the scaling dimension of the 3-4-5-0 interaction from $5$ to $5K$, making it relevant for $K<2/5$. Density-matrix renormalization group calculations show the opening of an excitation gap in this regime without the appearance of a degenerate ground state, the hallmark of symmetric mass generation.

</details>


### [48] [Additional constraints for the tensor bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24859)
*Samuel Laliberte,Reiko Toriumi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨两种新的正定性约束（positivity constraints）变体——基于“开泡”（open bubbles）和基于“颜色矩阵”（color matrices）——并将其用于约束有限 N 下的酉张量积分（unitary tensor integrals），揭示在该极限下对高斯普适性（Gaussian universality）的偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究提出了新的正定性约束（positivity constraints）以约束任意酉张量积分（unitary tensor integrals），但尚缺乏对这些约束变体的系统探索与具体应用效果的分析。

Method: 从泡不变量（bubble invariant）中移除张量或颜色收缩（color contraction），分别构造“开泡”和“颜色矩阵”两种正定性约束变体，并利用它们对有限 N 下的酉张量积分施加约束。

Result: 利用提出的正定性约束，在有限 N 下获得了酉张量积分的尖锐边界（sharp bounds），并探测到该极限下对高斯普适性的偏离。

Conclusion: 两种正定性约束变体可有效约束有限 N 下的酉张量积分，并为非高斯行为（non-Gaussian behavior）的出现提供探测手段。

Abstract: Recently, new positivity constraints were suggested to constrain arbitrary unitary tensor integrals. In the present work, we explore two variants of these positivity constraints: one built from ``open bubbles'', which are tensor-like objects found by removing a tensor from a bubble invariant, and the second built from ``color matrices'', which are matrices found by removing a color contraction from a bubble invariant. Using these positivity constraints, we find sharp bounds on unitary tensor integrals at finite $N$, and probe deviations from Gaussian universality in this limit.

### [49] [Interplay of Holographic and New Agegraphic Dark Energy in Cosmology: A hybrid dark energy model from a generalized length-time cut-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23728)
*Sayani Maity,Aritra Sanyal,Prabir Rudra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 受广义相对论中时空统一性启发，提出一种结合全息暗能量（HDE）和新年代学暗能量（NADE）的混合暗能量模型，通过空间和时间红外截断的混合来定义暗能量密度，分别在空间或时间贡献占主导时退化为HDE或NADE。该模型在与冷暗物质相互作用和非相互作用两种情形下均能成功描述宇宙演化，且哈勃张力显著低于其他模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全息暗能量（Holographic dark energy, HDE）和新年代学暗能量（New Agegraphic dark energy, NADE）模型分别仅基于空间截断或时间截断，但广义相对论（General Relativity）提示时空应该统一。因此，本文提出将空间和时间红外截断（infrared cutoff）结合为一个统一的时空截断，以此构建更完整的暗能量模型。

Method: 将HDE和NADE的能密度线性组合，构建混合暗能量（hybrid dark energy）模型，分别考虑与冷暗物质（cold dark matter）存在相互作用和无相互作用两种情形。通过状态方程参数（equation of state parameter）、减速参数（deceleration parameter）、状态寻找参数（statefinder parameter）和Om诊断（Om-diagnostic）等宇宙学参数研究其宇宙学含义，并使用声速平方（squared speed of sound）进行稳定性检验。利用哈勃数据、重子声学振荡（BAO）数据和暗能量光谱巡天（DESI）数据对模型参数空间进行约束，并评估哈勃张力（Hubble tension）。

Result: 所构建的混合暗能量模型能成功描述宇宙演化。该模型的哈勃张力（Hubble tension）显著低于其他暗能量模型。

Conclusion: 提出的混合暗能量模型结合了空间和时间截断两种思路，在宇宙学描述上具有可行性，且对哈勃张力的缓解效果优于已有模型。

Abstract: The spatial and temporal infrared cutoffs are the source of the Holographic dark energy (HDE) and New Agegraphic dark energy (NADE) models, respectively. Inspired by the spacetime unification of space and time in General Relativity, we propose that a combined spacetime cutoff should govern the dark energy density, with HDE and NADE appearing as limiting cases when the spatial or temporal contribution predominates. In this connection, we explore a hybrid model of holographic and new Agegraphic dark energy, where the energy density of the resulting model is a combination of the two models. We consider an interacting and a non-interacting scenario between the hybrid dark energy model and cold dark matter. Cosmological implications of the model is studied via different cosmological parameters like the equation of state parameter, deceleration parameter, statefinder parameter, and Om-diagnostic. A stability check for the model has been performed using the squared speed of sound. Finally the parameter space of the model is constrained using observational data like Hubble data, BAO data and DESI data. We have also checked the Hubble tension for our hybrid model and found it to be substantially low in comparison to other models. From our analysis we see that the constructed hybrid dark energy model can describe the evolution of the universe successfully.

### [50] [Potentially healthy time evolution in interacting $p$-form fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23731)
*Fethi M. Ramazanoğlu,Kıvanç İ. Ünlütürk*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究 p-形式场（p-form fields）的自相互作用（self-interaction）是否会破坏双曲性（hyperbolicity），发现 3-形式场在 4 维时空中可像矢量场一样保持健康演化，而 2-形式场仍会丧失双曲性；此外指出去除质量项（mass term）并不能真正解决奇异性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究发现，某些自相互作用矢量场在达到有限场强后会丧失健康时间演化，并推广至更高阶形式场。然而，部分矢量场可通过特定自相互作用项避免此问题。本文旨在探究一般 p-形式场是否也存在类似的例外情形。

Method: 在 4 维时空中，分别分析 2-形式场与 3-形式场的自相互作用耦合项对时间演化双曲性的影响，并与已知的矢量场结果进行对比。此外，检验去除质量项这一方案是否真正能解决双曲性丧失问题。

Result: 3-形式场在 4 维时空中类似于矢量场，可以通过特定自相互作用实现健康的时间演化；但 2-形式场的类似耦合仍会导致双曲性丧失。去除质量项虽是一种提案，但会将奇异性转移至运动方程的其他部分，因此大概率无法提供适定（well-posed）的时间演化。

Conclusion: 不同阶数的 p-形式场对自相互作用的响应存在本质差异，3-形式场可避免双曲性丧失而 2-形式场不能；去除质量项并非解决该问题的有效途径。研究还指出了未来推广这些发现的方向。

Abstract: It was recently discovered that many self-interacting vector fields can have healthy time evolution when field amplitudes are small, however, further dynamics becomes impossible if the norm of the field reaches a certain finite value. This result was also generalized to higher form fields using the fact that vector fields can also be viewed as 1-form fields. However, other recent work demonstrated that some exceptional vector field theories do not suffer from such problems if the self-interaction term is chosen in a specific way. Here, we study whether a similar exception exists for $p$-form fields in general. We show that, in 4 spacetime dimensions, 3-form fields with self interaction can indeed have healthy time evolution similarly to vectors. However, the analogous coupling terms still lead to loss of hyperbolicity for 2-form fields. We study the reasons for these differences, and comment on directions to generalize our findings. We also demonstrate that eliminating the mass term, one of the proposals to build healthy self-interacting vector field theories, moves the singularity to other parts of the equations of motion, hence, most likely does not provide well-posed time evolution.

</details>


### [51] [Removing Ostrogradsky modes in multi-field higher-order scalar-tensor theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23734)
*Hamed Bouzari Nezhad*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了多场高阶标量-张量理论（multi-field higher-order scalar-tensor theories）中如何消除奥斯特罗格拉茨基模式（Ostrogradsky modes）。通过ADM分解（ADM decomposition）和哈密顿分析（Hamiltonian analysis），推导出主退化条件（primary degeneracy condition）和额外一致性条件，确保理论仅传播2+N个自由度（degrees of freedom），包括两个引力张量模式和每个场一个标量模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶标量-张量理论中通常存在不稳定的奥斯特罗格拉茨基鬼模式（Ostrogradsky ghost），需要系统的方法来识别并排除这些非物理自由度。现有研究多聚焦于单场情形，多场理论中退化条件（degeneracy condition）的结构尚未被充分理解。

Method: 针对具有任意数量N个标量场、对二阶导数具有二次依赖性的广义理论类别，执行ADM分解并发展哈密顿分析，限定在度规动力学块（metric kinetic block）可逆的分支。推导场空间中的主退化条件矩阵形式，并进一步分析约束代数（constraint algebra）以获得额外的反对称一致性条件。

Result: 主退化条件在多场理论中并不充分，需辅以约束传播过程中产生的一致性条件（consistency conditions），其中部分在场空间指标下是反对称的，在单场情形中没有直接类似物。主退化条件、一致性条件及约束代数的最终秩条件（rank condition）共同确保理论传播2+N个自由度，无额外奥斯特罗格拉茨基模式。

Conclusion: 该退化框架在单场极限、多场二次霍恩德斯基型子类（quadratic Horndeski-type subclass）以及一个显式简并的多场子类中得到了验证，表明所提出的条件可以满足。

Abstract: We study multi-field higher-order scalar-tensor theories and examine how the unwanted Ostrogradsky modes can be removed. For a general class of theories with an arbitrary number $\mathcal{N}$ of scalar fields and quadratic dependence on their second derivatives, we perform an ADM decomposition and develop the Hamiltonian analysis in the branch where the metric kinetic block is invertible. The primary degeneracy condition takes the form of a matrix condition in field space, but in a genuine multi-field theory it is not by itself sufficient: preserving the primary degeneracy constraints generates additional consistency conditions, some of which are antisymmetric in the field-space indices and have no direct analogue in the single-field case. Together with the primary degeneracy condition and a final rank condition on the constraint algebra, these conditions are sufficient for the theory to propagate $2+\mathcal{N}$ degrees of freedom, the two tensor modes of gravity together with one scalar mode per field, and no additional Ostrogradsky mode. We illustrate the construction in the single-field limit, in a multi-field quadratic Horndeski-type subclass, and in an explicit degenerate multi-field subclass that shows these conditions can be satisfied.

</details>


### [52] [Physical properties of charged black holes from the nonlinear electrodynamics model based on electric potential regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23746)
*S. Habib Mazharimousavi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦引力与非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics, NED）最小耦合下生成的静态球对称黑洞解，发现其因果结构、热力学性质和观测特征随参数（质量M、电荷Q、非线性标度r₀）变化而显著丰富，包括单/双/三视界、热稳定相变以及阴影偏离Reissner-Nordström几何等结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性电动力学（NED）对带电黑洞因果结构、热力学相空间和动力学响应的影响，揭示其相较于标准Reissner-Nordström黑洞的新特征与可观测偏离。

Method: 采用由点电荷正则化电势构造的非线性电动力学（NED）模型，与爱因斯坦引力最小耦合，求解静态球对称黑洞解；通过分析Horizon结构、中心奇点性质、Hawking温度与热容（heat capacity）推导热力学行为，并利用零测地线（null geodesics）与黑洞阴影（black hole shadows）研究观测特征。

Result: 解由ADM质量M、电荷Q和非线性标度r₀三个参数刻画，展现出包含单视界、双视界、三视界及裸奇点几何的丰富因果结构；中心奇点性质由组合量 m - (2/3)q² 决定，可呈类空或类时奇点。热力学分析发现两个临界电荷参数：低于临界电荷时黑洞热不稳定，高于临界电荷则在Davies点界定的有限视界半径范围内出现稳定相；电荷足够大时，极端构型（温度为零）进一步约束稳定区域。观测方面，非线性电动力学修正使黑洞阴影相对于Reissner-Nordström几何产生显著偏离，且超过临界电荷后光子球（photon sphere）可能消失。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学（NED）显著丰富了带电黑洞的因果结构、热力学相空间和动力学响应，提供了可观测的偏离标准Reissner-Nordström范式的特征。

Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric black hole solutions arising from Einstein gravity minimally coupled to a nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) model constructed from a regularized electric potential of a point charge. The resulting spacetime is characterized by three parameters, namely, the ADM mass $% M $, the electric charge $Q$, and the nonlinear scale $r_{0}$. We show that, depending on the values of $M$ and $Q$, the solutions exhibit a rich causal structure comprising black holes with single, double, and triple horizons, as well as naked singular geometries. The nature of the central singularity is determined by the combination $m-\frac{2}{3}q^{2}$, allowing for both spacelike and timelike singularities. We perform a detailed thermodynamic analysis by deriving the Hawking temperature and heat capacity, revealing the existence of two critical charge parameters that govern the thermal behavior. Below a critical charge, the black holes are thermally unstable, whereas above it a stable phase emerges within a finite range of horizon radii bounded by Davies points. For sufficiently large charge, extremal configurations with vanishing temperature arise, further constraining the stability region. We also investigate observational signatures by analyzing null geodesics and black hole shadows, showing that nonlinear electrodynamics corrections lead to noticeable deviations from the Reissner-Nordström geometry, including the possible absence of a photon sphere beyond a critical charge. Our results highlight that nonlinear electrodynamics significantly enriches the causal structure, thermodynamic phase space, and dynamical response of charged black holes, providing potentially observable deviations from the Reissner-Nordström paradigm.

</details>

*Aheibam Boycha Meitei,Yenshembam Priyobarta Singh,T. Ibungochouba Singh,Irom Ablu Meitei,Kangujam Yugindro Singh*

TL;DR: 本文研究了扩展广义不确定性原理（EGUP）对 Kerr-Newman 黑洞在精质（quintessence）环境下的热力学量的影响，并与广义不确定性原理（GUP）和扩展不确定性原理（EUP）的结果进行了比较分析，涵盖了霍金温度、热容、吉布斯自由能、熵和压强等热力学量，以及黑洞剩余质量、温度和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在精质环境下的 Kerr-Newman 黑洞（KNBHQ）框架中，分别引入广义不确定性原理（GUP）、扩展不确定性原理（EUP）以及扩展广义不确定性原理（EGUP），推导并比较霍金温度、热容、吉布斯自由能、熵和压强等热力学量。

Result: 在 GUP（适用于早期宇宙）和 EUP（适用于晚期宇宙）以及 EGUP 的共同作用下，KNBHQ 的霍金温度、热容、吉布斯自由能、熵和压强在从早期宇宙到晚期的演化过程中表现出显著差异；同时获得了黑洞的剩余质量、剩余温度及其稳定性条件。

Conclusion: EGUP 能够统一描述 GUP 和 EUP 在不同宇宙阶段的效应，精质作为暗能量模型对 Kerr-Newman 黑洞热力学演化具有重要影响，且黑洞剩余性质（质量、温度）与稳定性受不确定性原理的具体形式调制。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the effects of the Extended Generalized Uncertainty Principle (EGUP) on the thermodynamic quantities of the Kerr-Newman black hole surrounded by quintessence (KNBHQ). Additionally, we conduct a comparative analysis of the outcomes derived from the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP) and the Extended Uncertainty Principle (EUP). The GUP is crucial in the context of the early universe, whereas the EUP is significant in the framework of the later universe. This analysis illustrates the variations in thermodynamic quantities, including Hawking temperature, heat capacity, Gibbs free energy, entropy and pressure of the Kerr-Newman black hole, as they evolve from the early universe to the latter universe under the influence of the dark energy model known as quintessence. The remnant mass, temperature and the stability of the KNBHQ are also studied.

### [54] [New Rotating Black Hole in Electromagnetic Fields: Cosmological Horizon without Cosmological Constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23782)
*Liang Ma,H. Lu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦引力（Einstein-Maxwell gravity）中发现了一种全新的电真空（electrovacuum）时空背景，其宇宙学视界（cosmological horizon）完全由电磁场支撑，而非依赖正宇宙常数（cosmological constant）或暗能量（dark energy）。在此基础上，构建了描述该背景中克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）的精确解，分析了包括视界和奇点在内的整体结构，并推导了黑洞热力学第一定律（first law of black hole thermodynamics）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过求解爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦场方程（Einstein-Maxwell field equations），获得新的电真空背景时空及其精确解；进而构建该背景中包含克尔黑洞的复合精确解，并分析其全局结构（包括视界和奇点），推导热力学第一定律。

Result: 得到了一类全新的电真空及相关的背景时空，其宇宙学视界完全由电磁场支撑；构造了该背景中克尔黑洞的精确解；获得了该系统的全局结构特征和黑洞热力学第一定律。

Conclusion: 纯电磁场即可支撑宇宙学视界，无需依赖正宇宙常数或暗能量，这一发现为探索黑洞与晚期宇宙学相关的宇宙学及天体物理现象提供了潜在的新方向。

Abstract: We obtain a new electrovacuum and related background spacetime that contains a cosmological horizon supported entirely by the electromagnetic field. We further construct an exact solution describing a Kerr black hole in this background. We study the global structure including horizons and singularities, and derive the first law of black hole thermodynamics. The emergence of a cosmological horizon in Einstein-Maxwell gravity without invoking a positive cosmological constant or dark energy is tantalizing, and may provide a new avenue for exploring cosmological and astrophysical phenomena related to black holes and the late-time cosmology.

### [55] [Black Hole Ringdown Nonlinearities in the Large-D Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23804)
*Roberto Emparan,Amanda Green-Salinas,David Pereñiguez,Jaime Redondo-Yuste*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在大维度极限（large-D limit）下利用黑洞动力学有效理论，首次系统研究了黑洞合并环降阶段（ringdown phase）的非线性效应，推导了静态黑洞受单一准正则模（quasinormal mode）驱动的三阶响应解析表达式，并将其应用于无自旋黑洞对头碰撞的环降分析。结果表明，纳入二次和三次非线性修正可将准正则模建模的精度提升若干个数量级，且非线性效应的强度随碰撞速度增加而显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞合并的环降阶段通常采用准正则模式（quasinormal modes）的线性理论描述，但非线性效应在高速碰撞等强场过程中可能变得显著。现有方法在分析非线性贡献时面临解析复杂和数值昂贵等困难。本文旨在利用大维度极限下的黑洞有效理论，提供一个解析可处理、数值高效且信号提取清晰的框架，以系统研究环降阶段非线性修正的作用。

Method: 采用大维度极限（large-D limit）下的黑洞动力学有效理论（effective theory of black hole dynamics），推导了静态黑洞受单一准正则模（quasinormal mode）驱动的三阶（third-order）非线性响应解析表达式。将该解析结果应用于无自旋（non-spinning）黑洞头对碰撞（head-on collisions）的环降信号分析，覆盖不同碰撞速度和质量比参数。

Result: 纳入非线性效应至二次（quadratic）和三次（cubic）阶后，准正则模建模描述黑洞弛豫（black hole relaxation）的精度提升了数个数量级。非线性效应的强度随碰撞速度增大而显著增长。

Conclusion: 黑洞合并环降阶段的非线性效应不可忽视，引入高阶非线性修正可显著提升准正则模建模的准确性；非线性强度随碰撞速度增加而增强，表明高速碰撞场景下非线性效应尤为关键。大维度有效理论为研究此类非线性问题提供了可控且高效的理论工具。

Abstract: We initiate the study of nonlinear effects in the ringdown phase of black hole mergers using the effective theory of black hole dynamics in the large-D limit. This framework offers several advantages: the quasinormal mode spectrum, including nonlinear corrections, is analytically tractable; numerical simulations of collisions are computationally inexpensive; and the extraction and analysis of the ringdown signal are clean and controlled. As a proof of concept, we derive analytic expressions for the third-order response of a static black hole driven by a single quasinormal mode, and apply them to study the ringdown following head-on collisions of non-spinning black holes across a range of velocities and mass ratios. We find that including nonlinear effects, up to quadratic and cubic order, improves the accuracy of quasinormal-mode modelling of black hole relaxation by several orders of magnitude. The results also show a clear growth in the strength of nonlinear effects as the collision velocity increases.

</details>


### [56] [A thorough investigation of cross-correlation estimators for stochastic gravitational-wave background searches in ground-based detector data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23816)
*Haowen Zhong,Joseph D. Romano,Vuk Mandic,Shivaraj Kandhasamy,Arianna I. Renzini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统性地重新审视并严格重新推导了频域交叉相关方法（cross-correlation method in the frequency domain），解决了时域加窗与数据重叠导致的非零协方差问题，提出了新的窄带估计量（narrowband estimator）表达式，并证明此前广泛使用的表达式在参数估计和模型选择中仍然产生正确结果。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究从时域出发，系统性地重新审视并严格重新表述频域中的交叉相关方法，明确指出并解决了时域中由加窗（windowing）和数据重叠（overlapping）引发的非零协方差问题。基于这一理论框架，推导出窄带估计量及其协方差的新表达式。

Result: 给出了与以往搜索所用表达式不同的窄带估计量及其协方差的新表达式。同时证明，尽管存在差异，此前领域内广泛使用的表达式在参数估计中仍能产生正确的后验分布（posterior distribution），在模型选择中仍能产生正确的对数贝叶斯因子（log-Bayes factor）。

Conclusion: 通过建立稳健的理论框架，本研究有助于对随机引力波背景观测进行更准确且具有物理洞察意义的解释，为当前及未来的相关研究奠定了必要的基础。

Abstract: Detecting a stochastic gravitational-wave background represents a crucial yet challenging objective within the field of gravitational-wave astronomy. Ground-based detectors currently rely almost exclusively on cross-correlation methods to detect stochastic gravitational-wave background signals. Traditionally, these methods define and optimize a broadband estimator initially constructed in the time domain. However, a growing number of analyses require precise narrowband estimators to accurately characterize the energy density of the underlying signal in specific frequency bins. Transitioning from time-domain broadband estimators to frequency-domain narrowband estimators introduces significant complexities that have not yet been fully explored in the existing literature. In this study, we systematically revisit and rigorously reformulate the cross-correlation method in the frequency domain, explicitly addressing and resolving issues related to non-zero covariances induced by windowing and overlapping of data in the time domain. We provide new expressions for the narrowband estimators and their covariances, which differ from those used in past searches. Fortunately, we show that the expressions that have been widely used in the field nonetheless lead to correct posterior distributions for parameter estimation and correct log-Bayes factors for model selection. By establishing a robust theoretical framework, our work facilitates more accurate and physically insightful interpretations of stochastic gravitational-wave background observations, laying an essential foundation for current and future research in this field.

### [57] [Primordial Black Holes: A Review of Formation and Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23846)

Abstract: Primordial Black Holes (PBHs) have emerged as a leading non-particulate candidate for dark matter and a unique cosmological probe, a paradigm shift accelerated by the detection of anomalous binary mergers by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) collaboration. While the literature is rich with phenomenological constraints, the fundamental quantum and relativistic underpinnings governing PBH genesis and evolution often receive comparatively less emphasis. This review aims to bridge that gap by systematically detailing the physics of PBH formation and their subsequent evolutionary trajectory. We critically examine the hydrodynamic complexity of the early universe, establishing the relativistic thresholds for collapse, the non-linear race against sound in the primordial plasma, and the rigorous mathematical utility of the compaction function. Furthermore, by incorporating the dynamic nature of FLRW backgrounds, higher curvature corrections, and quantum backreaction via the memory burden effect, we challenge the standard hawking evaporation and show that extreme-curvature environments halt evaporation entirely, leaving Planck-scale relics that evade current extragalactic bounds. Finally, we map the multimessenger observational landscape, highlighting how the imminent search for sub-solar mass inspirals by next-generation gravitational wave observatories -- such as the Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer -- could yield smoking-gun evidence for the PBH paradigm, ultimately transforming these primordial relics into unparalleled laboratories for high-energy physics.

### [58] [Energy Extraction via Magnetic Reconnection from a Rotating Dyonic Black Hole in $N = 2, \ U(1)^2$ Gauged Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23862)
*Raid M Suleiman,Shanshan Rodriguez,Dominic O. Chang,Leo Rodriguez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于 Comisso-Asenjo 机制，在四维 $N=2$, $U(1)^2$ 规范超引力框架下，研究了旋转带磁黑洞（dyonic black hole）通过磁重联（magnetic reconnection）提取能量的过程，系统分析了自旋、电荷、NUT 参数与规范耦合等参数对能量提取效率的影响，发现存在非单调的自旋依赖关系，且在中等自旋和中等电荷条件下可实现高效能量提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在更广义的引力理论（四维 $N=2$, $U(1)^2$ 规范超引力）中，旋转带磁黑洞能否通过磁重联机制提取能量，并系统分析各类参数（自旋、电磁荷、NUT 参数、规范耦合）对能量提取可行性和效率的影响。

Method: 采用 Comisso-Asenjo 机制，在零角动量观测者（ZAMO frame）参考系中推导渐近流体力学单位焓能量 $ε^{\infty}_\pm$，通过改变黑洞自旋 $a$、电磁荷、NUT 参数 $N_g$ 以及规范耦合 $g$，计算截止磁化强度 $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$，并绘制允许 $ε^{\infty}_-<0$（负能量重联流出）的参数空间区域。

Result: 截止磁化强度 $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ 和 Comisso-Asenjo 能量提取的存在性受 $g$ 和带磁电荷强度的严格控制；增大 $g$ 或使电荷趋于极值会提高 $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ 并缩小 CA 活动区域（ergoregion 中的有效部分）。与 Kerr 黑洞不同，自旋 $a$ 通过归一化因子 $Ξ$ 和四阶视界函数 $Δ_g$ 间接起作用，AdS/NUT 变形产生的几何效应主导了传统的参考系拖拽增强效应。提取功率和效率关于 $a$ 呈非单调变化，在 $a\sim0.8$ 的中等自旋处达到峰值。

Conclusion: 近极值自旋并非实现高效能量提取的必要条件；在 $g$ 较小且 $Q$ 适中的参数条件下，中等自旋即可获得高效率。高效提取还要求极高的磁化强度和近乎径向的重联流出，从而将活动重联层限制在视界外的一个薄壳区域内。

Abstract: We study energy extraction via magnetic reconnection from a rotating dyonic black hole in four-dimensional $N=2$, $U(1)^2$ gauged supergravity. Using the Comisso-Asenjo mechanism in the ZAMO frame, we derive the asymptotic hydrodynamic energy per unit enthalpy $ε^{\infty}_\pm$ and determine when reconnection outflows attained negative energy at infinity. By varying the spin $a$, electric and magnetic charges, NUT parameter $N_g$, and gauge coupling $g$, we compute the cutoff magnetization $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ and map the region of parameter space that admits $ε^{\infty}_-<0$. We find that $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ and the very existence of Comisso-Asenjo extraction are tightly controlled by $g$ and the dyonic charges: increasing $g$ or pushing the charges toward extremality raises $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ and shrinks the CA-active part of the ergoregion. Unlike Kerr, the spin enters through the normalization factor $Ξ$, and the quartic horizon function $Δ_g$, so geometric effects from the AdS/NUT deformation dominate the usual frame-dragging enhancement. As a result, the extracted power and efficiency are non-monotonic in $a$ and peak at intermediate spin ($a\sim0.8$); near-extremal rotation is not required for high efficiency, provided $g$ is small and $Q$ is moderate. Efficient extraction further demands extreme magnetization and nearly radial outflows, confining the active reconnection layer to a thin shell, just outside the horizon.

### [59] [Newtonian Shirokov Effect: Epicyclic Frequency Splitting from Mass Multipoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23912)
*Anuar Idrissov,Kuantay Boshkayev,Abylaikhan Tlemissov,Hernando Quevedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文分析了轴对称牛顿势中近圆轨道的小振动，发现了多极矩（multipole）频率分裂的选择定则：除偶极子（dipole）外，所有多极矩均会分裂径向与垂直本征频率；偶极子可被质心重新定义吸收，不产生坐标无关的频率分裂。该研究提供了分别测量扁率 J₂ 和质心偏移 r_CM 的两种互补探针，并给出了太阳系内的数值估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将相对论性希罗科夫效应（Shirokov effect）——即近圆轨道在引力场中径向与垂直本征频率的分裂——推广到经典极限，系统考察牛顿多极势中轨道小振动的完整图景，并澄清多极矩分裂频率的选择定则。

Method: 在轴对称牛顿势的质量多极展开中，计算有效势在真实（可能倾斜的）平衡位置处的完整黑塞矩阵（Hessian），并精确求解耦合的双模振子系统，得到径向与垂直本征频率的解析表达式。通过直接轨道积分验证理论结果。

Result: (i) 四极矩（quadrupole）在 J₂ 一阶下分裂径向与垂直本征频率：Ω_θ²−Ω_r²=−3GQ/r₀⁵=6GMJ₂R²/r₀⁵，等价于经典天体力学中扁率体的拱点进动率与交点进动率之差；(ii) 引力偶极子不产生频率分裂，其等于 M r_CM，可通过重新归心于质心消除，真实倾斜平衡下的一阶耦合项被抵消；(iii) 真正的八极矩（octupole）同样分裂频率：ω₊²−ω₋²≈6G|O|/r₀⁶。选择定则并非基于奇偶宇称：除偶极子外，所有多极矩均分裂频率。

Conclusion: 频率分裂可用于测量源的天体扁率 J₂，轨道平面倾斜 δθ₀≈−r_CM/r₀ 则用于测量质心偏移 r_CM，后者是一个轨道几何可观测量而非频率可观测量。四极矩效应在希罗科夫原始可观测——n 圈轨道后的长期横向漂移——中给出 ξ^θ=ξ₀^θ πn (6J₂R²/r₀²)，在 1 au 处约为 10⁻⁸ cm，在 0.1 au 附近约为 10⁻⁶ cm，与希罗科夫的史瓦西估计相当。

Abstract: We analyze small oscillations of nearly circular orbits in an axisymmetric Newtonian potential expanded in mass multipoles, as the classical counterpart of the relativistic Shirokov effect. Computing the full Hessian of the effective potential at the true (possibly tilted) equilibrium and solving the coupled two-mode oscillator exactly, we obtain a complete picture. (i) A quadrupole splits the radial and vertical epicyclic frequencies, $Ω_θ^2-Ω_r^2=-3GQ/r_0^5=6GMJ_2R^2/r_0^5$, at first order in $J_2$; the Newtonian analogue of the Shirokov splitting, equivalent to the classical statement that an oblate body's apsidal and nodal rates differ. (ii) A gravitational dipole produces no splitting: it equals $M r_{\rm CM}$, is removable by re-centering at the center of mass, and cannot appear in any coordinate-independent frequency; the apparent first-order coupling cancels at the true tilted equilibrium, any residual absorbed by the induced quadrupole of the shifted source, confirmed by direct orbit integration. (iii) A genuine octupole does split the frequencies, $ω_+^2-ω_-^2\approx6G|O|/r_0^6$. The selection rule is thus not even/odd parity: every multipole splits the frequencies except the dipole. These yield two complementary probes of an axisymmetric source: the frequency splitting measures the oblateness $J_2$, while the orbital-plane tilt, $δθ_0\simeq-r_{\rm CM}/r_0$, measures the center-of-mass offset $r_{\rm CM}$, an orbital-geometry observable rather than a frequency one. We give solar-system estimates for both. Carried through to Shirokov's original observable -- the secular transverse drift after $n$ orbits -- the quadrupole effect gives $ξ^θ=ξ_0^θ\,πn\,(6J_2R^2/r_0^2)$, of order $10^{-8}$ cm at $1$ au and $\sim10^{-6}$ cm near $0.1$ au, comparable to Shirokov's Schwarzschild estimate.

</details>


### [60] [Nonrotating and rotating black holes with secondary disformal hair in a ghost-free metric-affine parity-violating scalar-torsion theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24041)
*E. Brito,G. Macedo,J. R. Nascimento,A. Yu. Petrov,P. J. Porfírio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个无鬼影的度规-仿射标量-挠率模型，其中赝标量场与Nieh-Yan密度耦合，并与Einstein-Palatini张量进行导数耦合。理论具有射影不变性，在平移对称扇区中仅依赖于标量的梯度。通过求解独立联络，发现其对称部分是与度规$h_{μν}$关联的Levi-Civita联络（$h_{μν}$与$g_{μν}$呈变形对应），而反对称部分为由$v_μ=\partial_μ\vartheta$源出的纯轴挠率。识别出一个无鬼影的退化分支$α=6β^2κ^2$，在该分支下$h$-度规框架中的Ricci平坦几何满足度规方程且Noether流恒为零。以Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞为例，在$h$-度规框架中构建了静态和类Babichev-Charmousis的含时标量场分布，并分析了视界正则性；在Kerr情形下给出了稳态未来正则的标量场分布，揭示了在$g$-度规框架中的变形修正属于次级变形标量毛而非初级Noether荷毛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力理论中，标量-挠率耦合模型常面临鬼影（ghost）不稳定性问题，且如何在不引入额外自由度的情况下构造自洽的射影不变（projectively invariant）模型尚待探索。本文旨在构建一个无鬼影的度规-仿射标量-挠率模型，并研究其黑洞解中标量场的行为与毛发的性质。

Method: 该模型将赝标量场（pseudoscalar field）与Nieh-Yan密度（Nieh-Yan density）耦合，并与Einstein-Palatini张量进行导数耦合。通过射影规范固定（projective gauge fixing），精确求解独立联络：对称部分为与$h_{μν}$关联的Levi-Civita联络，反对称部分为纯轴挠率。识别了无鬼影退化分支$α=6β^2κ^2$，并在该分支下以Schwarzschild和Kerr度规为背景求解标量场分布。

Result: 在退化分支下，Ricci平坦的$h$-度规框架几何自动满足度规方程，Noether流恒为零。Schwarzschild背景下得到了静态和类Babichev-Charmousis含时标量场解，并验证了Eddington-Finkelstein坐标下的视界正则性。Kerr背景下，定标量场分布是轴对称的且依赖于径向和角坐标；在$g$-度规框架中标量场产生变形修正（disformal corrections），表现为次级变形标量毛（secondary disformal scalar hair）而非初级Noether荷毛（primary Noether-charge hair）。

Conclusion: 该无鬼影模型为标量-挠率耦合引力提供了一类自洽的理论框架，其退化分支中的黑洞解仅携带次级变形标量毛。这揭示了在射影不变理论中，标量毛发的起源可能来自度规变形而非守恒荷，为区分不同类型标量毛的物理意义提供了新见解。

Abstract: In this paper, we formulate a ghost-free metric-affine scalar-torsion model in which a pseudoscalar field is coupled to the Nieh--Yan density and derivatively coupled to the Einstein-Palatini tensor. The theory is projectively invariant and, in the shift-symmetric sector, depends on the scalar only through its gradient. After fixing the projective gauge, the independent connection is solved exactly: its symmetric part is the Levi-Civita connection associated with the metric \(h_{μν}\), disformally related to the metric $g_{μν}$, while its antisymmetric part is a purely axial torsion sourced by $v_μ=\partial_μ\vartheta$. We identify a degenerate ghost-free branch, $α=6β^2κ^2$, for which Ricci-flat geometries in the $h$-metric frame solve the metric equations and the Noether current vanishes identically. For example, we consider Schwarzschild and Kerr geometries in the $h$-metric frame, which generate disformal deformations on these geometries from the perspective of the $g$-metric frame. For the Schwarzschild black hole in the $h$-metric frame, we construct static and Babichev--Charmousis-like time-dependent scalar profiles, and discuss horizon regularity in Eddington--Finkelstein coordinates. For the Kerr black hole in the $h$-metric frame, we show that the fixed-norm scalar profile is generically axisymmetric, depending on both the radial and angular coordinates, and we construct a stationary future-regular profile in ingoing Kerr coordinates. The Kerr solution with the nontrivial scalar field is stealth only in the $h$-metric frame. In the $g$-metric frame, it produces disformal corrections stemming from the nontrivial scalar field profile and it represents secondary disformal scalar hair rather than primary Noether-charge hair.

</details>


### [61] [Nanohertz gravitational waves from domain walls nucleated during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24070)
*Zhi-Yong Huang,Tie-Jun Gao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由宇宙暴胀期间经量子隧穿成核的畴壁（domain walls, DWs）产生的标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves, SIGWs），发现有限成核持续时间能增强曲率扰动，从而在纳赫兹频段产生与脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）观测信号（NANOGrav和EPTA）匹配的引力波背景，并预言了可被其他探测器检验的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解释脉冲星计时阵列合作组报告的纳赫兹随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background, SGWB）的起源，并突破传统瞬时成核框架下曲率功率谱过弱、无法产生足够强度信号的局限。

Method: 构建了一个两场暴胀模型（two-field inflation model），包含暴胀子（inflaton）φ和旁观场（spectator field）χ，二者通过势能V(φ,χ)耦合，使得畴壁张力σ(t)随暴胀子经过临界值而平滑演化。通过引入有限成核持续时间，得到畴壁半径分布参数γ≡\overline{R^4}/(\overline{R^2})^2>1，从而增强曲率扰动，并由过渡特征宽度确定曲率功率谱的截断尺度k_{\text{cut}}。

Result: 在三个代表参数集下计算了标量诱导引力波谱，发现其纳赫兹峰值谱与NANOGrav和EPTA信号吻合。通过选择不同参数，模型还同时预言了可被其他引力波探测器观测到的潜在信号。

Conclusion: 有限成核持续时间的畴壁机制能够有效增强曲率扰动，为脉冲星计时阵列观测到的纳米赫兹引力波背景提供合理解释，并具备可被多波段引力波实验检验的预测能力。

Abstract: We investigate scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) produced by domain walls (DWs) nucleated via quantum tunneling during inflation with an extended nucleation time. In contrast to the small-period nucleation framework, where DWs form instantaneously and produce a curvature power spectrum too weak to account for the nanohertz stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) reported by pulsar timing array (PTA) collaborations, we show that a finite nucleation duration leads to a distribution of DW radii characterized by $γ\equiv\overline{R^4}/(\overline{R^2})^2>1$, which enhances the resulting curvature perturbations. We construct a two-field inflation model with an inflaton $φ$ and a spectator field $χ$ coupled through the potential $V(φ,χ)$, where the DW tension $σ(t)$ evolves smoothly as the inflaton rolls past a critical value. The characteristic width of this transition determines the cutoff scale $k_{\text{cut}}$ of the curvature power spectrum, enabling the SIGW peak to be placed in the nanohertz frequency band with detectable amplitude. For three representative parameter sets, we compute the SIGW spectra and find that the nanohertz-peaked spectrum matching the NANOGrav and EPTA signals. By selecting different parameters, our model simultaneously predicts potentially observable signals at other gravitational-wave detectors.

</details>


### [62] [Nonlinear Stability of Kerr-Sen Black Holes in Merging Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24215)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-轴子理论（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton-axion theory）中Kerr-Sen黑洞（Kerr-Sen black holes）的稳定性，以及探索在标量背景中黑洞是否会在动力学演化过程中获得标量毛发（scalar hair）。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical relativity）框架，对头对并合双黑洞（head-on binary black hole）进行模拟，使用近似初值（approximate initial data）并扫描参数空间的一部分区域。

Result: 非零电荷下，标量场在并合后持续存在；存在自旋时，并合残留物（remnant）保留轴子场；初始未标量化的黑洞在标量背景中会获得并保持标量毛发；甚至初始未标量化的Kerr-Newman黑洞（Kerr-Newman black holes）也会在演化中标量化（scalarize）并维持标量化状态。

Conclusion: Kerr-Sen黑洞在该替代引力理论（alternative gravity theory）中表现出稳定性；在标量背景中，黑洞能够获得并保持标量毛发，表明标量化是动力学稳定的过程。

Abstract: We investigate the stability of Kerr-Sen black holes, which arise in Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton-axion theory. Within a numerical relativity framework, we perform head-on binary black hole simulations with approximate initial data across a portion of the parameter space. We find that for nontrivial electric charge, a dilaton field persists through merger and that in the presence of spin, the remnant will also retain an axion field. The persistence of these fields for long times after merger strongly suggests the stability of these black holes within this alternative gravity theory. We further test whether initially unscalarized black holes will acquire hair in the presence of a scalar background. We find that black holes immersed in such a background retain scalar hair. Furthermore, we find that even initially unscalarized Kerr-Newman black holes will scalarize and remain scalarized throughout the evolution.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索修正引力理论中旋转黑洞的天体物理可观测效应，并检验Kerr-MOG时空能否与现有恒星级黑洞候选体的观测数据自洽。

Method: 采用Kerr-MOG度规描述旋转黑洞，利用Novikov-Thorne吸积盘模型分析辐射效率，并基于Blandford-Znajek机制计算相对论性喷流功率；结合连续谱拟合法（continuum-fitting method）的观测辐射效率估计，以及瞬态喷流能量学（transient jet energetics）观测数据，对每个源在(a, α)参数空间进行约束。

Result: 辐射效率与喷流功率的联合约束在多个源中显示出显著的重叠区域；对于高自旋源GRS1915+105，兼容性仅出现在较窄的Kerr-MOG参数范围内。

Conclusion: Kerr-MOG时空能够为多个黑洞X射线双星的观测性质提供一个可行的理论解释框架。

Abstract: We investigate the astrophysical implications of rotating black holes in modified gravity by studying the Kerr-MOG spacetime and applying it to several stellar-mass black hole candidates: A0620-00, H1743-322, XTE J1550-564, GRS1124-683, GRO J1655-40, and GRS1915+105. The Kerr-MOG geometry is characterized by the black hole mass, the spin parameter $a$, and the modified gravity parameter $α$. We analyze how the presence of the MOG parameter modifies the spacetime structure and the location of the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). Within the Novikov--Thorne accretion disk model, we show that $α$ significantly affects the radiative efficiency of accretion disks and introduces a degeneracy between the spin and the modified gravity parameter. Using observational estimates of radiative efficiencies inferred from the continuum-fitting method, we constrain the allowed regions in the $(a,α)$ parameter space for each source. We further examine the relativistic jet power using the Blandford--Znajek mechanism and compare the theoretical predictions with the observed transient jet energetics, considering two representative jet Lorentz factors, $Γ=2$ and $Γ=5$. By combining the constraints from the radiative efficiency and jet power, we identify regions where both observables can be simultaneously reproduced. For several sources significant overlap regions appear, while for the highly spinning source GRS1915+105 the compatibility occurs only within a narrow range of Kerr--MOG parameters. These results suggest that the Kerr--MOG spacetime can provide a viable framework for interpreting the observed properties of several black hole X-ray binaries.

### [64] [Thin accretion disks around a Schwarzschild acoustic black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24315)
*R. M. Yusupova,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在Novikov-Thorne框架下研究了围绕Schwarzschild声学黑洞的薄吸积盘性质。声学黑洞由一个非零背景流体四速度参数ξ刻画，研究显示盘在两个不同ξ区间表现出增强或减弱辐射特征的两种机制，其中边际稳定轨道半径在ξ≈2.8处的分支转变导致通量、温度和光度轮廓的显著改变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过Novikov-Thorne框架系统研究Schwarzschild声学黑洞周围薄吸积盘的辐射性质，并与标准Schwarzschild黑洞进行比较，以期提供有效致密天体几何的唯象学诊断手段。

Method: 采用Novikov-Thorne形式论（Novikov-Thorne formalism），以Schwarzschild声学黑洞作为有效背景几何，唯象地比较吸积盘的可观测辐射量。数值示例采用黑洞质量M=15M⊙的玩具模型（toy model）。

Result: 声学黑洞展示出两种依赖参数ξ的吸积盘辐射机制：当0<ξ≤2.8时为增强机制（strengthening regime），辐射特征相对于Schwarzschild情形增强；当ξ>2.8时为减弱机制（weakening regime），辐射特征降低。边际稳定轨道半径r_ms在ξ≈2.8附近发生分支变化，导致通量、温度和光度轮廓的急剧改变。

Conclusion: 声学黑洞与标准Schwarzschild黑洞在吸积盘辐射特性上的显著差异，可为比较有效致密天体几何提供唯象学的诊断依据。

Abstract: We investigate the properties of a thin accretion disk in the Novikov-Thorne framework around a Schwarzschild acoustic black hole characterized by a nonzero background fluid four-velocity $v_{r} = \sqrt{2Mξ/r}$, where $ξ$ is a tuning parameter. The Novikov-Thorne formalism is used here phenomenologically, with the Schwarzschild acoustic black hole treated as an effective background geometry for comparing disk observables with those of the Schwarzschild black hole. We show that the acoustic black hole exhibits two regimes depending on $ξ$. For $0 < ξ\leq 2.8$, the disk is in a strengthening regime, in which the radiative characteristics are enhanced relative to the Schwarzschild case. For $ξ> 2.8$, the disk is in a weakening regime, in which the radiative characteristics are reduced relative to the Schwarzschild case. The most pronounced change in the radiative characteristics is associated with the behaviour of the marginally stable orbit radius $r_{ms}$, whose branch change near $ξ\approx 2.8$ produces a sharp modification of the flux, temperature, and luminosity profiles. For the numerical illustrations, we adopt a toy model with black hole mass $M = 15M_{\odot}$ and compare the corresponding flux, temperature, spectral luminosity, efficiency, and Eddington luminosity with those of the Schwarzschild black hole. These differences may provide phenomenological diagnostics for comparing effective compact object geometries.

### [65] [Fermionic Love number of higher-dimensional Reissner-Nordström black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24365)
*Xiankai Pang,Yu Tian,Hongbao Zhang,Qingquan Jiang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将先前关于费米子潮汐洛夫数（fermionic tidal Love numbers, TLNs）的工作推广到高维Reissner-Nordström黑洞。通过求解高维无质量Dirac方程并提取渐近行为，发现费米子TLNs在所有维度$D \geq 4$和角动量$l$下均非零（极值黑洞除外），且$l$依赖性随维度增加而减弱，在无限维极限下完全消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推广先前对四维时空中费米子潮汐洛夫数的研究至高维Reissner-Nordström黑洞，探索维度效应对费米子扰动下黑洞响应行为的影响。

Method: 在$D$维时空中利用内射Eddington坐标（ingoing Eddington coordinates）和正则标架（regular tetrads）求解无质量Dirac方程；通过识别正则解分支并从其在无穷远处的渐近行为中提取费米子潮汐洛夫数。

Result: 费米子TLNs在所有$D \geq 4$和总角动量$l$下均非零，仅极值黑洞（extremal black holes）除外；与玻色子TLNs（bosonic TLNs）在$D>4$时对某些$l$为零不同，费米子TLNs的$l$依赖性随维度$D$增加而减弱，并在无限维极限下完全消失。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了高维时空中黑洞对费米子扰动的响应具有丰富的维度依赖结构，为理解高维引力背景下黑洞的潮汐响应行为提供了新的认识。

Abstract: In this paper, we generalize our previous work on the fermionic tidal Love numbers (TLNs) to higher-dimensional Reissner-Nordström black holes. The massless Dirac equation is solved in $D$-dimensional spacetime using ingoing Eddington coordinates and regular tetrads. After identifying the regular solution branch, we extract the fermionic TLNs from its asymptotic behavior at infinity. The resulting TLNs exhibit a rich dimension-dependent structure that generalizes the four-dimensional case. Unlike bosonic TLNs, which vanish for certain values of the total angular momentum $l$ in dimensions $D>4$, fermionic TLNs remain non-zero for all $l$ and $D \geq 4$, except for extremal black holes. Moreover, the $l$-dependence weakens as $D$ increases, disappearing entirely in the infinite-dimensional limit. These results provide new insights into black hole responses to fermionic perturbations in higher-dimensional spacetimes.

### [66] [On Deformed Phase Space Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24419)
*A. Crespo-Hernández,E. A. Mena-Barboza,M. Sabido*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在非对易相空间（noncommutative phase space）背景下重新审视Schwarzschild黑洞，通过将视界面积算符映射为二维谐振子结构，推导了相空间非对易性诱导的修正，计算了修正后的面积谱、黑洞质量能级、跃迁频率、Hawking温度和熵，并猜想非对易熵贡献与Barrow熵之间的关联。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用广义Bopp平移（generalized Bopp shift）对正则坐标和动量进行变换，将视界面积算符映射为一个二维谐振子结构，从而在相空间非对易框架下推导黑洞的修正面积谱、质量能级、跃迁频率以及热力学量。

Result: 得到了修正后的面积谱、黑洞质量能级、跃迁频率、Hawking温度和熵，并明确了形变参数θ和η对黑洞热力学性质的具体物理影响。

Conclusion: 相空间非对易性对Schwarzschild黑洞的热力学性质产生可量化的修正；此外，本文猜想非对易贡献的熵与Barrow熵之间存在某种联系，为后续理论统一提供了可能的方向。

Abstract: We revisit the Schwarzschild black hole in the context of noncommutative phase space. By mapping the horizon area operator into a two-dimensional harmonic oscillator structure, we derive the modifications induced by phase space noncommutativity. The formalism is developed using the generalized Bopp shift on the canonical coordinates and momenta. We computed the modified area spectrum, black hole mass levels, transition frequencies, Hawking temperature, and entropy, highlighting the physical implications of the deformation parameters $θ$ and $η$ on the thermodynamical properties of the deformed black hole. Finally, we conjecture a connection between the noncommutative contribution to the entropy and Barrow's entropy.

### [67] [Binary black hole scattering with generic spins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24432)

TL;DR: 本文首次将高阶后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian, PM）理论对一般自旋黑洞散射的预测与数值相对论（numerical-relativity, NR）模拟进行对比，旨在改进偏心（eccentric）和进动（precessing）波形建模。通过提取NR中的方位角和极角散射角，建立其与PM自旋反冲可观测量之间的联系，并引入用于非束缚运动的渐进欧拉角（asymptotic Euler angles）推导其几何关系。NR模拟揭示了强场进动转向点结构，包括PM微扰结果中不存在的极角符号翻转现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从NR模拟中提取方位角散射角（azimuthal scattering angle）和极角散射角（polar scattering angle），将其与PM自旋反冲可观测量（spin-kick observable）建立关联；引入用于非束缚运动的渐进欧拉角，推导其与散射角之间的几何关系。

Result: NR模拟结果暴露了一个强场进动转向点结构（strong-field precessional turning-point structure），其中包含PM微扰结果中不存在的极角符号变化（polar-angle sign change）。

Conclusion: 高阶PM理论与NR模拟在弱场区域一致，但在强场区域存在定性差异，尤其表现在极角进动行为上。该发现对后续偏心与进动波形建模的改进具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: In this Letter, we confront high-order post-Minkowskian (PM) predictions for generic-spin black-hole scattering with numerical-relativity (NR) simulations for the first time, targeting improvements for eccentric and precessing waveform modelling. We extract azimuthal and polar scattering angles from NR and relate them to the PM spin-kick observable. We introduce asymptotic Euler angles for unbound motion and derive their geometric relation to the scattering angles. Notably, NR exposes a strong-field precessional turning-point structure, including a polar-angle sign change absent in the perturbative PM results.

### [68] [Gravity theory of the generalized mass to horizon entropy The Iyer Wald approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24495)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 明确证明了GMHE可以从一个推广的拉格朗日量L∝R^(1+ε)中有效重建，其中ε≡(n-1)/2表征了相对于广义相对论（general relativity, GR）标准形式的小偏离。

Abstract: In this letter, our aim is to study the gravitational origin of the \textit{generalized mass-to-horizon entropy} (GMHE), described by an entropic exponent index $n$ and a multiplicative parameter $γ$. We employ Iyer-Wald's approach within the modified $\mathfrak{f(R)}$ gravity scenario in order to assess the horizon entropy of the black hole (BH) by considering solutions with constant curvature for the spherically symmetric vacuum field equations. In this process, we explicitly show that the GMHE can effectively be reconstructed from a generalized Lagrangian $\mathfrak{L}\propto \mathfrak{R}^{1+ε}$, where $ε\equiv\frac{n-1}{2}$ measures tiny departures from the standard formulation of general relativity (GR). Finally, we discuss the physical implications of our results in relation to cosmology and the prospects for alleviating the thermodynamic instability of Schwarzschild BHs.

### [69] [Strong field lensing and shadows of $\boldsymbol{f(Q,\mathcal{B})}$ gravity black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24544)
*Rahul Das,Umananda Dev Goswami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了 $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ 引力理论（一种在 $f(Q)$ 引力基础上引入边界项 $\mathcal{B}$ 的扩展理论）中黑洞的强场透镜效应。采用 Booza 方法计算了静态球对称黑洞时空的偏折角，发现其偏折程度小于 Schwarzschild 黑洞。进一步分析了爱因斯坦环、角位置 $\vartheta_{\infty}$、角间距 $s$ 和相对放大率 $r_\text{mag}$ 等可观测量，并利用 EHT 合作组对 Sgr A* 黑洞阴影的观测数据，将模型参数约束为 $-3\lesssim q_0 \lesssim -2$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在修正引力理论中研究黑洞的强场透镜效应，旨在检验引力理论在强引力环境下的有效性。$f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ 理论通过引入边界项 $\mathcal{B}$ 扩展了 $f(Q)$ 引力，但其强场透镜特性尚待系统分析。

Method: 采用 V. Booza 发展的强场透镜分析方法，计算静态球对称 $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ 引力黑洞时空的偏折角，并与 Schwarzschild 黑洞对比。随后计算爱因斯坦环半径、角位置 $\vartheta_{\infty}$、角间距 $s$ 及相对放大率 $r_\text{mag}$ 等可观测量，并利用 EHT 合作组对 Sgr A* 黑洞阴影的观测数据对模型参数进行约束。

Result: 在所考虑的模型参数范围内，$f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ 引力黑洞对光的偏折程度始终小于 Schwarzschild 黑洞。除相对放大率 $r_\text{mag}$ 外，其他可观测量随模型参数的变化行为一致。基于 Sgr A* 阴影数据的约束表明，对于所有可取的 $s_0$ 值，另一模型参数 $q_0$ 的允许范围为 $-3\lesssim q_0 \lesssim -2$。

Conclusion: $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ 引力理论下的黑洞在强场透镜效应中表现出与 Schwarzschild 黑洞不同的特性，且通过 EHT 观测数据有效约束了模型参数范围，为该引力理论的检验提供了观测依据。

Abstract: We investigate the strong field lensing of light by black holes (BHs)emerging in $f(Q, \mathcal{B})$ theory of gravity, which is an extension of $f(Q)$ gravity theory by including a boundary term $\mathcal{B}$. Our analysis starts with the study of horizon structure for the BH spacetime in $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ gravity. The strong field lensing analysis is done by employing the method developed by V.~Booza. We calculate the deflection angle for the static and spherically symmetric $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ gravity BH spacetime and compare the results with the Schwarzschild BH. It is found that for all considerable scenarios of model parameters the $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ gravity BH produces less deflection of light than the Schwarzschild BH. We extend our study to examine the outermost relativistic Einstein rings and three other observables, viz., angular position $\vartheta_{\infty}$, angular separation $s$ and relative magnification $r_\text{mag}$. We see that except $r_\text{mag}$, other observables show the same kind of behavioural change with respect to model parameters. We also study the shadow of the considered BH. Moreover, using the shadow data of BH Sgr A* from EHT collaborations, we constrain the model parameters of the $f(Q,\mathcal{B})$ theory for the BH spacetime. The constraining analysis reveals that for all considerable values of the model parameter $s_0$, the allowed range of the other model parameter $q_0$ is $-3\lesssim q_0 \lesssim -2$.

</details>


### [70] [The $ω$-Effect from a Multimode Squeezed Graviton State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24613)
*Nick E. Mavromatos,Sarben Sarkar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从微观层面推导了纠缠中性介子系统（entangled neutral-meson systems）中的ω效应（$ω$-effect），该效应源于克尔黑洞周围轴子云（axion cloud）产生的多模压缩引力环境（multimode squeezed gravitational environment）。通过Takagi分解将引力子场表达为独立压缩超模（squeezed supermodes），其异常关联子（anomalous correlators）为先前D粒子泡沫模型中的唯象随机涨落提供了可计算的微观对应。在求迹引力子浴后，异常关联子与弱相互作用混合共同诱导两介子反对称与对称扇区之间的跃迁，从而在EPR态中产生一个小的交换对称混合参量ω，其表达式为Takagi超模的压缩振幅和相位与弱相互作用味混合矩阵元的加权求和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠中性介子系统中的ω效应是探测量子引力环境（quantum-gravitational environments）诱导CPT破坏的灵敏探针。本文旨在为这一效应提供微观推导，将其联系于来自克尔黑洞轴子云的多模压缩引力环境，从而将先前D粒子泡沫模型中的唯象描述提升至基于可计算微观物理的层面。

Method: 采用开放量子系统（open quantum system）框架，将克尔黑洞周围的轴子云视为产生多模压缩引力子态的引力环境。引入Takagi分解处理复对称压缩核（complex symmetric squeezing kernel），将引力子场分解为携带异常关联子的独立压缩超模。随后对该引力子浴求迹，并结合弱相互作用（weak interaction）诱导的味混合，计算由此产生的两介子反对称与对称扇区之间的跃迁。

Result: 得到了ω参量的显式表达式：它可写为所有Takagi超模的压缩振幅与相位的加权和，权重由弱相互作用的味混合矩阵元确定。该表达式形式上取代了D粒子泡沫模型中唯象的味改变D粒子反冲涨落方差，代之以可计算的引力子关联函数。该框架表明，ω效应可能是非经典引力环境态的普适特征，不限于特定的轴子云场景。

Conclusion: 所建立的微观框架暗示，ω效应可能更一般地作为非经典引力环境态的特征信号出现，其可观测性可延伸至其他天体物理和微观黑洞源。这为利用高精度中性介子实验检验量子引力效应提供了新的理论基础。

Abstract: The $ω$-effect in entangled neutral-meson systems provides a sensitive probe of CPT violation induced by quantum-gravitational environments. In open quantum systems, interactions with inaccessible gravitational degrees of freedom can render the reduced meson dynamics non-unitary, causing the CPT operator to become ill-defined, even when the underlying microscopic Hamiltonian is CPT invariant. We present a microscopic derivation of the $ω$-effect arising from a multimode squeezed gravitational environment generated by an axion cloud around a Kerr black hole. Using the Takagi decomposition of the associated complex symmetric squeezing kernel, the graviton field is expressed in terms of independent squeezed supermodes possessing anomalous correlators. These correlators provide a microscopic quantum counterpart of the stochastic fluctuations that appear in earlier D-particle foam descriptions of the $ω$-effect, replacing phenomenological variances of flavour-changing D-particle recoil by calculable graviton correlation functions. After tracing over the graviton bath, the anomalous correlators and the weak-interactions-induced mixing combine to generate transitions between the antisymmetric and symmetric two-meson sectors. This results in a small exchange-symmetric admixture, parametrised by $ω$, in the otherwise antisymmetric EPR state. We obtain an explicit expression for $ω$ in terms of a sum over Takagi supermodes weighted by their squeezing amplitudes and phases together with the weak-interaction flavour-mixing matrix element. The resulting framework suggests that the $ω$-effect may be a generic signature of non-classical states of gravitational environments, extending beyond the specific axion-cloud scenario considered here. The observability of the $ω$-effect from other astrophysical and microscopic black-hole sources is discussed.

</details>


### [71] [When Black Holes Can Wear Pants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24642)
*Giacomo Cacciapaglia,Manuel Del Piano,Francesco Sannino,Vania Vellucci*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了黑洞碎裂（black hole fragmentation）——即黑洞视界分裂为多个更小视界——可能发生的条件。经典广义相对论中，Bekenstein-Hawking面积定律禁止Schwarzschild黑洞碎裂；对于自旋Kerr黑洞，运动学分析也施加约束，仅在近极端情形下可能例外。文章进一步考察了高维Gregory-Laflamme不稳定性、超辐射不稳定性以及四维中修改熵/视界半径与质量关系的引力模型，发现碎片的发射在熵上可能有利，但其发生仍取决于初始态的运动学组态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解黑洞碎裂是否及如何发生，对于原初黑洞（primordial black holes）和黑洞并合（black hole mergers）等灾变事件具有重要物理意义，但此前缺乏系统的理论条件分析。

Method: 采用经典广义相对论框架下的面积定律与运动学分析，并结合高维Gregory-Laflamme不稳定性、非轴对称辐射捕获中的超辐射不稳定性（superradiant instability），以及四维中修改熵/视界半径与黑洞质量关系的引力模型进行综合考察。

Result: 经典广义相对论中Schwarzschild黑洞被面积定律禁止碎裂；Kerr黑洞的运动学约束进一步阻止碎裂，仅近极端情形（near-extremal cases）可能例外。在考察的各种模型中，小碎片发射在熵上可能有利，但其发生仍取决于初始态的运动学组态。

Conclusion: 碎裂的发生不仅需要熵上的有利条件，还受限于初始态的运动学组态。该分析厘清了黑洞可能发生碎裂的理论图景，对原初黑洞和黑洞并合等过程具有直接参考价值。

Abstract: We investigate the conditions under which black hole fragmentation, the splitting of a black hole horizon into multiple smaller ones, may occur. The simplest realization is that of a single black hole horizon splitting into two, giving rise to the eponymous pants topology. In classical general relativity, the Bekenstein-Hawking area law forbids such processes for Schwarzschild black holes. For spinning Kerr black holes, purely kinematic analyses impose constraints that prevent fragmentation, even in regimes where entropy considerations might allow it, except possibly in near-extremal cases. We then hunt for scenarios where black holes can wear pants: from the well-known Gregory-Laflamme instability in higher dimensions, to the potential effect of superradiant instabilities in non-axisymmetric radiation trapping, to finally gravitational models that modify the relations between entropy and/or horizon radius and the black hole mass in four dimensions. In all such cases, emission of small fragments can be entropically favored, however its occurrence still depends on the kinematic configuration of the initial state. Our analysis clarifies the theoretical landscape where black holes may fragment, which is particularly relevant for primordial black holes and catastrophic events such as black hole mergers.

</details>


### [72] [Reduction of the Finsler gravity vacuum equation and dynamics for the cosmological Landsberg spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24698)
*Christian Pfeifer,Fidel F. Villaseñor*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文识别了标量Finsler引力真空方程（scalar Finsler gravity vacuum equation）约化为Finsler Ricci曲率（Finslerian Ricci curvature）为零的精确条件，并应用于求解Landsberg型（Landsberg type）均匀各向同性Finsler时空函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Finsler引力中，爱因斯坦真空方程（Einstein vacuum equations）通过Ricci张量（Ricci tensor）为零的简单约化不再直接成立，因此需要寻找类似约化成立的条件。

Method: 通过解析论证（analytic arguments），研究标量Finsler引力真空方程在纯度量（purely metric）和Palatini（Palatini）两种表述下的约化条件。

Result: 约化成立的条件包括：存在Finsler函数（Finsler function）\(F\)的某次幂\(F^n\)具有足够正则性，且其对应的Finsler度量（Finsler metric）在光锥（light cones）上非退化；同时标量方程中的Landsberg项（Landsberg term）必须为零。

Conclusion: 该结果显著推广了[Villasenor2024]中要求\(F^2\)正则的强假设，并展示了在Landsberg型均匀各向同性Finsler时空函数求解中的应用。

Abstract: When solving the Einstein vacuum equations, a very helpful feature is that they reduce simply to the vanishing of the Ricci tensor. In Finsler gravity, a promising extension of general relativity that can describe the gravitational field of kinetic gases from a phase space perspective in terms of Finsler geometry, such a reduction is not as straightforward.
  In this article, we identify precise conditions under which the scalar Finsler gravity vacuum equation (in either its purely metric or its Palatini formulation) reduces to the vanishing of the Finslerian Ricci curvature. Through analytic arguments, we find that this happens if there exists some power $F^n$ of the Finsler function $F$ that is sufficiently regular and whose associated Finsler metric is non-degenerate on the light cones. Moreover, the Landsberg term in the scalar equation must vanish. This result significantly generalizes the findings of [Villasenor2024], where a reduction theorem was established under the quite strong assumption that $F^2$ is regular, which is not satisfied by many examples currently under consideration.
  We demonstrate the impact of our findings by applying them to solve the Finsler gravity equations for homogeneous and isotropic Finsler spacetime functions of Landsberg type.

</details>


### [73] [Radial Mirror Scattering and the QNM Convergence Region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24812)
*Alex Kehagias,Antonio Riotto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从径向散射角度重新审视了史瓦西延迟格林函数中拟正则模态展开的收敛区域。通过将乌龟坐标关于一个特殊反射点进行自然反射，将原Regge-Wheeler问题映射到一个具有相同拟正则模谱的镜像径向问题。该反射虽非时空对称性，也不保持势函数不变，但为控制收敛的第二光锥距离提供了简单的镜像解释。折叠径向线后，直接通道与镜像通道表现为双分量半线问题的对角与非对角传播。最后，将该结构与AdS₂格林函数联系起来，其中相同的直接加镜像光锥结构源自真实的边界反弹零测地线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视史瓦西黑洞背景中拟正则模态展开的收敛条件，为收敛区域提供一种清晰且直观的谱解释。

Method: 采用径向散射观点，引入乌龟坐标关于一个特殊反射点的自然反射，将原Regge-Wheeler问题映射为镜像径向问题；随后将径向线在反射点处折叠，将直接和镜像贡献分解为双分量半线问题的对角与非对角传播通道。

Result: 发现反射点定义了控制收敛的第二光锥距离，并给出其镜像解释；双分量半线问题框架将直接和镜像贡献分别对应为对角和非对角传播通道；该结构与AdS₂格林函数中的直接-镜像光锥结构具有相似性，后者源于真实的边界反弹零测地线。

Conclusion: 为拟正则模态展开的收敛条件提供了谱解释，并阐明了反射点在史瓦西径向格林函数中的作用。

Abstract: We revisit the convergence region of the quasinormal modes expansion of Schwarzschild retarded Green functions from a radial scattering viewpoint. The tortoise coordinate admits a natural reflection about a distinguished point, which maps the original Regge-Wheeler problem to a mirror radial problem with the same quasinormal mode spectrum. Although this reflection is not a spacetime symmetry and does not leave the potential invariant, it gives a simple image interpretation of the second lightcone distance that controls convergence. Equivalently, after folding the radial line at the reflection point, the direct and mirror contributions arise as diagonal and off-diagonal propagation channels of a two-component half-line problem. We also relate this structure to the AdS$_2$ Green function, where the same direct-plus-image lightcone structure arises from a genuine boundary-bouncing null geodesic. This provides a spectral interpretation of the convergence condition and clarifies the role of the reflection point in the Schwarzschild radial Green function.

### [74] [The Bondi--Sachs gauge, BMS frames, and memory in black hole perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24816)
*Andrew Spiers,Adam Pound,Jordan Moxon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个在Kerr背景上迭代变换至Bondi–Sachs规范并固定BMS框架的框架，以解决下一代引力波探测器（如LISA）所需波形模型中对BMS框架精确控制的需求，特别针对黑洞微扰论和引力自作用力计算中的红外发散和规范奇异性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA等下一代引力波探测器需要更高精度的波形模型，因此必须精确控制此前无关紧要的规范自由度，尤其是渐近BMS框架的选择。这一问题在黑洞微扰论（black hole perturbation theory）中尤为突出，特别是在引力自作用力（gravitational self-force）计算中，现有模型处于未知框架且面临二阶微扰的红外远区规范奇异性。

Method: 作者提出一个迭代变换至Bondi–Sachs规范并固定Kerr背景上BMS框架的框架。该方法将Bondi–Sachs形式推广至多尺度展开（multiscale expansions），并引入软毛（soft hair）和“遗忘规范”（forgetful gauges）概念。

Result: 该框架能够规避红外发散（infrared divergences），并自然纳入记忆效应（memory effects），包括此前仅在自作用力波形中事后添加的“记忆扭曲”（memory distortion）。该框架还可用于振铃分析（ringdown analysis）。

Conclusion: 该框架有望在引力波波形建模中实现对BMS框架的精确控制，对数值相对论（numerical relativity）和后牛顿理论（post-Newtonian theory）的比对具有重要意义。

Abstract: As LISA and other next-generation detectors demand increasingly accurate waveform models, there is a growing need for these models to precisely control gauge freedoms that had previously been inconsequential. One such intrinsic freedom is the choice of the asymptotic Bondi--Metzner--Sachs (BMS) frame. The need to control the BMS frame is particularly pronounced in black hole perturbation theory, where there has been little work to this end -- most glaringly in gravitational self-force calculations, which are in an unknown frame and encounter infrared, far-zone gauge singularities at second perturbative order. Here we present a framework for iteratively transforming to the Bondi--Sachs gauge and fixing the BMS frame on a Kerr background. This includes an extension of the Bondi--Sachs formalism to the multiscale expansions that underpin most self-force-based waveforms, introducing soft hair and a concept of ``forgetful gauges'' in the process. Our framework evades infrared divergences and naturally incorporates memory effects that had previously only ever been added ``after the fact'' in self-force waveforms, including the recently discovered ``memory distortion''. Our formalism could also be used for ringdown analysis, and we expect it to be vital for comparisons with numerical relativity and post-Newtonian theory.

### [75] [Quintic Modification to Lifshitz Quasi-topological Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24835)
*A. Bazrafshan,A. R. Olamaei,M. Ghanaatian*

TL;DR: 本文将 Lifshitz 黑洞的分析扩展到五次准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity）理论，结合有质量阿贝尔矢量场（massive Abelian vector field），通过数值方法构造了静态解，并分析了热力学性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将 Lifshitz 黑洞的研究从三次和四次准拓扑引力推广到五次情形，探讨在有质量矢量场存在下更高阶曲率修正对 Lifshitz 背景和黑洞解的影响。

Method: 采用常曲率视界的静态 Ansatz，导出约化场方程并识别一维有效系统的径向守恒量；利用近 horizon 展开和打靶法（shooting method）构造数值解。

Result: 给出了相对论分支 z=1 和 Lifshitz 分支 z=2 下三种视界拓扑（k=-1,0,+1）的数值解；度量函数和规范场函数的定性行为与三、四次准拓扑 Lifshitz 黑洞一致；所展示的数值分支具有正热容（positive heat capacity）。

Conclusion: 五次准拓扑引力框架下可构造 Lifshitz 黑洞数值解，其热力学行为（Wald 熵、Hawking 温度及局部热稳定性）与低阶情形定性相似。

Abstract: We extend the analysis of Lifshitz black holes to quintic order in five-dimensional quasi-topological gravity coupled to a massive Abelian vector field. Starting from a static ansatz with a constant-curvature horizon, we derive the reduced field equations and identify the radially conserved quantity of the one-dimensional effective system. We then analyze the algebraic conditions that permit Lifshitz backgrounds, both in the absence and in the presence of the massive vector field. Since closed-form black-hole solutions are not available for the generic quintic theory, we construct numerical solutions using near-horizon expansions and a shooting method. We present solutions for the relativistic branch \(z=1\) and the Lifshitz branch \(z=2\), covering the three horizon topologies \(k=-1,0,+1\). The numerical profiles of the metric functions and the gauge-field function show behavior that is qualitatively consistent with earlier studies of cubic and quartic quasi-topological Lifshitz black holes. We also compute the Wald entropy and Hawking temperature, and examine the local thermal behavior through logarithmic entropy -- temperature plots. For the representative parameter choices considered here, the numerical branches shown possess positive heat capacity.

### [76] [Non-perturbative, background independent Fock representations for canonical quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24858)
*T. Thiemann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证了在广义相对论的非微扰正则量子化中，存在严格且背景无关的Fock表示（Fock representation），其Hilbert空间是可分的，有望减少量子化歧义并提高理论的可预测性，并简要讨论了宇宙学截断与量子反弹机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论（general relativity）的紫外完备量子场论被认为需要非微扰（non-perturbative）方法，而经典广义相对论的背景无关性（background independence）为量子几何与物质场的Hilbert空间表示提供了物理选择。现有非微扰正则量子化方案中的不可分Hilbert空间带来了量子化歧义（quantisation ambiguities），亟需更具预测性的替代表示。

Method: 基于正则量子化（canonical quantisation）框架，构建背景无关的Fock表示（background independent Fock representation），以描述几何与物质场。该Fock空间是可分的（separable），与现有显式背景无关且非微扰的方案形成对比。作为简单应用，讨论了宇宙学截断（cosmological truncation）与量子反弹（quantum bounces）机制。

Result: 存在严格且背景无关的Fock表示，其Hilbert空间可分，从而可避免因不可分性导致的量子化歧义，提高理论的可预测性。在宇宙学截断下，该表示可自然导出量子反弹机制。

Conclusion: 背景无关的Fock表示为非微扰正则量子化提供了一个新的、可分Hilbert空间框架，有助于减少量子化歧义并提升理论的可预测性。该文仅呈现了最基本形式，更多细节与扩展见姊妹论文。

Abstract: A UV complete quantum field theory of general relativity is believed to require a non-perturbative approach. Moreover, background independence of classical general relativity supplies a physical selection for suitable Hilbert space representations of the quantum geometry and matter fields.
  In this contribution we show that, contrary to common intuition, there exist rigorous, background independent Fock representations available for a non-perturbative canonical quantisation of geometry and suitable matter fields.
  This is interesting because the Fock Hilbert space is separable while the Hilbert space of other manifestly background independent and non-perturbative canonical quantisation programmes is not. Since non-separability is a source for quantisation ambiguities, such a Fock representation may help to arrive at a significantly more predictive theory. As a simple application we discuss the cosmological truncation and mechanisms for quantum bounces.
  To make this manuscript concise we focus on the simplest incarnation of this idea. More details and many extensions are supplied in a companion paper.

</details>

### [77] [Probing the pairing symmetry of moiré graphene superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23994)
*Sayak Biswas,Rajdeep Sensarma,Mohit Randeria*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文结合实验与理论手段，约束了魔角莫尔石墨烯（magic-angle moiré graphene）在空穴掺杂侧 ν=-2 附近、基于非公度凯库勒螺旋（incommensurate Kekulé spiral, IKS）正常态的可能超导序参量（superconducting order parameter），并针对节点超导（nodal superconductivity）的实验约束，提出了通过 Zeeman 场方向响应区分单重态（singlet）与三重态（triplet）配对以及确定 d-vector 的判据性实验方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔角莫尔石墨烯的超导配对对称性（pairing symmetry）是一个尚未解决的基础性问题，明确其配对机制对于理解该体系强关联物理和非常规超导机理至关重要。

Method: 通过结合实验与理论输入，从非公度凯库勒螺旋（IKS）正常态出发，约束可能出现的超导序参量；针对节点超导的实验约束，基于超导态对 Zeeman 场（Zeeman field）方向的响应，提出两类实验方案：第一类为探测节点附近低能激发的谱学与热力学测量，第二类为探测边界处拓扑保护的安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）的相位敏感测量。

Result: 研究给出了区分单重态与三重态配对的具体预测，并明确了在三重态情形下确定 d-vector 的判据；边界处拓扑保护安德烈夫束缚态的谱学被证明是配对对称性的“确凿证据（smoking gun signature）”。

Conclusion: 提出的两类基于 Zeeman 场方向响应的实验方案可为魔角莫尔石墨烯的超导配对对称性提供决定性的检验，从而解决该领域的基础争议。

Abstract: The pairing symmetry of magic-angle moiré graphene is a fundamental question that remains unresolved. Combining experimental and theoretical inputs, we constrain the superconducting order parameters that can emerge from the incommensurate Kekulé spiral (IKS) normal state on the hole-doped side of $ν= -2$. Imposing the additional experimental constraint of nodal superconductivity, we are left with the task of distinguishing between singlet or triplet pairing, and of determining the d-vector in the latter case. We propose definitive tests to identify the pairing symmetry based on two classes of experiments using the response of the superconducting state to Zeeman field orientation. The first set of predictions is for spectroscopic and thermodynamic measurements sensitive to low-energy excitations near the nodes. The second set is for phase-sensitive measurements of topologically protected Andreev bound states near boundaries, whose spectroscopy is shown to provide a smoking gun signature of the pairing symmetry.

</details>


### [78] [Multiple phases in K2Cr3As3: a playground for manipulating topological superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24108)
*Seigo Ogawa,Tomoki Miyoshi,Saki Uchida,Kazuaki Matano,Shinji Kawasaki,Yoshihiko Inada,Guo-qing Zheng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过核磁共振测量在无磁有序、高转变温度（6.2 K）的Cr基化合物K₂Cr₃As₃中发现了自旋三重态超导电性的标志性特征，揭示了三种不同的超导相及其配对自旋方向（d(k)-矢量）的演化，建立了该材料作为模型自旋三重态超导体和拓扑相调控平台的地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋三重态拓扑超导体（spin-triplet topological superconductor）极为罕见，但其能够承载可用于容错量子计算的马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states）。此前研究集中于U基化合物，但这类材料存在转变温度（Tc）低以及共存竞争序等问题，导致实验困难且结论常相互矛盾，亟需寻找更优的候选材料体系。

Method: 本研究通过核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）测量手段，探测来自内部自旋自由度的自旋三重态超导电性的标志性特征，并表征拓扑相的高度可调谐性。

Result: 在K₂Cr₃As₃中发现了三种不同的超导相：低磁场下，随冷却过程体系从螺旋态（helical state, Phase A）转变为手征态（chiral state, Phase B），d(k)-矢量从面内旋转至面外方向，两相均在能隙中存在点节点（point nodes）；高磁场下的Phase C实现了线节点能隙（line-nodal gap），其d(k)-矢量位于基面内。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了K₂Cr₃As₃作为模型自旋三重态超导体（model spin-triplet superconductor）的地位，并表明它是一个用于调控拓扑相（topological phases）的有前景的平台。

Abstract: Spin-triplet topological superconductors are rare but of fundamental interest as they can host Majorana bound states that can be used in fault-tolerant quantum computing. Recent efforts have been devoted to searching for spin-triplet states in U-based compounds, but these materials have a low transition temperature (Tc) and coexisting competing orders, which creates significant experimental challenges and often leads to contradictory conclusions. The Cr-based candidate K2Cr3As3 offers a promising alternative: it has a much higher Tc of 6.2 K and no magnetic order. Here we report a hallmark signature of spin-triplet superconductivity arising from the internal spin degrees of freedom via nuclear magnetic resonance measurements, and demonstrate the high tunability of the topological phases. We discovered three distinct superconducting phases and revealed the evolution of the paired-spins direction (d(k)-vector). At low magnetic fields, K2Cr3As3 evolves from a helical (Phase A) to a chiral state (Phase B) with a rotation of the d(k)-vector from in-plane to out-of-plane direction upon cooling, although both phases have point nodes in the gap. A linenodal gap is realized in the high-field Phase C, where the d(k)-vector lies in the basal plane. These findings establish K2Cr3As3 as a model spin-triplet superconductor and a promising platform for manipulating topological phases.

</details>

### [79] [As above, so below: assessing extremeness of the neutron-star equation of state based on the unstable branch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23929)
*Tyler Gorda,Oleg Komoltsev,Aleksi Kurkela,Jürgen Schaffner-Bielich*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究论证了中子星物质微观模型在高密度区间的行为受到因果性、稳定性和热力学一致性的严格约束，发现纯强子模型在超出最大中心密度后常需要与原假设截然不同的行为，而包含额外自由度的模型表现更优，从而不支持纯核子模型描述所有稳定中子星，并支持稳定大质量中子星中出现额外自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有中子星物质微观模型广泛用于天体物理应用，但研究重点集中于稳定中子星所能达到的最大密度以下，尚未系统考察模型假设在更高密度区域可能产生的重要影响。

Method: 通过要求模型满足因果性（causality）、稳定性（stability）和热力学一致性（thermodynamic consistency）并将其向微扰QCD（perturbative-QCD）区域扩展，从而揭示更高密度下的必然行为；同时提供了构建和可视化此类扩展的工具。

Result: 纯强子模型在达到最大中心密度后，其在更高密度下的行为往往需要与原模型假设发生根本性改变；而包含额外自由度（additional degrees of freedom）的模型在高密度区域表现更优。

Conclusion: 纯核子模型（purely nucleonic models）不适用于描述所有稳定中子星，稳定大质量中子星中应存在某种类型的额外自由度。

Abstract: Microscopic models of neutron-star matter have been widely used in astrophysical applications. The focus of attention has been on densities up to the maximal densities reached in stable neutron stars. The possibility that the underlying model assumptions may have important implications at higher densities has not been addressed. Here, we show that the behaviour at higher densities is strongly constrained by requiring a causal, stable, and thermodynamically consistent extension to the perturbative-QCD regime. We explicitly reveal what that behaviour must be and provide a tool for constructing and visualizing such extensions. We find that purely hadronic models trusted up to the maximal central density often require radically different behaviour at higher densities from that assumed in the original model, while models with additional degrees of freedom fare better. Our analysis disfavors purely nucleonic models for describing all stable neutron stars and supports the appearance of some type of additional degrees of freedom in stable massive neutron stars.

</details>

### [80] [Uniaxial poroelastic tendon model with crimped fibre recruitment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24393)
*Zoe C. Godard,Sarah L. Waters,Derek E. Moulton*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种一维多孔弹性（poroelastic）模型，将卷曲原纤维（crimped fibrils）的募集机制纳入肌腱力学分析，发现含纤维模型在加载时更软、松弛更慢，并在应力-应变曲线中产生滞回环（hysteresis），其行为与实验观察一致，为肌腱结构提供自然保护机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 肌腱等生物软组织力学中，纤维募集（fibre recruitment）扮演重要角色，但现有基于多孔弹性（poroelasticity）框架的肌腱模型尚未纳入卷曲纤维（crimped fibrils）的募集机制。

Method: 构建一维多孔弹性模型，固相骨架由软的新胡克（neo-Hookean）背景基质和初始不承载的卷曲原纤维组成（FIB模型），通过单轴常载加载与卸载实验，与纯新胡克（NH）模型对比，系统动力学由扩散系数依赖刚度的扩散方程控制。

Result: 在肌腱参数范围内，FIB模型比NH模型更软，加载时稳态趋近更慢；卸载时因纤维重新卷曲导致软组织软化，松弛显著变慢，产生应力-应变滞回环，且滞回随加载增加而减小。

Conclusion: 卷曲纤维的引入使肌腱能在不过度拉伸纤维或基质的情况下承受更大应变，提供了结构保护机制，且该框架易于扩展至其他纤维本构律（constitutive laws），便于生物学解释与实验数据对比。

Abstract: Fibre recruitment plays an important role in tendon and other biological soft tissue mechanics. Due to their large water content, a popular modelling approach for tendons is poroelasticity. Within this framework some tendon studies have included fibres, though none have included crimped fibre recruitment. We present a one dimensional poroelastic model in which the solid skeleton is composed of a soft neo-Hookean background matrix and crimped fibrils which do not bear load (FIB model). As the tissue is stretched, fibrils are straightened and contribute to load bearing. The fibre-reinforced tissue is compared to a tissue with a purely neo-Hookean (NH) skeleton in response to a uniaxial constant applied load (loading) and release of the load (unloading). The system dynamics are governed by a diffusion equation where the diffusion coefficient depends on stiffness. Within tendon parameter ranges, the FIB model is softer than the NH model, and so approaches steady state more slowly during loading. The presence of crimped fibrils allows the tendon to stretch further without excessively straining the fibrils or the NCM, providing a natural protection mechanism for the tendon's structural components to load, in agreement with experiments. During unloading, the FIB model is much slower to relax as the tissue softens due to fibril re-crimping. This asymmetry in loading and unloading manifests as a hysteresis loop in the stress-strain curve averaged over the tendon. The hysteresis is reduced with increasing applied load. The inclusion of fibrils allows for clearer biological interpretation and potential comparison to data. While the stress law employed in this study is bespoke for the application at hand by accounting for crimp and fibril recruitment, other fibril constitutive laws can readily be considered and incorporated into this framework.

</details>


### [81] [Emergent Self-Organisation of Intelligent Active Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24547)
*Priyanka Iyer,Segun Goh,Gerhard Gompper*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了具备自推进、环境感知、信息处理和自主导向等特征的智能活性粒子（intelligent active particles），强调其中非互易相互作用（non-reciprocal interactions）的普遍性以及信息在群体中的传播，涵盖生物系统与工程系统，并指出流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）对群体行为（如集群、捕食-猎物行为及复杂环境导航）的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能活性粒子系统在生物和工程领域广泛存在，但对其核心特征（如非互易相互作用与信息传播）以及流体动力学效应的系统理解尚不充分，需要整合分析以揭示其涌现动力学（emergent dynamics）的普遍规律。

Method: 采用综述性分析方法，基于活性物质（active matter）与群体运动（collective motion）的研究框架，归纳智能活性粒子的共性特征——自推进、定向感知、信息处理、决策与目标导向自控，并分析非互易相互作用及流体动力学在这些系统中的角色。

Result: 研究发现，智能活性粒子的典型涌现行为包括集群与群群（swarms and flocks）形成、捕食者-猎物行为（predator-prey behavior）以及复杂环境中的导航；这些行为普遍受到流体动力学相互作用的显著影响。

Conclusion: 智能活性粒子系统的动力学核心在于非互易相互作用与信息传播的耦合，而水媒介质中的流体动力学效应是不可忽视的关键因素，为理解生物群体运动与设计工程活性系统提供了统一视角。

Abstract: Intelligent active particles are characterized by self-propulsion, directional sensing of their environment, information processing, decision making and goal-oriented self-steering. This implies, in particular, the prevalence of non-reciprocal interactions, and the importance of information propagation through agent groups. Examples include biological systems (cells, insects, birds, fish, pedestrians) as well as engineered systems (nano- and microbots). As many agents move in an aqueous medium, hydrodynamic interactions strongly affect the dynamics. The emergent dynamics includes the formation of swarms and flocks, predator-prey behavior, and the navigation in complex environments.

</details>
