Warburton,M. Watanabe,S. Watanuki,C. Wessel,X. P. Xu,B. D. Yabsley,S. Yamada,W. Yan,W. P. Yan,J. Yelton,K. Yi,J. H. Yin,K. Yoshihara,C. Z. Yuan,J. Yuan,L. Yuan,Y. Yusa,L. Zani,F. Zeng,M. Zeyrek,B. Zhang,X. Zhao,V. Zhilich,J. S. Zhou,Q. D. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,L. Zhu,R. Žlebčík*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于Belle和Belle II实验在Υ(4S)共振峰处积累的711 fb⁻¹和492 fb⁻¹数据样本，本研究搜寻了X(3872)→π⁰χ_{cJ}(1P) (J=0,1,2)和X(3915)→π⁰χ_{c1}的π⁰跃迁过程，首次发现X(3872)→π⁰χ_{c0}衰变证据（显著度3.4σ），并测量了其分支比及其与π⁺π⁻J/ψ模式的比例。对于X(3915)→π⁰χ_{c1}未观察到显著信号，设置了上限。实验测量结果与X(3872)作为强子分子态（hadronic molecular state）的理论预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: X(3872)和X(3915)等奇特强子态（exotic hadron states）的内部结构是当前粒子物理的前沿问题。通过测量其π⁰跃迁到χ_{cJ}(1P)的分支比，可与强子分子态（hadronic molecule）等理论模型进行定量比较，从而揭示这些粒子的本质。

Method: 利用Belle和Belle II实验在Υ(4S)共振峰处收集的积分亮度分别为711 fb⁻¹和492 fb⁻¹的数据样本，在B⁺→π⁰χ_{cJ}K⁺衰变过程中搜寻X(3872)→π⁰χ_{cJ}和X(3915)→π⁰χ_{c1}的衰变信号。对于未观察到显著信号的模式，设置了90%置信度（credibility level）的上限。

Result: 首次发现X(3872)→π⁰χ_{c0}衰变，显著度为3.4σ（包含系统误差）。测得分支比乘积B(B⁺→X(3872)K⁺)×B(X(3872)→π⁰χ_{c0})=(20.0±6.8±2.3)×10⁻⁶，分支比比值B(X(3872)→π⁰χ_{c0})/B(X(3872)→π⁺π⁻J/ψ)=2.3±0.8±0.4。X(3872)→π⁰χ_{c1}和π⁰χ_{c2}的分支比乘积90%置信度上限分别为7.5×10⁻⁶和15.3×10⁻⁶。X(3915)→π⁰χ_{c1}未观察到显著信号，设置上限为6.6×10⁻⁶。J=0和2的衰变因宇称守恒（parity conservation）被禁止。

Conclusion: X(3872)→π⁰χ_{cJ}的测量分支比与基于X(3872)作为强子分子态（hadronic molecular state）解释的多项理论预言一致。X(3915)→π⁰χ_{c1}未发现显著信号，其上限进一步限制了该粒子的衰变性质。

Abstract: We search for the pionic transitions $X(3872)\toπ^0χ_{cJ}(1P)$ $(J = 0,~1,~2)$ and $X(3915)\toπ^0χ_{c1}$ in $B^+\to π^0χ_{cJ}K^+$ decays using the Belle and Belle~II data samples collected at the $Υ(4S)$ resonance, corresponding to integrated luminosities of $711~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and $492~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$, respectively. We report the first evidence for the decay $X(3872)\toπ^0χ_{c0}$ with a significance of $3.4σ$, including systematic uncertainties. We measure the product of branching fractions ${\cal B}(B^+\to X(3872)K^+)\times{\cal B}(X(3872)\toπ^0χ_{c0})=(20.0\pm6.8\pm2.3)\times10^{-6}$ and the branching fraction ratio ${\cal B}(X(3872)\toπ^0χ_{c0})/{\cal B}(X(3872)\toπ^+π^-J/ψ)=2.3\pm0.8\pm0.4$, where the first and second uncertainties are statistical and systematic, respectively. The upper limits at 90\% credibility on the products of branching fractions for the $π^0χ_{c1}$ and $π^0χ_{c2}$ modes are $7.5\times10^{-6}$ and $15.3\times10^{-6}$, respectively. The corresponding upper limits on the branching fraction ratios relative to the $π^+π^-J/ψ$ decay are $0.9$ and $1.8$. The measured branching fractions for $X(3872)\toπ^0χ_{cJ}$ are consistent with several theoretical predictions based on the hadronic molecular interpretation of the $X(3872)$. No significant signal is seen for the $X(3915)\toπ^0χ_{c1}$ decay, and we set the 90\% credibility upper limit of ${\cal B}(B^+\to X(3915)K^+)\times{\cal B}(X(3915)\toπ^0χ_{c1})<6.6\times10^{-6}$, while the decays for $J=0$ and 2 are forbidden by parity conservation.

</details>

### [83] [Quantum turbulence in the many-body regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23822)
*Sayak Bhattacharjee,Mahendra K. Verma,Alexander V. Balatsky,Srinivas Raghu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文从凝聚态物理视角探讨量子流体中湍流流体力学（turbulent hydrodynamics）的现象学，提出超越平均场近似、研究多体量子效应对湍流的影响，并列举了可在超冷原子和量子计算平台中探索的开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对量子流体湍流的研究多基于平均场理论（如 Gross-Pitaevskii 方程），缺乏对量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）和多体量子效应的系统理解，尤其是在接近零温的条件下。本文旨在填补这一空白，激发对量子多体系统中湍流现象的研究。

Method: 采用理论综述与问题驱动的方法：从弱相互作用超流体的平均场描述出发，引入量子涨落修正；通过举例低维周期势阱中的玻色子体系及其超流-绝缘体相变量子临界点（quantum critical point），展示多体量子效应可能出现的场景；最后整理出一系列开放问题，指向现代量子多体技术的应用。

Result: 提出了一套涵盖弱相互作用超流体、量子涨落效应、低维体系及量子临界点在内的研究框架；识别了超冷原子（ultracold-atom）和量子计算（quantum computing）平台作为潜在实验实现途径；以一系列开放问题收束，为后续研究提供方向。

Conclusion: 量子流体中的湍流流体力学应超越平均场近似，引入多体量子效应进行更深入的研究。本文属于“湍流与统计物理学前沿”（Frontiers of turbulence and statistical physics）主题专刊的一部分。

Abstract: We discuss phenomenology associated with turbulent hydrodynamics in quantum fluids from a condensed-matter perspective. We begin with weakly-interacting superfluids, often modeled by a mean-field theory governed by the Gross-Pitaevskii equation. Considering the effect of quantum fluctuations beyond the mean-field approximation, we propose a study of many-body quantum effects in turbulent hydrodynamics, especially near zero temperature. We motivate examples of quantum many-body systems where such effects may be uncovered. These include bosons confined in a periodic potential in low spatial dimensions (one and two), and the associated quantum critical point of the superfluid-insulator transition, realized in present-day ultracold-atom and quantum computing platforms. We conclude by listing a set of (open) questions that may be answered using modern quantum many-body techniques. This article is part of the theme issue 'Frontiers of turbulence and statistical physics'.

### [84] [Optical spectroscopy of Bose-Einstein condensates at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24568)
*R. M. F. Andersen,L. N. Stokholm,I. Zebergs,N. R. Neubert,A. S. Chatterley,N. Kjærgaard,J. J. Arlt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文报道了对超冷部分凝聚的87Rb气体的光学光谱测量，通过暗场（dark-field）配置和单光子灵敏度的频率捷变激光系统，在频域中区分了热原子和玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）组分的光谱特征。结合描述非均匀原子云中光传播的模型，提取了温度和原子数等参数，并对比飞行时间（time-of-flight）吸收成像进行了验证。光谱方法对近纯凝聚体中微小热组分具有更高灵敏度，并展示了暗场配置相对于明场（bright-field）配置的优越性能。研究揭示了光学稠密超冷气体中此前未探索的光谱结构，确立了光谱学作为超低温系统表征工具的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷气体的传统表征手段（如飞行时间吸收成像）对极低温度下微小热组分的敏感度有限，且无法在频域上直接分辨热原子与凝聚体组分。因此，需要发展一种原位、高灵敏度的光谱方法来揭示超冷气体中此前未被探测到的光谱结构，从而更精确地表征近纯凝聚体的热力学状态。

Method: 实验上采用暗场光学配置，结合单光子灵敏度和频率捷变激光系统，对超冷且部分凝聚的87Rb气体进行原位光谱测量。理论上构建了一个描述光在非均匀原子云中传播的模型，用于从光谱中提取温度与原子数等参数。

Result: 光谱测量成功在频域上区分了热原子和玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚组分；提取的温度和原子数与传统的飞行时间吸收成像结果一致；光谱方法对近纯凝聚体中的微小热组分展现出更高的灵敏度；暗场配置的光谱性能优于明场配置。

Conclusion: 研究发现了光学稠密超冷气体中此前未知的光谱结构，证实了所发展的暗场光谱学方法能够作为一种有效的工具，用于超低温系统中极低温度条件下的精确表征。

Abstract: We report on optical spectroscopic measurements of ultracold and partially condensed 87Rb gases, which show distinct spectral features due to the thermal and the Bose condensed components in the frequency domain. These features are detected in-situ by using a dark-field configuration with single-photon sensitivity and a frequency-agile laser system. To interpret the observed spectra, we develop a model for light propagation through an inhomogeneous atomic cloud. This model enables the extraction of temperature and atom number, which we benchmark against conventional time-of-flight absorption imaging. The spectroscopically obtained cloud parameters show enhanced sensitivity to small thermal fractions in nearly pure condensates. We further compare the spectroscopy in dark-field and bright-field configurations, demonstrating the superior performance of the former. Our results reveal previously unexplored spectral structure in optically dense ultracold gases and establish spectroscopy as a tool for characterizing ultracold systems at very low temperatures.

</details>


### [85] [Quantum droplets and condensates in an optical lattice coupled to a dissipative cavity: Collective excitations and non-equilibrium dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24580)
*G. Vivek,Sudip Sinha,Subhasis Sinha*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用经典场方法研究了耦合到耗散腔模的一维光晶格中的稀薄玻色气体和自束缚量子液滴，揭示了极化激元型能隙激发、弛豫时间发散等非平衡现象，并发现了孤子型非平衡态及其类似疤痕（scarring）的动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期光-物质相互作用系统实验的启发，本文旨在探索耦合耗散腔的周期晶格中玻色气体和量子液滴的非平衡性质。

Method: 采用经典场方法（classical-field approach）求解该非平衡系统的稳态（stationary states）和集体激发（collective excitations）。

Result: 除了通常的玻戈留玻夫（Bogoliubov）模式外，识别出一种极化激元（polariton-like）型能隙激发，其频率在密度有序转变（density ordering transition）前软化，且弛豫时间在临界点附近发散。在液滴体系中分析了束缚模式（bound modes），并发现了包括具有扭结构型（kink-like configuration）的凝聚体和双液滴态（double-droplet state）在内的孤子型（solitonic）非平衡态。这些态在临界耦合之外失稳，但仍能在动力学中持续显现，类似疤痕现象（scarring phenomena）。

Conclusion: 耗散腔耦合为在实验可及的设置中探索凝聚体和量子液滴的丰富非平衡动力学提供了一条多样化的途径。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experiments on light-matter interacting systems, we investigate a dilute Bose gas and self-bound quantum droplets in a one-dimensional optical lattice coupled to a lossy cavity mode. Using a classical-field approach, we determine the stationary states and collective excitations of this non-equilibrium system. Apart from the usual Bogoliubov modes, we identify a polariton-like gapped excitation, the frequency of which softens as a precursor of the density ordering transition. Moreover, its relaxation time diverges as the critical point is approached, signaling the non-equilibrium nature of this transition. Dynamically, this polariton-like mode can be probed by inducing cavity field fluctuations, which in turn generates spatio-temporal oscillations of both the condensate and droplet states. In the droplet regime, we also analyze the bound modes which bear the characteristics of such non-equilibrium self-bound state. In addition, we uncover solitonic non-equilibrium states, including condensate with kink-like configuration and double-droplet state, and investigate their robustness following a sudden quench. Remarkably, although these states become unstable beyond a critical coupling, they continue to manifest in the dynamics, akin to the scarring phenomena. Our results demonstrate that dissipative cavity coupling provides a versatile route for exploring rich non-equilibrium dynamics of condensates and quantum droplets within experimentally accessible settings.

</details>


### [86] [Universality beyond the Kibble-Zurek mechanism in the condensation of coherently coupled Bose gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24864)
*Subhadeep Patra,Paolo Comaron,Arko Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过随机投影Gross-Pitaevskii方程研究相干耦合玻色气体非平衡凝聚过程中点状拓扑缺陷的普适空间统计，发现无论是基本缺陷还是复合缺陷（全量子涡旋），其空间分布均服从泊松点过程（Poisson point process），并通过Voronoi剖分（Voronoi tessellation）和空间形状因子（spatial form factor）进一步刻画了超越Kibble-Zurek机制（KZM）平均密度标度的普适随机几何特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越Kibble-Zurek机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism, KZM）仅预测平均缺陷密度的局限，探索相干耦合玻色气体在非平衡凝聚过程中拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的空间统计规律及其普适性。

Method: 采用随机投影Gross-Pitaevskii方程（stochastic projected Gross-Pitaevskii equation）模拟化学势线性淬灭驱动的对称性破缺相变；利用泊松点过程分析、Voronoi剖分以及空间形状因子（spatial form factor）等多种统计工具表征基本缺陷与复合缺陷的空间组织。

Result: 基本缺陷与复合缺陷（全量子涡旋，full quantum vortices）的位置均服从泊松点过程；Voronoi胞元面积统计符合Poisson-Voronoi预测；空间形状因子展现出特征性的dip-ramp-plateau结构。

Conclusion: 建立了一种超越传统Kibble-Zurek标度的拓扑缺陷普适随机几何（universal stochastic geometry），并将其识别为相干耦合玻色气体非平衡凝聚的一个基本特征。

Abstract: We study the universal spatial statistics of point-like topological defects formed during the nonequilibrium condensation of a coherently coupled Bose gas using the stochastic projected Gross-Pitaevskii equation. The symmetry-breaking transition is driven by a linear quench of the chemical potential, leading to stochastic vortex nucleation in the individual condensate components. When the two components are considered together, these elementary defects may combine across components to emerge as composite topological defects known as full quantum vortices. Beyond the mean defect density predicted by the Kibble-Zurek mechanism (KZM), we investigate the spatial organization of both the elementary and composite defects and show that their positions are well described by a Poisson point process, revealing a universal stochastic geometry. This universality is further described through Voronoi tessellation, whose cell-area statistics follow Poisson-Voronoi predictions. We also introduce the spatial form factor for characterizing the vortex configurations and demonstrate the emergence of a characteristic dip-ramp-plateau structure. Our results establish universal stochastic geometry of topological defects beyond conventional Kibble-Zurek scaling and identify it as a fundamental feature of nonequilibrium condensation in coherently coupled Bose gases.

</details>

### [87] [Hydrofluoric acid-free titanium etching for rare-event searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24524)
*P. Knights,I. Manthos,K. Nikolopoulos,G. Rogers,D. Spathara,P. Walters*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究提出使用硫酸（sulphuric acid）替代氢氟酸（hydrofluoric acid）对钛（titanium）进行化学蚀刻，以提升稀有事件探测实验（rare-event search experiments）中结构材料的安全性与可操作性。实验表明，硫酸在较低浓度和温度下也能有效蚀刻钛，并可能通过钝化层（passivation layer）的形成来控制总去除质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有事件探测实验对结构材料的放射性纯度（radiopurity）要求极高。钛因其力学强度高、密度低、可加工性好且商业可获得相对高纯形式，成为理想候选材料。然而，传统蚀刻钛所需的氢氟酸在深地实验室（deep underground laboratory）环境中存在严重的健康与安全隐患，亟需寻找替代方案。

Method: 采用Grade 1钛样品，分别在20%和40%的硫酸溶液中，于20°C和40°C温度下进行最多24小时的蚀刻实验。通过质量变化测量、表面粗糙度分析（surface roughness analysis）和扫描电子显微镜（scanning electron microscopy, SEM）对蚀刻效果进行量化表征。

Result: 在40%硫酸、40°C、24小时的静态溶液中，钛的蚀刻量可达3.5±0.3 mg/cm²。硫酸在较低浓度和温度下同样表现出有效的蚀刻能力。蚀刻过程中形成的钝化层可能有助于控制总去除质量。

Conclusion: 硫酸可作为传统氢氟酸的安全替代品，用于稀有事件探测实验中钛结构的蚀刻处理，且具备在温和条件下操作的可能性，并能通过钝化层机制实现蚀刻过程的控制。

Abstract: Rare-event search experiments require construction materials with high radiopurity to minimise background contributions. Thanks to its high mechanical strength, low density, machinability, and commercial availability in relatively radiopure forms, titanium is a suitable material for structural elements in rare-event searches. In such applications, a chemical etching stage is typically performed to remove surface contamination or to prepare the surface for further treatment. However, due to its chemical resistance, the etching of titanium conventionally requires hydrofluoric acid, posing serious health and safety concerns that are further exacerbated in deep underground laboratory settings. An alternative approach is proposed, which uses sulphuric acid. Grade 1 titanium samples were etched in 20\% and 40\% sulphuric acid solutions at 20$^\circ$C and 40$^\circ$C for up to 24\,h. The effects of etching were quantified through mass change measurements, surface roughness analysis, and scanning electron microscopy. Sulphuric acid effectively etches titanium, with up to $3.5\,\pm\,0.3$ mg/cm$^2$ of titanium removed for an unagitated solution of 40\% sulphuric acid at $40^\circ$C for 24\,h. Furthermore, sulphuric acid is shown to be effective at etching at lower concentration and temperature. The formation of a passivation layer during the etching may enable control of the total mass removed.

</details>

### [88] [Polarized Deep-Inelastic Scattering with Spin Correlations in Herwig 7](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23845)
*M. R. Masouminia,A. Papaefstathiou,P. Richardson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Herwig 7中实现了极化深度非弹性散射（polarized DIS）的次领头阶（NLO）处理，采用POWHEG匹配方案和自旋关联方法，并验证了自旋密度矩阵初始化对部分可观测量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的全排他蒙特卡罗模拟提供极化深度非弹性散射（polarized DIS）的精确理论处理，特别是实现次领头阶（NLO）水平的自旋关联效应。

Method: 在Herwig 7中实现POWHEG匹配方案下的极化DIS次领头阶（NLO）处理，包含中性流γ/Z交换和带电电流散射；通过从极化DIS玻恩过程（Born process）的自旋密度矩阵（spin-density matrix）初始化部分子簇射（shower），并传播接受的真实辐射过程（real-emission）的自旋密度矩阵，构建自旋关联处理。

Result: 积分截面与固定阶计算一致；玻恩级自旋密度初始化对簇射敏感可观测量有可见影响；但接受的真实辐射过程中的额外自旋信息对当前考虑的纵向极化可观测量没有可分辨的影响。

Conclusion: 所提出的自旋关联处理方法在NLO水平上可行，其中玻恩级自旋信息对部分可观测量重要，而真实辐射的自旋信息在纵向极化情形下可被忽略。

Abstract: We investigate polarized deep-inelastic scattering (DIS) in the context of fully exclusive Monte Carlo simulations for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). We present a next-to-leading-order (NLO) treatment of polarized DIS in Herwig 7 using the POWHEG matching scheme, including neutral-current $γ/Z$ exchange and charged-current scattering. We also construct a spin-correlation treatment for NLO-matched events, first by initializing the shower from the spin-density matrix of the polarized DIS Born process and then by propagating the spin-density matrix of the accepted real-emission configuration without changing the POWHEG event weight or hardest-emission choice. We validate the integrated cross sections against fixed-order calculations, use parton-level comparisons without subsequent shower evolution to isolate the accepted POWHEG real-emission kinematics, and employ shower-level observables to test the numerical importance of the Born-level and real-emission spin information. We find that the Born-level spin-density initialization can have a visible impact on shower-sensitive observables, while the additional spin information from the accepted real-emission configuration is not resolved for the longitudinally polarized observables considered here.

</details>


### [89] [Mapping jet substructure in heavy-ion collisions with track functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23971)
*João Barata,Yeonju Go,Daniel Pablos*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究重离子碰撞中高能QCD级联动力学，通过分析径迹函数（track functions）在夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中的标度演化，发现介质诱导的能量损失会显著改变喷注碎片化模式，且不同蒙特卡洛模型（JEWEL与HYBRID）给出的修正幅度存在差异，从而将径迹函数识别为能够区分喷注-介质相互作用微观图像的观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高能重离子碰撞中喷注（jet）在夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）中的碎片化行为，揭示介质效应对喷注子结构的修正机制。

Method: 采用径迹函数（track functions）描述从初始部分子（parton）到所有带电强子能量流的非微扰过程，利用重整化群（renormalization group, RG）分析其标度演化，并结合JEWEL与HYBRID两种蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）喷注淬火（jet quenching）模型进行数值模拟。

Result: 两种模型下径迹函数分布的高阶矩（higher moments）与累积量（cumulants）均偏离真空基线，证实介质诱导能量损失对碎片化模式的印记；两种模型之间的定量修正幅度存在显著差异；介质中领先矩的RG流与真空演化定性一致。

Conclusion: 径迹函数可作为区分不同喷注-介质相互作用微观图像的观测量，且RG流在QGP中的检验为将重离子喷注测量与量子场论（QFT）对部分子分支的基本理解相连接提供了途径。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of high-energy QCD cascades in heavy-ion collisions, focusing on modifications to jets' substructure induced by the presence of a quark-gluon plasma (QGP). To this end, we study the properties and scale evolution of track functions, non-perturbative objects encoding the flow of energy from an initiating parton to all charged hadrons. In contrast to the more standard fragmentation functions, these objects have a non-linear renormalization group (RG) evolution, being sensitive to the entire jet fragmentation process. Using the JEWEL and HYBRID Monte-Carlo models of jet quenching, we find that in both frameworks the higher moments and cumulants of the track functions' distributions exhibit sizable deviations from their vacuum baselines, demonstrating that medium-induced energy loss imprints itself in the in-medium jet fragmentation pattern. We find that the quantitative magnitude of these modifications differs significantly between the two models. This identifies track functions as a class of observables capable of discriminating between competing microscopic pictures of jet-medium interactions. We further examined the (in-medium) RG flows for the leading moments, which remain in qualitative agreement with the in-vacuum evolution. This provides an avenue to directly test the RG flows inside a QGP, linking heavy-ion jet measurements to basic QFT understanding of partonic branching. Finally, we comment on the feasibility and challenges associated with extracting track functions from experimental data.

</details>


### [90] [Bottom quark electroweak dipole moments at a high-energy $μ-$collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24410)
*D. Barducci*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT），研究了多TeV能区高能μ子对撞机（μ-碰撞器）探测b夸克电弱偶极相互作用（electroweak dipole interactions）的灵敏度，发现$μ^+μ^-\to b\bar{b}h$过程可对$d=6$算符的Wilson系数施加比当前及未来电弱精确测量和$B\to X_s\gamma$衰变更强的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架，将b夸克偶极相互作用的修正参数化为$d=6$阶算符的Wilson系数；对$μ^+μ^-\to b\bar{b}$和$μ^+μ^-\to b\bar{b}h$两种散射过程进行快速探测器模拟（fast detector simulation）水平的分析。

Result: 由于偶极相互作用的手征结构（chiral structure），$μ^+μ^-\to b\bar{b}h$过程能够对$d=6$算符的Wilson系数施加更强的约束。所得上限优于当前及未来电弱精确测量（EW precision measurements）的界限，并且也改进了由$ΔF=1$跃迁$B\to X_s\gamma$测量给出的限制。

Conclusion: 多TeV能区的高能μ子对撞机在约束b夸克电弱偶极相互作用方面具有显著的探测潜力，其中$μ^+μ^-\to b\bar{b}h$通道尤其有效，可为超越标准模型的新物理搜索提供更强约束。

Abstract: We study the sensitivity of a high-energy $μ-$collider with center of mass energy in the multi--TeV range in testing electroweak dipole interactions of the $b-$quark. We parametrize the relevant deformations in the language of the Standard Model effective field theory, where the dominant modifications arise at the $d=6$ level. We analyse $μ^+ μ^- \to b \bar b$ and $μ^+ μ^- \to b \bar b h$ scatterings, performing a study at the level of a fast detector simulation. Owing the chiral structure of the dipole interaction, the study of the $μ^+ μ^- \to b \bar b h$ process allows to enforce the stronger bounds on the Wilson coefficients of the $d=6$ operators. The limits that can be obtained surpass present and future bounds from EW precision measurements also improving upon the ones arising from the measurement of the $ΔF=1$ transitions $B\to X_sγ$.

### [91] [Disentangle RG Running Parameters with Medium-Baseline Reactor Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24560)
*Shao-Feng Ge,João Paulo Pinheiro,Shaoyang Qin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了重整化群（renormalization group）跑动对混合角和轻子CP相位的beta函数如何影响JUNO实验中的慢速和快速振荡模式，并指出JUNO-TAO近探测器可通过补充测量恢复中微子质量顺序（neutrino mass ordering）的灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究重整化群跑动对中微子振荡参数的影响，尤其是对JUNO实验中慢速和快速振荡模式的潜在干扰，以及这种干扰可能削弱质量顺序测量灵敏度的风险。

Method: 通过分析混合角和轻子CP相位的重整化群跑动beta函数，分别考察它们对慢速模式和快速模式的影响。慢速模式受太阳角beta函数（β_s）和Majorana CP相位beta函数（β_M1）修正；快速模式则受Dirac CP相位β_δD和Majorana CP相位β_δM3的修正。

Result: 慢速模式的振幅受太阳角beta函数影响，其相位受Majorana CP相位beta函数影响；快速模式受Dirac及Majorana CP相位beta函数修正。重整化群跑动效应会干扰快速模式对中微子质量顺序的测量灵敏度。JUNO-TAO近探测器可提供补充测量以恢复质量顺序灵敏度。

Conclusion: 重整化群跑动效应对JUNO实验中中微子质量顺序的测量构成潜在干扰，但通过JUNO-TAO近探测器的补充测量，有望恢复该灵敏度。

Abstract: We study how the renormalization group running beta functions of mixing angles and leptonic CP phases affect the slow and fast oscillation modes at JUNO. While the slow mode is modulated by the solar parameters, its amplitude can also be affected by the solar angle beta function $β_s$ and its phase by the Majorana CP phase counterpart $β_{\rm M1}$. On the other hand, the fast mode also receives corrections from the beta functions of the Dirac CP phase $δ_D$ and the Majorana CP phase $δ_{\rm M3}$. Since the fast mode is essentially the one measuring the neutrino mass ordering, the RG running effect can then interfere to deteriorate the sensitivity. Fortunately, the JUNO-TAO near detector can provide supplementary measurements of the RG running parameters to restore the mass ordering sensitivity.

### [92] [Analytic electromagnetic signatures of compact pentaquark structure: A multi-current QCD light-cone sum rules analysis of the $P_{ψs}^Λ$ states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24582)
*Ulaş Özdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出多流QCD光锥求和规则（LCSR）可作为区分隐粲五夸克态内部结构（紧致双重夸克-反夸克构型 vs. 松散强子分子）的诊断工具，通过轻夸克贡献比率μ_u/μ_d=-2和特定流J_3中粲贡献μ_c=0两个签名，给出了四个紧致五夸克态电流的磁矩预测，并与已有分子图像结果形成对比，为紧致图像提供了可检验的判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越质量谱，寻找能够区分紧致双重夸克-反夸克（diquark-diquark-antiquark）构型与松散束缚强子分子（hadronic molecule）的不依赖于态-流配对的观测签名。

Method: 采用多流QCD光锥求和规则（light-cone sum rules, LCSR），通过插值流代数（algebra of interpolating currents）导出味扇区间贡献的精确解析关系；对四个具有J^P=1/2^-的紧致双重夸克-反夸克电流J_1(x)-J_4(x)计算磁矩。

Result: 轻夸克贡献满足μ_u/μ_d=e_u/e_d=-2，反映共同的洛伦兹-色核（Lorentz-color kernel）；J_3电流中粲贡献μ_c=0由反粲耦合的狄拉克结构而非赝标量粲双重夸克嵌入单独导致。四个电流磁矩预测值分别为μ_{J1}=-1.35^{+0.35}_{-0.28} μ_N、μ_{J2}=3.14^{+0.65}_{-0.50} μ_N、μ_{J3}=1.01^{+0.25}_{-0.20} μ_N、μ_{J4}=-1.79^{+0.41}_{-0.34} μ_N，大小|μ|~1-3 μ_N高于夸克模型和重五夸克手征微扰理论预期（|μ|≲0.5 μ_N）。分子LCSR分析给出μ_u/μ_d=-1/2而非-2，可在味分解层面形成对比。

Conclusion: 两个签名（轻夸克比率和粲贡献消失）不受态-流配对影响，为紧致五夸克图像提供了可证伪的实验检验手段。

Abstract: Probing the internal organization of hidden-charm pentaquarks -- including the spin-color correlations that distinguish compact diquark-diquark-antiquark configurations from loosely bound hadronic molecules -- requires observables beyond mass spectroscopy. We argue that multi-current QCD light-cone sum rules (LCSR) provide a diagnostic framework through exact analytic relations among flavor-sector contributions enforced by the algebra of the interpolating currents. We identify two such signatures: (i) the light-quark contributions satisfy $μ_{u}/μ_{d}=e_{u}/e_{d}=-2$ in all four currents considered, reflecting a common Lorentz-color kernel; and (ii) for the $J_{3}(x)$ current the charm contribution vanishes identically, $μ_{c}=0$, from the Dirac structure of the anti-charm coupling rather than the pseudoscalar charm-diquark embedding alone. Using four diquark-diquark-antiquark currents $J_{1}(x)$-$J_{4}(x)$ with $J^{P}=\tfrac{1}{2}^{-}$, we obtain $μ_{J_{1}}=-1.35^{+0.35}_{-0.28}\,μ_{N}$, $μ_{J_{2}}=3.14^{+0.65}_{-0.50}\,μ_{N}$, $μ_{J_{3}}=1.01^{+0.25}_{-0.20}\,μ_{N}$, $μ_{J_{4}}=-1.79^{+0.41}_{-0.34}\,μ_{N}$. These predictions are paired with the $P_{ψs}^Λ(4338)$ and $P_{ψs}^Λ(4459)$ on mass grounds as a working hypothesis, since the $\pm 0.11~\text{GeV}$ uncertainties accommodate either state within $1σ$ of all four currents. The magnitudes $|μ|\sim 1$-$3\,μ_{N}$ lie above quark-model and heavy pentaquark chiral perturbation theory expectations ($|μ|\lesssim 0.5\,μ_{N}$). Applying the same procedure to two previous molecular LCSR analyses yields $μ_{u}/μ_{d}=-1/2$ rather than $-2$, providing an LCSR-internal contrast at the flavor-decomposed level even when total magnitudes are comparable. The two signatures are immune to the state-to-current pairing and offer falsifiable tests of the compact picture.

### [93] [From Magnetic to Inverse Magnetic Catalysis: The Interplay of Quark and Gluon Mass Generation in Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23736)
*Fei Gao,Kairen Huang,Yi Lu,Yuxin Liu*

TL;DR: 本文通过功能量子色动力学（functional QCD）框架分析磁场对夸克和胶子传播子的影响，发现磁场增强夸克质量并诱导胶子屏蔽质量（gluon screening mass）增加，后者抑制夸克-胶子相互作用，在相变附近主导并导致反磁催化（inverse magnetic catalysis）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究磁场在量子色动力学（QCD）框架下对夸克和胶子传播子的影响，特别是解析磁催化（magnetic catalysis）与反磁催化（inverse magnetic catalysis）之间的竞争机制。

Method: 采用功能QCD框架，通过求解夸克和胶子传播子的耦合戴森-施温格方程（Dyson-Schwinger equations）进行分析。

Result: 发现磁场增强夸克质量，导致手征凝聚（chiral condensate）的磁催化；同时磁场增加胶子屏蔽质量，抑制夸克-胶子相互作用，减弱动力学手征对称破缺（dynamical chiral symmetry breaking）强度。

Conclusion: 胶子屏蔽质量的增强在靠近手征相变（chiral phase transition）时占据主导地位，从而引发反磁催化效应。

Abstract: We analyze the effects of the magnetic field on the quark and gluon propagators within the functional QCD framework. By solving the coupled Dyson-Schwinger equations for the quark and gluon propagators, we find that the quark mass is generally enhanced in the presence of a magnetic field, leading to magnetic catalysis of the chiral condensate. Meanwhile, the magnetic field also induces an increase in the gluon screening mass. The enhancement of the gluon screening mass suppresses the quark-gluon interaction and thereby weakens the strength of dynamical chiral symmetry breaking, establishing a competing mechanism against magnetic catalysis. In particular, this enhancement of the gluon screening mass becomes dominant near the chiral phase transition, which in turn gives rise to inverse magnetic catalysis.

### [94] [Scalar diquarks in the QCD vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23772)
*Hosein Gholami,Ugo Mire,Fabian Rennecke,Bernd-Jochen Schaefer,Shi Yin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理，利用泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）中的动力学强子化（dynamical hadronization）技术，构建了从基本QCD到真空低能区域的过渡框架。该框架无需引入QCD以外的自由参数，即可自然得到有效模型中的低能常数（low-energy constants），包括π介子、σ介子和标量二夸克（scalar diquark）的动力学涌现性质，以及可用于约束双味色超导（two-flavor color superconducting）相模型的低能常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QCD在低能区呈现出丰富的非微扰（nonperturbative）结构，复合场成为相关自由度，但如何从基本QCD第一性原理出发描述这一过渡一直是一个挑战。本文旨在建立一个不需要引入额外自由参数的框架，将QCD低能区有效模型中的常数与基本QCD参数直接联系起来。

Method: 采用泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）方法，结合动力学强子化（dynamical hadronization）技术，在双味QCD框架下对真空中的低能动力学进行第一性原理计算。该框架使得有效质量和耦合强度等低能常数自然地从重整化群流（renormalization group flow）中涌现出来，无需引入QCD基本参数以外的自由参数。

Result: 研究了π介子、σ介子和标量二夸克（scalar diquark）在虚时和实时中的动力学涌现现象，确定了一组QCD低能常数。特别地，该结果包含了标量二夸克此前未知的性质，为约束双味色超导（two-flavor color superconducting）相提供了微观输入。

Conclusion: 该框架成功从QCD第一性原理出发获得了低能有效模型的关键参数，无需额外自由参数。所得结果对于约束色超导（color superconducting）相具有重要价值，而这一相在理解致密中子星物质中起着关键作用。

Abstract: While QCD fundamentally only depends on the values of the strong coupling and the quark masses, it exhibits a rich nonperturbative structure at low energies, where composite fields emerge as the relevant degrees of freedom. In this work, we present a first-principles framework that captures the transition from fundamental QCD to its low-energy sector in vacuum. It builds on the dynamical hadronization technique within the functional renormalization group approach to two-flavor QCD. In this framework, the low-energy constants relevant for effective models, including effective masses and coupling strengths, naturally emerge from the underlying renormalization group flow without introducing free parameters beyond those of QCD itself. We investigate the dynamical emergence of the pion, the $σ$-meson and the scalar diquark in both imaginary and real time, and determine a set of QCD low-energy constants which can be used to fix the free parameters of models of dense quark matter with a two-flavor color superconducting phase. In particular, this includes previously unknown properties of the scalar diquark. Our results provide important microscopic input for constraining color superconducting phases, which are expected to play a key role in our understanding of dense neutron star matter.

### [96] [From the Great Wave of Translation to the Force between Quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24052)
*Chris Quigg*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文回顾了从运河中偶然观测到的奇特行波出发，最终推导出KdV方程（Korteweg–de Vries equation）并发现孤子（soliton）的过程。孤子对应薛定谔方程中的无反射势（reflectionless potential），而多个孤子的组合可构造支持多个束缚态（bound state）的对称无反射势。利用KdV方程可求解束缚态集合的反散射问题（inverse scattering problem），进而为夸克偶素（quarkonium）谱构建无反射近似禁闭势，并检验夸克间相互作用的味无关性（flavor-independence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示孤子与无反射势之间的数学对应关系，并探讨如何利用KdV方程的反散射 formalism 为夸克偶素谱构建禁闭势的近似，从而检验夸克间相互作用的味无关性。

Method: 通过孤立孤子对应单个束缚态的无反射势，将多个孤子组合构造支持多个束缚态的对称无反射势；利用KdV方程建立束缚态集合的反散射问题求解路径，并将该形式体系（formalism）应用于夸克偶素谱分析。

Result: 该形式体系允许构建禁闭势的无反射近似，用于描述夸克之间的作用力，并检验夸克间相互作用的味无关性。

Conclusion: KdV方程及其对应的反散射问题为解决束缚态系统提供了有效数学工具，并在夸克偶素物理中具有实际应用价值，支持对夸克相互作用基本性质的检验。

Abstract: The chance observation of a novel traveling wave in a canal led over time to the formulation of a nonlinear wave equation -- the Korteweg--de Vries equation -- that describes strikingly robust disturbances now called solitons. The figure of an isolated soliton corresponds to a reflectionless potential that supports a single bound state in the one-dimensional Schrödinger equation. An appropriate combination of individual solitons yields a symmetric reflectionless potential that supports multiple bound states. Thus, the KdV equation opens the path to solving the inverse scattering problem for a collection of bound states. Applied to the quarkonium spectra, this formalism allows the construction of reflectionless approximations to the confining potentials that account for the force between quarks, and to tests of the flavor-independence of the interquark interaction.

### [97] [Neutrinoless double $β$ decay and leptogenesis in seesaw model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24109)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出Type I跷跷板模型中的费米子 ν_R + Cν̅_R^T 并非真正的马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermion），因此不会产生无中微子双β衰变（neutrinoless double β decay）；通过类比博戈留波夫变换（Bogoliubov transformation）定义C对称的马约拉纳费米子，可同时自然实现轻子生成（leptogenesis）与无中微子双β衰变。

Method: 基于d=4洛伦兹群表示中马约拉纳-外尔费米子（Majorana-Weyl fermion）不存在性定理进行论证，并引入类比博戈留波夫变换的方法重新定义C对称的马约拉纳费米子。

Result: Type I跷跷板模型中通常被视为马约拉纳费米子的 ν_R + Cν̅_R^T 并非真正的马约拉纳费米子，因此在 ν_L - Cν̅_L^T 情形下无中微子双β衰变不会发生；通过新定义可以同时实现轻子生成与无中微子双β衰变。

Conclusion: 在跷跷板模型中需要重新审视马约拉纳费米子的定义，而基于博戈留波夫变换的类比方法为同时解释轻子生成与无中微子双β衰变提供了可行的理论途径。

Abstract: The fermion $ν_{R}+C\overline{ν_{R}}^{T}$ in the Type I seesaw model, which is commonly identified with a Majorana fermion, is not a Majorana fermion and thus no neutrinoless double $β$ decay (in the case of $ν_{L}-C\overline{ν_{L}}^{T}$) due to the theorem on the absence of a Majorana-Weyl fermion in the representation of the d=4 Lorentz group. The leptogenesis is realized naturally together with the neutrinoless double $β$ decay by first defining C symmetric Majorana fermions in the seesaw model using an analogue of the Bogoliubov transformation.

</details>


### [98] [Second-order effective renormalized Hamiltonian of Quantum Chromodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24699)
*Kamil Serafin,Carter M. Gustin,Peter J. Love*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在哈密顿动力学的前沿形式（front form）下计算并重整化了量子色动力学（QCD）的有效哈密顿量，利用重整化群（renormalization group）方法处理到耦合常数的二阶。研究发现，在单色子（color singlet）子空间中，当胶子质量趋于零时没有发散，而非单色子子空间中出现对数发散，这源于自能项与胶子交换有效项之间的相互作用所产生的SU(3)卡西米尔算符（Casimir operator）对数项。最终的有效哈密顿量适用于经典或量子计算机上的非微扰数值计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在哈密顿动力学的前沿形式下构建一个经过适当重整化的QCD有效哈密顿量，以便用于非微扰计算，并探究胶子质量趋于零时该理论的奇异行为。

Method: 采用针对有效粒子的重整化群程序（renormalization group procedure for effective particles），计算到耦合常数的二阶；通过引入小胶子质量来调节红外奇点（infrared singularities）；通过计算有效哈密顿量的矩阵元来确定所需的抵消项（counterterms）。

Result: 有效哈密顿量在Fock空间的一个稠密子空间上具有定义良好的对称形式；在紫外重整化完成后，单色子子空间中胶子质量趋于零时未发现发散；自能项与胶子交换有效项的相互作用产生了正比于SU(3)卡西米尔算符乘以胶子质量对数的项，导致非单色子子空间矩阵元对数发散，而单色子子空间因卡西米尔算符为零而保持有限。

Conclusion: 本文构建的有效哈密顿量是良好定义的，并适用于经典计算机或量子计算机上的非微扰数值计算，为后续的QCD非微扰研究提供了可行的理论框架。

Abstract: The effective Hamiltonian of quantum chromodynamics in the front form of Hamiltonian dynamics is calculated and renormalized. The renormalization group procedure for effective particles up to the second order in the coupling constant is used. Small gluon mass is used to regulate infrared singularities of the theory. The counterterms necessary to renormalize the theory are determined by computing matrix elements of the effective Hamiltonian. The effective Hamiltonians are well-defined symmetric forms on a dense subspace of the Fock space. The zero modes are cut off but, once ultraviolet renormalization is performed, no divergences are found in the color singlet subspace in the limit of the gluon mass approaching zero. A major result is that the interplay between self-energy terms and gluon exchange effective terms generates a term proportional to the quadratic SU(3) Casimir operator times the logarithm of the gluon mass. Therefore, the matrix elements are logarithmically divergent in the color nonsinglet subspace, but finite in the color singlet subspace, because the Casimir operator vanishes in the color singlet subspace. The effective Hamiltonians are suitable for nonperturbative numerical calculations using either classical or quantum computers.

</details>

### [99] [Weyl orbit particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23887)
*Martin T. Luu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文展示了仿射Toda理论（affine Toda theory）的变体中，粒子质量谱与Weyl群（Weyl group）元素轨道的关系，并推广了原理论中与Cartan矩阵（Cartan matrix）的关联，最后以$D_{2n}(a_{n-1})$族为实例计算了经典质量谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仿射Toda理论的质量谱已知可由Cartan矩阵的特定特征向量表示，且粒子与Coxeter元素（Coxeter element）在根集（set of roots）中的轨道一一对应。近期出现了针对多种Weyl群元素的仿射Toda理论变体，需要将这些质量谱计算从Coxeter情形推广到更一般的Weyl群元素情形。

Method: 通过建立粒子与Weyl群元素在根集中轨道的对应关系，将经典质量谱的计算推广至非Coxeter情形，并以原始仿射Toda理论与Cartan矩阵的关系为基线，说明广义化形式。以复单李代数（complex simple Lie algebras）Weyl群中唯一的非Coxeter无限族$D_{2n}(a_{n-1})$（属于本原正则共轭类，primitive regular conjugacy classes）为例进行具体计算。

Result: 结果表明，这些广义质量谱计算确实推广了仿射Toda理论中与Cartan矩阵的经典关系。针对$D_{2n}(a_{n-1})$族的计算给出了相应的经典质量谱。

Conclusion: 该工作将仿射Toda理论的质量谱计算从Coxeter元素情形扩展到更广泛的Weyl群元素情形，为理解这些理论变体的粒子结构提供了统一的谱计算框架。

Abstract: The mass spectrum of affine Toda theory is known to be expressible in terms of a suitable eigenvector of the relevant Cartan matrix. The particles correspond in a precise manner to the Coxeter element orbits in the set of roots. Recently, variants of affine Toda theory have been constructed for many different Weyl group elements. Again, the particles correspond to orbits in the set of roots and this allows the calculation of the classical mass spectrum. We show how these spectral calculations generalize the affine Toda relation with the Cartan matrix. As an example, we calculate the spectrum for the unique non-Coxeter infinite family $\textrm{D}_{2n}(a_{n-1})$ of primitive regular conjugacy classes in the Weyl groups of complex simple Lie algebras.

</details>

### [101] [Typical geometry of self-repelling polymers in a constant force field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24352)
*Kamil Khettabi,Yvan Velenik*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究二维晶格上受恒力场作用的一类自排斥聚合物（包括简单随机游走、自回避行走和排斥性Domb-Joyce模型），在固定长度和端点条件下，证明了其典型轨迹指数级收敛于一个确定性的宏观形状，该形状由变分问题唯一极小元刻画，并可作为高度依赖的Finsler度量的测地线来解释；同时分析了小场强下接近经典悬链线和大场强下收敛于通用多边形形状的两种极限行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解受外力场作用的自排斥聚合物在约束条件下的宏观行为，特别是其自由能和典型轨迹的极限形状，并揭示小场强和大场强下的普适性特征。

Method: 采用变分法（variational method），将宏观形状刻画为某个变分问题的唯一极小元，并将其解释为高度依赖的Finsler度量（height-dependent Finsler metric）下的测地线（geodesic）；通过极限分析研究小场强和大场强下的渐近行为。

Result: 确定了聚合物在固定长度和端点下的极限自由能，并证明典型轨迹以指数概率集中于一个确定性的宏观形状；在小场强对称情形下，该形状接近经典悬链线（catenary）；在大场强下，收敛于由最近邻晶格约束决定的通用多边形形状。

Conclusion: 受恒力场作用的自排斥聚合物在宏观尺度上表现出确定性形状，该形状可通过变分问题和Finsler测地线统一刻画，且在不同场强下呈现普适的极限几何特征。

Abstract: We study a general class of self-repelling polymers on $\mathbb Z^2$, including the simple random walk, the self-avoiding walk and the repulsive Domb-Joyce model, in the presence of a constant force field acting on each monomer. Conditioning the polymer to have fixed length and fixed endpoints, we identify the limiting free energy and prove that typical trajectories concentrate exponentially near a deterministic macroscopic shape. This shape is characterized as the unique minimizer of a variational problem and can be interpreted as a geodesic of a height-dependent Finsler metric. We also analyze two limiting regimes with universal features: for small field strength, in the symmetric case, the geodesic is close to a classical catenary, while for large field strength it converges to a universal polygonal shape governed by the nearest-neighbor lattice constraint.

### [102] [Morse momentum wavefunctions and rational functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24401)
*Luc Vinet,Alexei Zhedanov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在动量表象中重新审视了Morse势的束缚态，发现其动量波函数满足二阶差分算子的本征方程，可被识别为Koepf与Masjed-Jamei提出的有限双正交有理函数（finite biorthogonal rational functions）的对称特例，并具有有理双谱性（rational bispectrality）和R_{II}型系统结构；通过极点提取，这些波函数还可表示为参数依赖阶数的Meixner-Pollaczek多项式，从而给出了零点分布的简洁描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在动量表象中重新考察Morse势的束缚态波函数，揭示其与双正交有理函数及有理双谱性（rational bispectrality）等数学结构的深层联系。

Method: 提取基态因子后，利用动量变量的有限有理函数（rational functions）构造波函数；分析其作为二阶差分算子本征函数的性质，将其识别为Koepf与Masjed-Jamei有限双正交有理函数（finite biorthogonal rational functions）的对称特例；研究其关于度变量的广义本征值问题（generalized eigenvalue problem），并提取极点以转化为Meixner-Pollaczek多项式形式。

Result: Morse势的动量波函数满足二阶差分方程，属于有限双正交有理函数的对称特例；它们同时满足关于度变量的广义本征值问题，从而纳入有理双谱性（rational bispectrality）与R_{II}型系统框架；极点提取后，波函数可等价表示为具有度依赖参数的Meixner-Pollaczek多项式，由此获得零点分布的简单刻画。

Conclusion: Morse势提供了有限双正交有理函数（finite biorthogonal rational functions）的具体量子力学实现，并展示了其在动量表象中与差分算子和正交多项式理论的自然联系。

Abstract: We revisit the bound states of the Morse potential in the momentum representation. After the ground-state factor is extracted, the remaining factors are finite rational functions of the momentum variable. These functions are eigenfunctions of a second-order difference operator and are identified with the symmetric specialization of a finite family of biorthogonal rational functions introduced by Koepf and Masjed-Jamei. They also satisfy a generalized eigenvalue problem in the degree variable, thereby placing the Morse momentum wavefunctions within the framework of rational bispectrality and $R_{II}$-type systems. Finally, after extraction of their poles, the same wavefunctions are expressed in terms of Meixner--Pollaczek polynomials with degree-dependent parameters. This gives a simple description of their zeros. The Morse potential thus provides a concrete quantum-mechanical realization of finite biorthogonal rational functions.

### [103] [On the Berry-Keating Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24405)
*Fabio Bagarello,Sergiusz Kużel*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了Berry-Keating算符（Berry-Keating operator, $H_{BK}$）的两种互补视角——希尔伯特空间视角（Hilbertian viewpoint）与分布论视角（distributional approach），以探讨其与黎曼假设（Riemann hypothesis）之间尚未完全解决的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Berry-Keating算符与黎曼假设之间的深层联系至今仍未被充分理解，尽管近期文献已给予大量关注。本文旨在通过两种不同视角对该算符进行重新审视，以弥合理解上的缺口。

Method: 第一种方法采用纯希尔伯特空间（purely Hilbertian）的视角，基于膨胀算符（dilation operators）和梅林变换（Mellin transform）进行分析。第二种方法采用分布论（distributional）方法，聚焦于阶梯算符（ladder operators）、广义本征态（generalized eigenstates）以及广义相干态（generalized coherent states）。

Result: 两种视角被证明具有某种互补性，为理解Berry-Keating算符的结构及其与黎曼假设的可能联系提供了不同层面的数学工具。

Conclusion: Berry-Keating算符与黎曼假设的关系仍是一个开放问题，本文提出的两种互补视角为后续研究提供了新的分析框架。

Abstract: We review here two different viewpoints on the Berry-Keating operator $H_{BK}$, whose connection to the Riemann hypothesis remains an intriguing and not yet fully understood question, despite considerable attention in the recent literature. In particular, we propose two somehow complementary views to $H_{BK}$: the first is based on a purely Hilbertian point of view, on dilation operators and on the Mellin transform. The second is a distributional approach, with a specific view to ladder operators, generalized eigenstates of $H_{BK}$, and generalized coherent states.

</details>


### [104] [A symmetry reduction of the Painlevé IV hierarchy to the Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24662)
*Mohamad Alameddine,Olivier Marchal*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，与偶数阶 Painlevé IV 层级相关的等单值形变问题，在施加一个对称性约化后，可精确映射到 Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II 层级，从而为后者提供了一种几何解释——等单值形变问题的对称性约化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连接两种 Painlevé 层级（偶数阶 Painlevé IV 与 Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II），为 Flaschka-Newell 层级建立来自等单值形变问题的几何解释，以补充其经典上作为修正 KdV 层级相似性约化的代数描述。

Method: 考虑黎曼球面上具有一个正则奇点和一个无穷远处偶数阶奇点（对应偶数 Painlevé IV 层级）的秩二亚纯联络（rank-two meromorphic connection）的等单值形变（isomonodromic deformation）。施加对称性 $Ψ(-λ)= σ_1 Ψ(λ) σ_1$，证明该对称性定义了一个不变子流形，其诱导的等单值动力学与 Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II 层级一致，并且两种层级下的 Lax 矩阵、达布坐标（Darboux coordinates）和哈密顿结构可以显式匹配。

Result: Flaschka-Newell 层级第一个成员的哈密顿量可以从偶数 Painlevé IV 层级中直接恢复；两种层级之间的 Lax 矩阵、达布坐标和哈密顿结构实现了精确对应。

Conclusion: 本文为 Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II 层级提供了等单值形变问题对称性约化的几何解释，从而在几何框架下将其与偶数阶 Painlevé IV 层级统一起来。

Abstract: We study the isomonodromic deformation problem associated with rank-two meromorphic connections on the Riemann sphere having one regular singularity and one irregular singularity of even order at infinity, corresponding to the even Painlevé IV hierarchy. We show that the symmetry $Ψ(-λ)= σ_1 Ψ(λ) σ_1$ defines an invariant submanifold whose induced isomonodromic dynamics coincides with the Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II hierarchy. Under this identification, the corresponding Lax matrices, Darboux coordinates and Hamiltonian structures can be matched explicitly. In particular, the Hamiltonians of the first members of the Flaschka-Newell hierarchy are recovered from the even Painlevé IV hierarchy. This provides a geometric interpretation of the Flaschka-Newell hierarchy as a symmetry reduction of an isomonodromic deformation problem, complementing its classical description as a similarity reduction of the modified Korteweg-de Vries hierarchy.

</details>

### [106] [Data-Based Dynamical Systems Reconstruction: An Adequacy/Reliability Test](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24873)
*Guillermo Capobianco,Ulises Chialva,Horacio G. Rotstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了从含噪数据中重建随机系统（stochastic system）的验证问题，指出现有基于损失函数或确定性动力学（deterministic dynamics）重建标准指标的局限性，并提出一种基于两步检验的探索性方法，该法不依赖任意误差容忍阈值；同时讨论了系统简并性（degeneracy）、不可辨识性（non-identifiability）及随机动力学固有特征对该方法的应用限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对从含噪数据中重建随机系统的验证方法存在不足：仅依赖损失函数（loss function）或适用于确定性动力学重建的标准指标（standard metrics）具有局限性，因此需要一种不依赖于任意误差容忍阈值（error-tolerance thresholds）的通用评估手段。

Method: 提出一种探索性方法（exploratory approach），基于两步检验（two-step test）对重建效果进行总体评估，该方法无需设定人为的误差容忍阈值。

Result: 两步检验方法为随机系统重建提供了一种更通用的验证途径，摆脱了对损失函数和确定性指标的传统依赖。

Conclusion: 系统简并性（degeneracy）与不可辨识性（non-identifiability）以及随机动力学（stochastic dynamics）的内在特征会对两步检验方法的应用施加一定约束，即该方法并非无条件适用。

Abstract: In this work, we address the problem of validating the reconstruction of a stochastic system from noisy data. We demonstrate the limitations of criteria based solely on the loss function or on standard metrics used for reconstructing deterministic dynamics. We also propose an exploratory approach, based on a two-step test, which allows for a general assessment of the reconstruction without relying on arbitrary error-tolerance thresholds. However, we discuss how system degeneracy and non-identifiability, together with features intrinsic to stochastic dynamics, impose certain constraints on the application of this test.

</details>

### [107] [Chiralization of Quiver Varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23807)
*Ioana Coman,Myungbo Shim,Masahito Yamazaki,Yehao Zhou*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文针对带箭图（quiver）Q及其规范维数v和标架维数w，定义了扩展箭图簇（extended quiver variety）并构造了两种手征化（chiralize）该几何的顶点代数（vertex algebra）：一是通过量化射束（jet bundle）构造的顶点超代数层（sheaf of vertex superalgebras），二是通过BRST约化βγbc系统与海森堡顶点算子代数（Heisenberg VOA）的构造，并证明了二者之间存在自然的代数映射。在特定技术假设下，还证明了负度数BRST上同调为零以及该映射是单射。在物理上，该顶点超代数与H-扭曲三维N=4箭图规范理论（quiver gauge theory）的边界顶点算子代数（boundary VOA）密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为扩展箭图簇这一几何对象建立对应的手征代数结构，以从顶点代数（vertex algebra）的角度理解其几何性质，并探索其在三维N=4超对称规范理论（supersymmetric gauge theory）边界顶点算子代数（boundary VOA）中的物理体现。

Method: 首先，在扩展箭图簇上构造一个ħ-adic顶点超代数层，该层量化了扩展箭图簇的射束（jet bundle），并通过取全局截面（global sections）的C×-有限部分的ħ=1特化定义顶点代数。其次，对与箭图关联的βγbc系统和海森堡顶点算子代数（Heisenberg VOA）的张量积进行BRST约减（BRST reduction），定义另一个顶点超代数。最后，在两种构造之间建立自然的顶点超代数映射，并在技术假设下证明负度数BRST上同调（cohomology）为零以及映射为单射（injective）。

Result: 成功构造了两种与扩展箭图簇相关的顶点超代数，并证明了二者之间存在自然的代数映射。在技术假设下，证明了βγbc系统与海森堡VOA张量积的负度数BRST上同调为零；在更强假设下，证明了上述映射为单射。

Conclusion: 所构造的两种顶点超代数从代数和几何两个角度手征化了扩展箭图簇的结构，且代数映射的单射性表明了两种构造之间的一致性。物理上，该顶点超代数与H-扭曲三维N=4箭图规范理论的边界VOA紧密相关，为理解该理论的边界代数结构提供了数学基础。

Abstract: Given a quiver Q with gauge dimension $\bf v$ and framing dimension $\bf w$, one can define the extended quiver variety $\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$, which is a smooth family of deformations of the Nakajima quiver variety $\mathcal M(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$. In this paper we discuss two vertex algebras which chiralize the geometry $\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$. We construct a sheaf of $\hbar$-adic vertex superalgebras $\mathscr D^{\mathrm{ch}}_{\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w),\hbar}$ on $\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$ which quantizes the jet bundle of $\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$, and define a vertex algebra $\mathsf D^{\mathrm{ch}}(\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w))$ to be the $\hbar=1$ specialization of the $\mathbb C^{\times}$-finite part of the vector space of global sections $Γ(\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w), \mathscr D^{\mathrm{ch}}_{\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w),\hbar})$. We define another vertex superalgebra $\mathcal V(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$ by BRST reduction of the tensor product of the $βγbc$-system and Heisenberg VOA associated to the quiver Q, and show that there exists a natural vertex superalgebra map from $\mathcal V(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$ to $\mathsf D^{\mathrm{ch}}(\widetilde{\mathcal M}(\mathbf v,\mathbf w))$. Under certain technical assumptions, we prove that the negative degree BRST cohomologies of the tensor product of $βγbc$-systems and Heisenberg VOA associated to the quiver Q are zero, and under stronger assumptions, that the aforementioned vertex superalgebra map is injective.
  Physically, the vertex superalgebra $\mathcal V(\mathbf v,\mathbf w)$ is closely related to the boundary VOA of the H-twisted 3D $\mathcal N=4$ quiver gauge theory associated to the quiver Q with gauge and framing dimension vectors $\bf v$ and $\bf w$.

</details>

### [108] [Field-like Perturbation Enabled Six-state Readout in Triaxial $α$-$\mathrm{Fe}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{3}$|Pt Bi-layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23714)
*Aditya A. Wagh,Shwetha G. Bhat,Krishna Jha,Aiswarya Sukumaran,P. S. Anil Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在倾斜反铁磁（canted antiferromagnetic）α-Fe₂O₃|Pt双层膜中实现了六态存储的读取。通过静态类场微扰打破自旋霍尔磁电阻（SMR）读出中180°简并态的限制，并结合双调制SMR测量抑制热漂移，最终提出一种仅依赖电流的两步协议完成六态读出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解电流诱导的自旋轨道转矩（spin-orbit torques）为实现反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）序的全电控制提供了途径。然而，传统自旋霍尔磁电阻（spin Hall magnetoresistance, SMR）读出无法区分180°分离的态，在α-Fe₂O₃中仅能分辨三个态，限制了多态存储的应用。

Method: 采用α-Fe₂O₃|Pt双层膜体系，利用面外三轴各向异性（easy-plane triaxial anisotropy）稳定六态记忆。通过外加静态类场微扰（field-like perturbation）打破易面内相反态的简并性，结合同时施加电流与场激励的双调制SMR（dual-modulation SMR）测量抑制热漂移，并利用解析与数值模拟以及二次谐波SMR计算分析微观机制。

Result: 静态类场微扰可在一次谐波SMR信号中明确分辨所有六个态。双调制SMR有效抑制热漂移，确保读出可靠性。二次谐波SMR计算揭示了竞争相互作用（competing interactions）对解除相反态简并的关键作用。

Conclusion: 提出了一种仅依赖电流的两步协议（two-step current-only protocol），可在倾斜反铁磁α-Fe₂O₃|Pt双层膜中实现完整的六态读出。

Abstract: Understanding current-induced spin-orbit torques provides a route for all-electrical control of antiferromagnetic (AFM) order. Here, we demonstrate the reading of six-state memory stabilized by easy-plane triaxial anisotropy in canted antiferromagnetic $α$-$\mathrm{Fe}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{3}$|Pt bilayers. The conventional spin Hall magnetoresistance (SMR) readout cannot distinguish states separated by $180^\circ$, limiting detection to only three states in $α$-$\mathrm{Fe}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{3}$. We show that a static field-like perturbation via external field lifts the degeneracy of opposite states in $α$-$\mathrm{Fe}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{3}$, enabling unambiguous resolution of all six states in the first-harmonic SMR signal. Our analytical and numerical modeling elucidate the role of spontaneous canting in lifting such degeneracy in $α$-$\mathrm{Fe}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{3}$. We demonstrate that dual-modulation SMR measurements (simultaneous current and field excitations) are effective in mitigating thermal drifts in the signals and are essential for reliable readout. Furthermore, our computations of the second-harmonic SMR reveal the interplay of competing interactions governing the decisive lifting of the degeneracy of opposite states. Finally, we propose a two-step current-only protocol for six-state readout in canted AFM $α$-$\mathrm{Fe}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{3}$|Pt bilayers.

</details>


### [109] [Visualizing Symmetry Broken Chern Insulators and their Quantum Melting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23795)
*Minhao He,Yen-Chen Tsui,Ran Peng,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Oskar Vafek,Ali Yazdani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）在双层石墨烯与六方氮化硼（hBN）对齐的莫尔超晶格体系中，直接观测到了Hofstadter能谱中的相互作用驱动的对称性破缺陈绝缘体（Chern insulator），并揭示了Hofstadter态在分数填充下的相变与量子熔化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在磁场下，莫尔量子材料（moiré quantum materials）的电子态会形成Hofstadter能谱，为研究能带拓扑（band topology）与强电子-电子相互作用（strong electron-electron interaction）之间的相互作用提供了独特平台。本文旨在通过实验手段直接观测并解析这一过程中的对称性破缺与拓扑相变。

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）对与六方氮化硼（hexagonal BN）对齐的双层石墨烯（bilayer graphene）进行测量，直接可视化Hofstadter态及其在分数填充条件下的行为。

Result: 在Hofstadter能带的分数填充（fractional filling）下，观测到莫尔原胞（moiré unit cell）发生加倍、三倍或四倍化的相，以及具有复杂原胞内波函数（intra-unit-cell wave functions）的态。进一步在两种不同的陈数态（Chern states）中，分别可视化了两类量子现象：一是由拓扑缺陷（topological defects）出现与增殖驱动的量子熔化（quantum melting），二是与相竞争（phase competition）和相分离（phase separation）共存的量子转变（quantum transition）。

Conclusion: 实验结果证实了相互作用驱动的对称性破缺陈绝缘体在Hofstadter能谱中的形成，揭示了拓扑缺陷与相分离在量子相变中的关键角色，深化了对莫尔体系中拓扑与强关联相互作用耦合机制的理解。

Abstract: In the presence of a magnetic field, electronic states of moiré quantum materials develop a Hofstadter spectrum that provides a unique setting for studying the interplay between band topology and strong electron-electron interaction. Using scanning tunneling microscopy, we study Hofstadter's states in bilayer graphene aligned with hexagonal BN and directly visualize the formation of interaction-driven symmetry breaking Chern insulators. Our measurements reveal the formation of phases that double, triple or quadruple the moiré unit cell at fractional filling of the Hofstadter bands, as well as states with complex intra-unit-cell wave functions. We visualize two distinct quantum phenomena in different Chern states, including quantum melting driven by the appearance and proliferation of topological defects, and a quantum transition co-occurring with phase competition and separation.

</details>


### [110] [Fine structure of the cyclotron resonance in heterobilayers of proximitized graphene and transition metal dichalcogenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23895)
*M. A. Rakitskii,K. S. Denisov,N. S. Averkiev*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文理论分析了单层石墨烯与过渡金属硫族化物（TMDs）异质双层中，由邻近效应（proximity effect）诱导的自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）对狄拉克电子回旋共振（cyclotron resonance）吸收谱的影响，揭示了双峰结构、自旋翻转吸收等磁光响应特征，并给出了相应的选择定则与微扰理论分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯本身自旋-轨道耦合很弱，但通过与过渡金属硫族化物（TMDs）等范德瓦尔斯（vdW）材料邻近化，可以增强其自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）。作者旨在理论分析这种邻近诱导自旋相互作用对异质双层中狄拉克电子在量子化磁场下的回旋共振（CR）吸收行为的影响，包括自旋-赝自旋拉什巴耦合（spin-pseudospin Rashba coupling）的作用。

Method: 通过求解邻近诱导自旋相互作用下的朗道能级（Landau levels）自旋纹理波函数，计算磁光吸收谱，并结合微扰理论（perturbation theory）分析吸收跃迁的选择定则（selection rules）。

Result: 揭示了主带间回旋共振（CR）跃迁中出现的精细双峰结构（fine double-peak structure），以及位于不同共振频率的自旋翻转吸收——即组合回旋共振（combined cyclotron resonance, CCR）。明确了CCR的选择定则，并讨论了吸收的偏振依赖性与邻近诱导的磁光响应。

Conclusion: 理论阐明了邻近诱导自旋相互作用对狄拉克电子回旋共振的影响机制，并指出了实验验证的可能途径。

Abstract: A monolayer graphene and its Dirac electrons can be equipped with an enhanced spin-orbit coupling (SOC) when proximitized by other van der Waals (vdW) materials, such as transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs). In this work we analyze the cyclotron resonance (CR) absorption of such heterobilayers at quantizing magnetic fields in the presence of proximity-induced spin interactions, including the spin-pseudospin Rashba coupling. We evaluate the spin-textured wave functions of the Landau levels and calculate the absorption spectrum paying special attention to its spin proximity induced modifications. We reveal the formation of a fine double-peak structure of the main interband CR transitions, as well as the presence of additional spin-flip absorption, the combined cyclotron resonance (CCR), centered at different resonant frequencies. The selection rules for CCRs are identified and complemented by the perturbation theory analysis. We also discuss the polarization dependence of the absorption and the proximity-induced emerging magneto-optical responses. Our theory explains the effect of proximity-induced spin interactions for Dirac electrons cyclotron resonance and points out at its experimental verifications.

</details>


### [111] [Generalized Fourier's law in mesoscopic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23909)
*Luciano C. Lapas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种热力学自洽的广义傅里叶定律，将热导率提升为非局域记忆算子，并通过结合介观非平衡热力学与Mori–Kubo–Zwanzig投影算子形式，定量解释了时域热反射实验中观测到的表观热导率抑制现象，为非扩散热输运提供了双通道弹道/扩散图像的热力学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当能量载子的平均自由程（mean free path）与温度场变化的时空尺度相当时，经典的傅里叶定律（Fourier's law）失效。因此需要推导一个热力学自洽的广义形式，以正确描述这种非扩散（nondiffusive）热输运行为。

Method: 将介观非平衡热力学（mesoscopic nonequilibrium thermodynamics）与Mori–Kubo–Zwanzig投影算子形式（projection-operator formalism）相结合，把热导率提升为一个非局域记忆算子 $\bmκ_{\mathrm{eff}}(\mathbf{k},ω)$。Onsager核（Onsager kernel）被精确分解为振动简正模（vibrational normal modes）的张量和，权重为玻色热容（Bose heat capacity）与弛豫函数（relaxation function），并内禀满足热力学第二定律。

Result: 两个关键结果：(1) 由于模式权重携带方向性群速度，Onsager核是各向异性的，即使名义上的各向同性晶体也会表现出方向依赖的表观热导率 $Λ_z\neqΛ_r$；(2) 在泵浦-探测（pump–probe）实验中，调制频率并不引入时间记忆，而是通过热穿透深度（thermal penetration depth）设定探测波矢，因此时域热反射测量中观察到的表观热导率抑制本质上是空间非局域性（spatial-nonlocality）效应，由亚微米尺度的载子平均自由程决定。对Si、Ge和Si$_{1-x}$Ge$_x$数据的拟合给出非局域长度（nonlocality length）为0.25–0.4 μm，与这些晶体的平均自由程谱一致。

Conclusion: 该框架为非扩散热输运中的双通道弹道/扩散图像（ballistic/diffusive picture）提供了热力学基础，表明在亚微米尺度下热输运行为主要由空间非局域性而非时间记忆效应主导。

Abstract: Fourier's law fails when the mean free path of the energy carriers becomes comparable to the length and time scales over which the temperature field varies. We derive a thermodynamically consistent generalization in which the conductivity is promoted to a nonlocal memory operator $\bmκ_{\mathrm{eff}}(\mathbf{k},ω)$, obtained by combining mesoscopic nonequilibrium thermodynamics with the Mori--Kubo--Zwanzig projection-operator formalism. The Onsager kernel decomposes exactly into a tensor sum over vibrational normal modes weighted by their Bose heat capacities and relaxation functions, and satisfies the second law by construction. Two consequences follow. First, because the modal weights carry the directional group velocity, the kernel is anisotropic, so a nominally isotropic crystal exhibits direction-dependent apparent conductivities $Λ_z\neqΛ_r$. Second, in a pump--probe experiment the modulation frequency does not introduce temporal memory but sets the probed wavevector through the thermal penetration depth, so the suppression of the apparent conductivity measured by time-domain thermoreflectance on Si, Ge and Si$_{1-x}$Ge$_x$ is a spatial-nonlocality effect set by a sub-micron carrier mean free path. Fitting the data of Wilson and Cahill yields nonlocality lengths of $0.25$--$0.4~μ$m consistent with the mean-free-path spectra of these crystals. The framework supplies a thermodynamic foundation for the two-channel ballistic/diffusive picture of nondiffusive heat transport.

</details>


### [112] [Andreev exceptional points in Josephson junctions formed by minimal Kitaev chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23956)
*Jorge Cayao,Masatoshi Sato*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究由两条最小Kitaev链（minimal Kitaev chain）构成的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction），发现非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）与超导相位差（superconducting phase difference）的相互作用可实现厄米体系（Hermitian realm）中不存在的稳定拓扑态，包括Andreev异常点（exceptional point）与异常线（exceptional line），并可通过电导信号进行探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非厄米性与超导相位差在最小Kitaev链约瑟夫森结中的协同效应，以在开放系统中实现厄米框架下无法获得的稳定拓扑态。

Method: 将最小Kitaev链约瑟夫森结耦合至正常储库（normal reservoir）以引入非厄米性，得到复值Andreev谱（complex Andreev spectrum）；分析该谱中由超导相位差控制的二阶异常点（second order exceptional point）及其形成的异常线；通过调节系统参数（如格点势能、非厄米性、电子共隧穿）研究零实部能量区域的拓扑保护。

Result: 非厄米性的空间非均匀分布使Andreev异常点可在零能或有限能处出现，并连接受非厄米拓扑保护（non-Hermitian topology）的稳定能量线；调节参数可使异常点扩展为异常线，包围受保护的二维零实部能量区域。

Conclusion: 来自正常储库的非厄米性可作为工程化非厄米拓扑相（non-Hermitian topological phase）的有效资源，在最小Kitaev链约瑟夫森结中具有潜在探测方案（局域与非局域电导信号）。

Abstract: We consider Josephson junctions formed by two minimal Kitaev chains and investigate how the interplay between non-Hermiticity and superconducting phase difference enables the realization of stable topological states that do not exist in the Hermitian realm. In particular, we focus on non-Hermiticity produced by coupling the minimal Kitaev chain Josephson junction to normal reservoirs, which renders the system open and characterized by a complex Andreev spectrum. Interestingly, we find that this complex spectrum hosts second order exceptional points, where a pair of eigenvalues and their respective eigenvectors coalesce, and are fully controlled by the superconducting phase difference. Depending on the spatial unequal distribution of non-Hermiticity, these Andreev exceptional points can appear at zero or finite energies connecting stable energy lines protected by non-Hermitian topology. Moreover, tuning the system parameters, such as onsite energies, non-Hermiticity, or electron cotunneling, the Andreev exceptional points give rise to Andreev exceptional lines enclosing protected two-dimensional zero real energy areas. We also discuss potential detection schemes of Andreev exceptional points by using local and nonlocal conductance signatures. Our results demonstrate the utility of non-Hermiticity from normal reservoirs as a useful resource for engineering non-Hermitian topological phases in minimal Kitaev chain Josephson junctions.

</details>


### [113] [Observation of even-denominator fractional quantum Hall states at $ν= 3/4$ and 5/4 in the lowest Landau level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23990)
*Siddharth Kumar Singh,Chengyu Wang,Adbhut Gupta,Kirk W. Baldwin,Loren N. Pfeiffer,Mansour Shayegan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究报告在超高质量72.5纳米宽GaAs量子阱中，于最低朗道能级（N=0）填充因子ν=3/4和5/4处发现了新的偶分母分数量子霍尔态（FQHSs）。这些态在密度升高、层间隧穿减弱且二维电子系统变为双组分时出现，对电荷分布对称性极为敏感，可通过Scarola-Jain双组分复合费米子框架（推广的Halperin Ψ331态）加以解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宽GaAs量子阱中的二维电子系统（2DES）因具有双层电荷分布和显著的层间隧穿，为研究奇异的分数量子霍尔态（FQHSs）提供了独特平台。通过精确控制2DES密度可在宽范围内调节层间隧穿，从而探索此前未知的偶分母FQHSs。

Method: 在72.5纳米宽的GaAs量子阱中制备超高质量的二维电子系统（2DES），通过调节密度改变层间隧穿强度，并监测填充因子ν=3/4和5/4附近FQHSs的行为变化。同时，通过改变双层电荷分布的对称性（不对称度仅约2%）测试这些态的双组分特性。

Result: 在最低朗道能级（N=0）的填充因子ν=3/4和5/4处发现了新的偶分母FQHSs。当密度升高使层间隧穿充分降低、2DES变为双组分时，基态从复合费米子费米海（composite fermion Fermi sea）演化为FQHSs。ν=3/4和5/4的FQHSs对电荷分布不对称性极其敏感，不对称度仅约2%即导致其迅速消失。

Conclusion: ν=3/4和5/4的FQHSs可通过Scarola-Jain双组分复合费米子框架（推广的双组分Halperin Ψ331态）自然解释，两者由粒子-空穴对称性（particle-hole symmetry）相互关联。实验结果阐明了宽量子阱中竞争的能量尺度和长度尺度在稳定新基态中的关键作用。

Abstract: Two-dimensional electron systems (2DESs) confined to wide GaAs quantum wells provide a unique platform to study exotic fractional quantum Hall states (FQHSs) because the 2DES has a bilayer charge distribution with significant interlayer tunneling. Precise control over the 2DES density allows the tuning of the interlayer tunneling over a wide range. Here, we present our discovery of new even-denominator FQHSs in the lowest Landau level (orbital index \textit{N} = 0) at filling factors $ν= 3/4$ and 5/4 in an ultrahigh-quality 2DES confined to a 72.5-nm-wide GaAs quantum well. The ground states at $ν= 3/4$ and 5/4 both evolve from composite fermion Fermi seas to FQHSs as the density is raised so that interlayer tunneling is sufficiently reduced and the 2DES becomes two-component, signaled by the behavior of the FQHSs flanking $ν= 3/4$ and 5/4. The two-component nature of the $ν=3/4$ and 5/4 FQHSs is also evident from their extreme sensitivity to the bilayer charge distribution symmetry: both states disappear quickly when the charge distribution is made asymmetric by only $\simeq 2\%$. We find a natural explanation for the 3/4 and 5/4 FQHSs in terms of two states linked by particle-hole symmetry, and using the Scarola-Jain bilayer composite fermion framework which is a generalization of the well-known, two-component, Halperin state ($Ψ_{331}$ state). Our observations elucidate the crucial role of competing energy and length scales in wide quantum wells in stabilizing new ground states.

</details>


### [114] [Gate-Controlled Spin Qubits in Confined Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24150)
*Hamed Vakili*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出在静电限域的交替磁性（altermagnetic）量子点中构建栅极定义的自旋量子比特（gate-defined spin qubits）。通过椭圆限域d波交替磁结构，实现了低能自旋极化二重态；即使无自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），相控四极栅极驱动即可实现单比特X门旋转；进一步扩展到双量子点，通过共振调控势垒可驱动两比特接近最大纠缠态，表明各向异性交替磁量子点为无需自旋轨道耦合的局域栅控自旋量子比特提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自旋量子比特通常依赖自旋轨道耦合或外加磁场来实现操控，增加了器件复杂度和退相干风险。探索一种无需自旋轨道耦合、仅通过局域电栅极调控即可实现量子比特操作的新型体系，是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 采用静电限域手段在d波交替磁性结构（d-wave altermagnetic structure）中形成椭圆量子点（elliptical confinement），利用交替磁序产生低能自旋极化二重态。通过相控四极栅极驱动（phase-controlled quadrupolar gate drive）共振调制限域各向异性，实现单比特旋转；对于双量子比特情形，则通过共振调控中央势垒（resonant central-barrier modulation）驱动逻辑两比特分量逼近最大纠缠态。

Result: 在所用参数范围内，量子比特态能隙位于微波（microwave）波段，而泄漏能隙（leakage gap）维持在meV量级。无自旋轨道耦合条件下，时域模拟表明四极栅极驱动可实现X_{π/2}和X_π旋转。双量子点谱可干净地投影到孤立量子点乘积态上，有效逻辑两比特哈密顿量中存在非零的非局域Pauli阻塞（nonlocal Pauli block）。

Conclusion: 各向异性交替磁量子点提供了一条无需自旋轨道耦合即可实现局域栅控自旋量子比特的可行路线，为未来全电控量子计算架构的设计提供了新的物理平台。

Abstract: We propose gate-defined spin qubits in electrostatically confined altermagnetic quantum dots. Elliptical confinement of the $d$-wave altermagnetic structure produces a low-energy doublet with opposite spin polarization. For the range of parameters used here, the qubit states energy gap lies in the microwave range while the leakage gap remains in the meV range. Even without spin-orbit coupling, time-dependent simulations show that a phase-controlled quadrupolar gate drive about a fixed bias point implements $X_{π/2}$ and $X_π$ rotations by resonantly modulating the confinement anisotropy. We extend the study to two-qubits using a double quantum dot. We show that the double quantum dot spectrum can be cleanly projected onto isolated quantum dot product states with a nonzero nonlocal Pauli block in the effective logical two-qubit Hamiltonian. Resonant central-barrier modulation then drives the logical two-qubit component close to a maximally entangled state. These calculations show anisotropic altermagnetic quantum dots as a route to locally gate-controlled spin qubits without requiring spin-orbit coupling.

</details>


### [115] [Band offsets and stability of WSe$_2$/RuCl$_3$ van der Waals charge-transfer contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24199)
*Thomas S. Nielsen,Edvard Solbrekken,Christian Overby,Christian V-B. Fokdal,Alfred J. H. Jones,Zhihao Jiang,Chakradhar Sahoo,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Søren Ulstrup*

TL;DR: 本研究利用微聚焦角分辨光电子能谱（micro-focused ARPES）测定单层WSe₂与层状Mott绝缘体α-RuCl₃接触后的电子结构，发现WSe₂的价带向费米能级移动了(0.68±0.05) eV，表明RuCl₃向WSe₂发生空穴掺杂（hole-doping）。该电荷转移效应受溶剂暴露、界面封装质量和RuCl₃加热等制备条件影响显著，对器件设计提出严格要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RuCl₃因其高电子亲和能（electron affinity）可在二维半导体中诱导简并空穴掺杂，有望用于电子器件中欧姆接触（ohmic contact）的电荷转移材料。为评估其适用性并指导含RuCl₃器件的设计，必须确定RuCl₃与半导体接触后的电子结构及能带偏移（band offset）的稳定性，这是理解界面输运性质的基础。

Method: 采用微聚焦角分辨光电子能谱（micro-focused angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, micro-ARPES），测量六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）衬底上与RuCl₃接触的单层WSe₂的电子结构。

Result: 形成功能型WSe₂/RuCl₃接触后，WSe₂的价带（valence band）向费米能级（Fermi energy）方向移动了(0.68±0.05) eV，表明RuCl₃向WSe₂发生了有效的电荷转移。

Conclusion: RuCl₃诱导的电荷转移效应在实验上难以观测，高度依赖于溶剂暴露、界面封装质量和RuCl₃加热等制备条件，因此实现高质量接触需对器件设计施加严格限制。

Abstract: The layered Mott insulator $α$-RuCl$_3$ induces degenerate hole-doping in two-dimensional semiconductors due to its large electron affinity, making it a promising charge-transfer material for establishing ohmic contacts in electronic devices. In order to assess the applicability and guide the design of devices incorporating RuCl$_3$ it is critical to determine the electronic structure and robustness of the band offsets that underpin the transport properties of semiconductors in contact with RuCl$_3$. Here, we apply micro-focused angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy to determine the electronic structure of single-layer WSe$_2$ contacted to RuCl$_3$ on hexagonal boron nitride substrates. We find that formation of a functioning WSe$_2$/RuCl$_3$ contact leads to a valence band shift of $(0.68 \pm 0.05)$ eV towards the Fermi energy in WSe$_2$. The charge transfer effect is challenging to observe as it depends sensitively on fabrication conditions such as solvent exposure, quality of interface encapsulation and heating of RuCl$_3$, imposing strict requirements on device design to attain high-quality contacts.

### [116] [Enabling Electrical Readout of Néel vector reversal in a van der Waals Antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24527)
*Raghvendra Posti,Ravi Kumar Bandepalli,Wenhao Liu,Anshuman Sahoo,Pratyush Saud,Zixin Zhai,Aswin L. N. Kondusamy,Zhenhong Cui,I-Hsuan Kao,Aalok Tiwari,Thomas Poirier,James H. Edgar,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Bing Lv,Jyoti Katoch,Simranjeet Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验展示了通过自旋依赖的隧穿磁电阻（tunnelling magnetoresistance, MR）效应，在基于范德华（vdW）的A型反铁磁（AFM）CrSBr原子薄膜中实现对奈尔矢量（Néel vector）180度反转的电学读出，填补了反铁磁存储器件中关键缺失的环节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁（antiferromagnet, AFM）中奈尔矢量（Néel vector）的鲁棒性与超快动力学特性有望推动下一代自旋电子学（spintronics）和磁振子学（magnonics）器件的发展。然而，在薄膜反铁磁中实现180度奈尔矢量反转的电学读出（electrical readout）这一关键需求仍未得到验证。

Method: 利用CrSBr的自旋依赖电子能带性质，将其与一个自旋极化层（spin-polarized layer）通过隧穿势垒（tunnel barrier）耦合。在该结构中，自旋依赖的隧穿磁电阻（magnetoresistance, MR）对参考电极的磁化方向与反铁磁层界面子晶格磁化（sublattice magnetization）之间的相对取向敏感，从而实现对奈尔矢量方向的电学检测。

Result: 观察到的磁电阻（MR）能够揭示偶数层CrSBr中奈尔矢量的180度反转，在该情况下相邻子晶格磁层恰好完全补偿，净磁化（net magnetization）为零。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种广泛适用的策略，用于范德华（vdW）基反铁磁中奈尔矢量的电学检测。

Abstract: Owing to its robustness against external perturbations and intrinsically ultrafast dynamics, the Néel vector in antiferromagnets (AFMs) can enable the development of next-generation spintronic and magnonic devices for memory and computing applications. To realize AFM-based magnetic memory devices, one of the key requirements is to demonstrate electrical readout of 180-degree reversal of Néel vector in thin film AFMs, which remains critically missing. In this work, we report experimental demonstration of a novel transport methodology to detect Néel vector reversal in atomically thin films of a van der Waals (vdW) based A-type AFM. For this, we utilize spin-dependent electronic band properties of CrSBr by coupling it to a spin-polarized layer, separated by a tunnel barrier. In this configuration, the spin-dependent tunnelling magnetoresistance (MR) becomes sensitive to the relative orientation between the magnetization of the reference electrode and the interfacial sublattice magnetization of the AFM layer, in turn enabling electrical detection of the Néel vector orientation. Importantly, the observed MR can also reveal 180-degree reversal of Néel vector in even-layers of CrSBr, wherein adjacent sublattice magnetic layers are exactly compensated and the net magnetization vanishes and thus establishes a broadly applicable strategy for electrical detection of Néel vector in vdW-based AFMs.

### [117] [AC Conductance in n-InSb Structures with Quantum Well. Acoustic Studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24663)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用声学方法（acoustic methods）测量n-InSb量子阱结构在最高18 T磁场和20–500 mK温度范围的交流电导；通过实验数据分离量子阱与平行导电层的贡献；并运用符合技术（coincidence technique）提取电子g因子及自旋极化影响。

Result: 确定了表面声波（SAW）衰减与速度的异常磁场依赖关系源自与量子阱平行的导电层的存在；成功区分了量子阱和旁路层的导电机制贡献；获得了量子阱中电子g因子及其随自旋极化程度的变化规律。

Conclusion: n-InSb量子阱结构中平行导电层的存在导致表面声波（SAW）传输特性的异常磁场依赖；分离该旁路层贡献后，可准确识别量子阱自身的导电机制；符合技术（coincidence technique）有效用于测定自旋极化依赖的电子g因子。

Abstract: We studied the ac conductance of an $n$-InSb quantum well structure using acoustic methods in magnetic fields up to 18 T and at temperatures ranging from 20 to 500 mK. We attribute the unusual magnetic field dependences of surface acoustic wave (SAW) attenuation and velocity observed in the experiment to the presence of a conducting layer parallel to the quantum well in the sample. We successfully separated the contributions from both the quantum well and the shunting layer, enabling the identification of their distinct conduction mechanisms. Furthermore, by employing the coincidence technique, we determined the electron g-factor in the quantum well and investigated its dependence on the degree of spin polarization.

Conclusion: 通过超净半导体异质结中的复合超晶格结构，可以模拟Haldane模型，为实验实现陈绝缘体提供了一种替代方案。

Abstract: The Haldane model represents the minimal lattice-based realization of a Chern insulator, exhibiting a quantized Hall conductance in the absence of Landau levels. In this work, we theoretically investigate the possibility to simulate the Haldane model in ultra-clean GaAs/AlGaAs heterostructures. Our proposal relies on recent experiments in which a high-mobility two-dimensional electron gas is subject to a gate-defined honeycomb electrostatic potential and a laterally periodic magnetic field generated by patterned ferromagnetic structures. ### [119] [Anyon Exchange Phase from Antidot Interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24831)
*Matthias Thamm,Felix Puster,Bernd Rosenow*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于非平衡凯尔迪什（Keldysh）方法，理论研究了嵌入法布里-珀罗干涉仪（Fabry-Perot interferometer）的量子反点（quantum antidot）系统，发现透射相位随栅压呈非单调演化，能够从中提取任意子（anyon）的裸交换相位（bare exchange phase）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall）系统中的准粒子是任意子，其交换相位（exchange phase）虽为任意子统计的核心特征，但此前实验上始终无法直接测量。

Method: 采用非平衡凯尔迪什（non-equilibrium Keldysh）形式，自洽地引入量子反点的能级占据（occupation）和能级展宽（level broadening），从而对嵌入法布里-珀罗干涉仪中的量子反点系统进行理论计算。

Result: 当栅压（gate voltage）将量子反点调至共振（resonance）时，透射相位（transmission phase）呈现非单调（non-monotonic）演化，这与电子情况下的单调（monotonic）演化截然不同。裸交换相位可以从相位平台（phase plateau）之间的差值中提取。

Conclusion: 该理论结果为实验上直接测量任意子的交换相位提供了可行方案，填补了分数统计（fractional statistics）验证中交换相位这一长期缺失的关键环节。

Abstract: Quasiparticles in fractional quantum Hall systems are anyons, carrying a fraction of the electron charge. Exchanging two of them gives rise to a fractional exchange phase. While the fractional charge and the braiding phase -- twice the exchange phase -- have been measured, the exchange phase itself has remained inaccessible. We study a quantum antidot embedded in a Fabry-Perot interferometer. Within a systematic non-equilibrium Keldysh treatment that consistently includes the occupation and level broadening of the antidot, we find that the transmission phase evolves non-monotonically when a gate voltage tunes the antidot through a resonance, in contrast to the monotonic evolution for electrons. The bare exchange phase can be extracted from the difference between the phase plateaus.

</details>

### [120] [A 35B Hybrid-Attention Mixture-of-Experts Model on a 6GB 2011 GPU: Hand-Written 4-bit CUDA Inference for Fermi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24031)
*A. C. Opus,J. Q. Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文报告了在2011年发布的NVIDIA Tesla C2075（Fermi架构，6GB显存）GPU上，端到端推理一个350亿参数、约30亿激活参数的混合专家模型（MoE）Qwen3.6-35B-A3B的实现与优化过程。采用混合执行策略——GPU负责层间流式加载的预填充（prefill），CPU使用手写W4A8整数GEMV内核处理解码（decode），并报告了多项加速技术及负结果，最终将预填充延迟降低34%，解码吞吐量提升约3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索并量化在过时硬件（2011年Fermi架构GPU，缺乏张量核心、原生FP16和现代CUDA工具链支持）上运行前沿大语言模型（LLM）的实际可行性与性能瓶颈，而非追求速度纪录。

Method: 采用混合执行策略：GPU通过主机RAM逐层流式加载专家权重（expert streaming）进行批处理预填充（prefill），CPU利用基于SSSE3 pmaddubsw指令的手写W4A8整数GEMV内核处理自回归解码（decode）。整个引擎（GEMM、混合注意力循环、MoE路由、视觉塔）针对计算能力2.0手工编写，使用遗留CUDA 8.0工具链编译。此外采用了专家固定（expert pinning）、单遍预填充（single-pass prefill）、NUMA交错（NUMA interleaving）以及基于位置索引的门控-增量网络（gated-delta-net）状态快照缓存等优化。

Result: 在947词元（token）提示上，将预填充延迟从57.2秒降至37.5秒（降低34%）；解码吞吐量从每秒2.8词元提升至8.6词元（约3倍）。循环状态的快照缓存将重复预填充从78秒降至0.5秒。语言模型头部卸载至空闲GPU、超线程（hyper-threading）及三次GPU内核重写均未带来性能提升（负结果）。

Conclusion: 尽管存在显著性能限制，但在十四年前的老旧GPU上运行当代前沿MoE模型是可行的。混合执行策略和手写整数SIMD内核是主要加速手段，而负结果揭示了该硬件的实际性能下限。

Abstract: We report end-to-end inference of \textbf{Qwen3.6-35B-A3B} -- a 35-billion-parameter, $\sim$3B-active Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) model with a hybrid gated-delta-net / full-attention backbone -- on a \textbf{2011 NVIDIA Tesla C2075} (Fermi, compute capability \smtwenty, 6\,GB), a GPU that predates tensor cores, native FP16 arithmetic, the \texttt{DP4A} integer dot-product instruction, and support in every modern CUDA toolchain. Because the 4-bit model ($\approx$10.5\,GB) is roughly twice the device memory, we adopt a \emph{hybrid} execution strategy: the GPU performs batched prompt \emph{prefill} with expert weights streamed layer-by-layer from host RAM, while \emph{decode} runs on the host CPU using a hand-written W4A8 integer GEMV built on the SSSE3 \texttt{pmaddubsw} instruction. The entire engine -- GEMM, hybrid-attention recurrence, MoE routing, and a from-scratch vision tower -- is written by hand for \smtwenty{} and compiled with the legacy CUDA 8.0 toolchain. On a 947-token prompt we reduce prefill latency from 57.2\,s to 37.5\,s ($-34\%$) through expert pinning, single-pass prefill, and NUMA interleaving, and we raise decode throughput from 2.8 to 8.6\,\tps{} ($\approx 3\times$) with the integer-SIMD kernel. A position-indexed snapshot cache for the recurrent (gated-delta-net) state restores prefix reuse on a recurrent architecture, cutting a repeated 78\,s prefill to 0.5\,s. We also report a set of \emph{negative} results -- offloading the language-model head to the idle GPU, hyper-threading, and three GPU-kernel rewrites all fail to help -- % which together pin down the practical floor of this hardware. Our aim is not a speed record but a careful account of what it takes, and where the walls are, to run a contemporary frontier-class MoE on fourteen-year-old silicon.

</details>


### [121] [The effect of pressure on the splitting in $^3$He in nematic aerogel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24308)
*V. V. Dmitriev,D. V. Petrova,A. A. Soldatov,A. N. Yudin*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本论文通过实验研究了压力对超流³He在非各向同性气凝胶（anisotropic aerogel）中超流转变温度分裂的影响，特别关注了有无⁴He覆盖层时的不同行为，并试图解释此前观测到的非线性依赖性理论与实验之间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知边界条件显著影响气凝胶中超流相的性质，且先前实验发现纯³He中转变温度分裂存在非线性依赖，但其非线性范围与基于磁散射效应的理论预测不符。本文旨在通过改变压力进行系统测量，探究该差异的根源。

Method: 研究者分别在纯³He体系以及气凝胶（aerogel）纤维被⁴He覆盖的体系中，测量了不同压力下的超流转变温度分裂（splitting of superfluid transition temperature）情况。

Result: 在⁴He覆盖气凝胶纤维的情况下，磁场中会出现Polar相、Polar畸变A相（polar-distorted A, DA）、Polar畸变B相（polar-distorted B, DB）及β相等新相；而无覆盖时，体系倾向于体相A相、B相和A₁相。纯³He中转变温度分裂表现出非线性依赖性，但非线性范围与磁散射（magnetic scattering）理论预期不符。

Conclusion: 为澄清理论与实验之间的差异，有必要在不同压力下对纯³He和有⁴He覆盖的气凝胶体系分别进行转变温度分裂的测量。

Abstract: Here, we present the results of an investigation of how the pressure affects the splitting of the superfluid transition temperature in $^3$He in anisotropic aerogel. It is well known that boundary conditions significantly influence the properties of superfluid phases in aerogel. When aerogel strands are coated with a $^4$He layer in magnetic field, new phases, such as the polar, polar-distorted A (DA), polar-distorted B (DB), and $β$ phases, become energetically favorable. In contrast, without this coating, the system tends to favor phases resembling the bulk A, B, and A$_1$ phases. Our earlier results showed a nonlinear dependence of the superfluid transition temperature splitting in pure $^3$He, but the range of nonlinearity did not match the theoretical predictions based on magnetic scattering effects. To further investigate this discrepancy, we performed measurements of the splitting under varying pressures for both pure $^3$He and with $^4$He coverage of the aerogel strands.

</details>
