### [122] [Computational references are not experiments: pre-registered validation of machine-learned sodium-cathode voltages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23725)
*Krishna Teja Vepa*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报告了机器学习筛选电池材料过程中，由于计算参考电压自身的系统误差，导致筛选模型在实验验证中失效的案例。作者在预注册验证后发现，误差主要由参考数据库（Materials Project PBE+U）而非模型本身主导，最终决定退役该筛选流程，并预先注册了对DFT参考数据的校准审计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示机器学习筛选电池材料时，过度依赖计算参考电压（computed reference voltages）可能导致模型验证失效的问题。当前领域几乎完全以计算数据训练和评估模型，但这些参考数据自身携带系统误差（systematic errors），其影响尚未被充分量化。

Method: 采用预注册验证（pre-registered validation）策略，在分析前提交判决阈值、失败模式及主要评价指标。使用图网络电压筛选（graph-network voltage screen）、现有文献分类层（prior-art triage layer）和局部PBE+U基准（local PBE+U bench）构成的筛选堆栈，对实验锚定文献值进行验证。

Result: 在6个已知钠离子正极材料（operator-audited set）上，原始留出平均绝对误差（raw held-out MAE）为0.67 V；预注册保守指标（交叉验证偏差校正误差的95%置信上限）为1.09 V。残差与电压强相关（r = -0.94），表明无法进行加性校正。在可比较的两个材料中，Materials Project PBE+U参考值比实验测量低约0.54 V。现有文献分类器发现至少70%的目标钠替代空间已被发表。

Conclusion: 该电池材料筛选流程在实验验证中失败，误差主要来源于DFT参考数据而非机器学习模型本身。作者决定退役该筛选流程，界定了其DFT账本（DFT ledger）中“已验证”（verified）的含义，并预注册了针对四个基准锂电对的校准审计（calibration audit）。

Abstract: Machine-learning screens for battery materials are trained and judged almost entirely against computed reference voltages, and those references carry their own systematic errors. We report a case in which this matters quantitatively: our own screening stack (a graph-network voltage screen, a prior-art triage layer, and a local PBE+U bench) fails pre-registered validation against experiment-anchored literature values. Verdict thresholds, failure modes, and the primary metric were committed before analysis. On an operator-audited set of known Na-ion cathodes (n = 6 after one documented exclusion; verdict unchanged at n = 7), the raw held-out mean absolute error was 0.67 V, the pre-registered conservative metric, the upper 95% confidence bound of the cross-validated bias-corrected error, was 1.09 V, and the residual was strongly voltage-dependent (r = -0.94), so no additive calibration is valid. On the two compounds where prediction, database reference, and experiment could all be compared, the Materials Project PBE+U reference sat about 0.54 V below measurement: the reference, not the model, dominated the error. A prior-art screen found at least 70% of the targeted Na substitution space already published. We retire the screen, bound what "verified" means for our DFT ledger, and pre-register a calibration audit of it against four benchmark Li couples.

</details>

*Mathieu Calvat,Gregory Sparks,Dhruv Anjaria,Chris Bean,Haoren Wang,Paul Gradl,Timothy M. Smith,Allison M. Beese,Gabriel Demeneghi,Kenneth Vecchio,Morad Behandish,J. C. Stinville*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 Materials Spatial Intelligence (MSI) 框架，通过多模态空间观测数据直接学习材料系统的潜在表征，在保留空间关系的同时实现性能预测、机制发现与微观结构优化，为材料科学中的可解释空间智能（spatial intelligence）奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器学习方法在材料科学中大多依赖手工描述符（handcrafted descriptors）或聚合表征（aggregated representations），忽视了微观结构的空间组织信息，从而限制了对其控制机制的深入理解。

Method: MSI 框架结合多模态表征学习（multimodal representation learning），将高分辨率微观结构与形变数据编码为共享潜在表征（shared latent representations），在保留空间关系的前提下支持属性预测、解释与优化。

Result: 在结构合金（structural alloys）中，MSI 能够识别控制力学行为（mechanical behavior）与性能权衡（property trade-offs）的关键特征，并实现基于特征驱动的微观结构优化（feature-driven microstructure optimization）与机制发现（mechanism discovery）。

Conclusion: MSI 为将空间智能应用于材料科学建立了基础框架，通过可解释的机器学习系统加速科学发现与材料设计。

Abstract: Many material systems exhibit complex spatial and temporal interactions across multiple length scales and modalities that govern macroscopic behavior. Although Machine Learning (ML) is widely used in materials science to predict this behavior, most approaches still rely on handcrafted descriptors or aggregated representations that overlook spatial organization, limiting insight into governing mechanisms. We introduce Materials Spatial Intelligence (MSI), a framework inspired by spatial intelligence that learns directly from multimodal spatial observations of material systems. MSI encodes high-resolution microstructural and deformation data into shared latent representations that preserve spatial relationships while supporting property prediction, interpretation, and optimization. By combining multimodal representation learning, MSI identifies the key features governing mechanical behavior and property trade-offs in structural alloys. Beyond prediction, MSI enables feature-driven microstructure optimization and mechanism discovery. More broadly, MSI establishes a foundation for applying spatial intelligence to materials science, leveraging interpretable ML systems to accelerate scientific discovery and materiel design

</details>


### [124] [Notes on remanent magnetization measurements in superconductors and hard ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23738)
*Sergey L. Bud'ko,Mingyu Xu,Weiwei Xie,Chaowei Hu,Ni Ni,Paul C. Canfield*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在零施加场条件下，对LuNi2B2C超导体和若干硬铁磁体进行了剩磁（remanent magnetization）与磁弛豫（magnetic relaxation）测量，并采用了类似热剩磁（Thermoremanent Magnetization, TRM）、等温剩磁（Isothermal Remanent Magnetization, IRM）以及锯齿形温度扫描（zigzag temperature sweep）等测量方案进行比较分析。

Result: 在TRM类、IRM类以及锯齿温度扫描剩磁测量中，超导体与硬铁磁体表现出一定的表观相似性与差异性。

Conclusion: 这些结果可能与金刚石对顶砧（diamond anvil cell）中的磁化测量相关，提示在高压实验中需注意超导与铁磁剩磁行为的区分。

Abstract: Data on zero applied field measurements of remanent magnetization and magnetic relaxation in a BCS superconductor LuNi2B2C and several hard ferromagnets are presented and compared. Apparent similarities and differences, in particular in Thermoremanent Magnetization (TRM) - like, Isothermal Remanent Magnetization (IRM) - like, and remanent magnetization measurements with zigzag temperature sweep measurements are outlined. It is discussed how these results could be relevant for the magnetization measurements in diamond anvil cells.

### [125] [Nonrelativistic Spin-Orbit-Coupling Effects in Odd-Parity Coplanar Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23806)
*Dongling Liu,Zheng-Yang Zhuang,Di Zhu,Zhigang Wu,Zhongbo Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出通过奇宇称共面磁体（odd-parity coplanar magnets）实现非相对论性自旋-轨道耦合效应（SOC），展示了一种无需重元素即可高度可调的自旋-轨道耦合新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）源自相对论效应，因此被限制在重元素材料中，且自旋-动量织构（spin-momentum texture）固定于材料特定模式，缺乏可调性。本文旨在探索一种非相对论性（nonrelativistic）途径来实现高度可调的SOC效应。

Method: 通过对称性引导的堆叠方法，将两个单层奇宇称交错磁体（odd-parity altermagnet）构建成双层共面磁体结构，并通过调控层内奈尔矢量（layer Néel vector）来切换不同类型的自旋织构。

Result: 该双层结构可分别实现Rashba、Weyl和Dresselhaus三种自旋织构（spin textures），且可通过调节层内奈尔矢量在这几种形式之间切换。进一步通过自旋埃德尔斯坦效应（spin Edelstein effect）和实现完全带隙的手性拓扑超导相（chiral topological superconducting phases），证明了该非相对论性SOC在物理上与相对论性SOC等价。

Conclusion: 奇宇称共面磁体被确立为一类全新的多功能平台，可用于工程化设计和调控自旋-轨道耦合效应，突破了传统SOC对重元素和固定自旋织构的限制。

Abstract: Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) is a relativistic effect that underpins a broad spectrum of phenomena in condensed matter physics, from topological phases of matter to spintronic functionality. Its relativistic origin, however, restricts strong SOC to heavy-element materials and locks spin-momentum texture into a fixed, material-specific pattern. Here we show that odd-parity coplanar magnets offer a nonrelativistic pathway to highly tunable SOC effects. We construct a bilayer coplanar magnet via symmetry-guided stacking of two monolayer odd-parity altermagnets and demonstrate that Rashba, Weyl, and Dresselhaus spin textures can all be realized, and that the spin texture can be switched between these forms simply by tuning the layer Neel vector. Through the spin Edelstein effect and the realization of fully gapped chiral topological superconducting phases, we demonstrate that this nonrelativistic SOC achieves physical equivalence to its relativistic counterpart. Our findings identify a new class of odd-parity coplanar magnets as a versatile platform for engineering SOC effects.

</details>


### [126] [Reversible non-equilibrium phase transformation in amorphous germanium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24097)
*Yang Huang,Marek Mihalkovič,Michael Widom*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理分子动力学（first principles molecular dynamics）模拟，在锗（germanium）中发现平衡熔点以下存在可逆液-玻璃转变（liquid-glass transition），伴随宽滞后回线（hysteresis loop）。通过绝对熵计算（absolute entropy calculations）直接获得液体和非晶态自由能，证实该转变是两个亚稳相（metastable phases）之间的一级相变（first order transition）。结果支持非晶锗薄膜通过亚稳液态实现爆炸再结晶（explosive recrystallization）并最终达到低温晶体结构的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究锗中液-玻璃转变的热力学本质，验证该转变是否为一级相变，并解释非晶锗薄膜中爆炸再结晶的微观机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理分子动力学（first principles molecular dynamics）模拟锗的相变行为；通过绝对熵计算（absolute entropy calculations）直接获取液体与非晶态的自由能，从而判定转变的相变级次。

Result: 在平衡熔点以下观察到可逆液-玻璃转变，并伴随宽滞后回线（hysteresis loop）。自由能计算表明该转变是发生在两个亚稳相（metastable phases）之间的一级相变（first order transition）。

Conclusion: 模拟结果支持非晶锗薄膜爆炸再结晶（explosive recrystallization）的模型：非晶相先转变为亚稳液态，再进一步弛豫至低温晶体结构。

Abstract: First principles molecular dynamics simulations of germanium reveal a reversible liquid-glass transition below the equilibrium melting point with a wide hysteresis loop. Direct calculation of the liquid and amorphous state free energies, enabled by absolute entropy calculations, verify that the transition is first order in character between two metastable phases. These results lend credence to models of explosive recrystallization from amorphous Ge thin films, through a metastable liquid state and finally reaching the low temperature crystalline structure.

</details>


### [127] [Low-temperature magnetic-field-driven thermal oscillator based on metal-superconductor joint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24100)
*Poonam Rani,Yoshikazu Mizuguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出并实验验证了一种基于金属-超导体（Cu-Pb）接合的磁驱动热振荡器（magnetically-driven thermal oscillator），通过调控外加磁场（H）利用超导体在超导转变（superconducting transition）处热导率的急剧变化，实现了频率、振幅和波形灵活可调且平均温度高度稳定的热振荡输出，可作为低温下的柔性交流热源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交流电流驱动的热振荡器（thermal oscillator）需复杂的输入功率控制才能实现频率、振幅和波形的灵活调节以及平均温度的稳定性，因而亟需一种更简洁高效的热振荡实现方案。

Method: 在金属-超导体（Cu-Pb）接合结构（junction）中，于金属（Cu）侧安装直流电流（DC current）驱动的加热器，超导体（Pb）侧边缘连接至热浴（thermal bath）。利用Pb线在超导转变处热导率（thermal conductivity）的尖锐且巨大的变化，通过调节外加磁场（H）驱动热振荡。

Result: 观测到振幅180 mK、频率0.17 Hz的正弦形（sine-shaped）热振荡（thermal oscillation），平均温度高度稳定；进一步通过增大磁场振幅（H amplitude）实现了更大振幅的方波形（square-shaped）振荡。

Conclusion: 该磁驱动热振荡器兼具温度稳定性、大振幅和相对高频的优势，可作为低温下灵活的交流热源（AC heat source）使用。

Abstract: Thermal control is one of the important technologies for fundamental science and thermal management. Among them, thermal oscillators have been in demands in the field of materials science and device application. In general, flexible frequency, amplitude, and waveform are needed for useful thermal oscillator, and the stability of the average temperature is also highly required. However, thermal oscillators based on an AC-current-driven heater require complicated control of input power to achieve the above-mentioned flexibility and stability of the outputs. Here, we demonstrate that magnetically-driven thermal oscillators fabricated using a metal-superconductor (Cu-Pb) joint achieve those requirements easily by tuning the applied magnetic field (H). A DC-current-driven heater is attached on the metal (Cu) side, and the superconductor (Pb) edge is attached to thermal bath. We use a sharp and huge change in thermal conductivity at the superconducting transition of the Pb wire to generate thermal oscillation at the Cu-wire side. A sine-shaped thermal oscillation with an amplitude of 180 mK and a frequency of 0.17 Hz is observed with highly stable average temperature. Furthermore, a larger amplitude is achieved in a square-shaped oscillation with a larger H amplitude. Our thermal oscillator with temperature stability, large amplitude, and relatively high frequency will work as a flexible AC heat source at cryogenic temperatures.

</details>


### [128] [Nonradiative Multiphonon Model of Deep-Level Transient Spectroscopy: Beyond Henry-Lang Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24227)
*Menglin Huang,Shanshan Wang,Junjie Zhou,Xinjing Guo,Shiyou Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文指出传统深能级瞬态谱（DLTS）分析中的Henry-Lang模型仅在康登近似、高温及强电子-声子耦合近似下成立，导致载流子发射与俘获的温度依赖关系错误。作者发展了一个严格的无辐射多声子（NMP）模型，发现温度依赖主要由具有大波函数重叠和高热占据的有效声子支配，且有效声子与晶格弛豫强相关。在12种半导体21种缺陷上的对比表明，Henry-Lang模型的载流子俘获截面温度依赖与NMP模型结果完全不同，室温下误差可达六个数量级，强调了有必要用严格NMP模型重新审视以往DLTS分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DLTS是缺陷表征的关键实验方法，但其分析模型（Henry-Lang模型与后续模型）之间存在矛盾，且Henry-Lang模型可能导致载流子发射与俘获的温度依赖关系出现错误，影响缺陷参数的准确提取。

Method: 作者发展了一个严格的无辐射多声子（nonradiative multiphonon, NMP）模型，并基于该模型重新分析DLTS测量的发射速率，研究了有效声子与晶格弛豫之间的关联及其对温度依赖行为的影响。

Result: 在Si、SiC和Ga₂O₃等12种半导体的21种缺陷上，Henry-Lang模型给出的载流子俘获截面温度依赖与严格NMP模型结果完全不同，室温下误差可达六个数量级。现有DLTS模型由于忽略了有效声子与晶格弛豫的强关联，在拟合发射速率时会引入实质性误差。

Conclusion: Henry-Lang模型仅在特定近似条件下成立，而严格NMP模型能够正确描述DLTS测量的温度依赖行为。有必要运用该严格模型重新审视以往基于DLTS的缺陷分析研究。

Abstract: Deep-level transient spectroscopy (DLTS) is a key experimental method for defect characterization, yet its analysis remains controversial, and the two widely used models developed by Henry and Lang are conflicting. We show that the Henry-Lang model is valid only under the Condon approximation, as well as high-temperature and strong electron-phonon coupling approximations, which cause incorrect temperature dependence of carrier emission and capture. Here we develop a rigorous nonradiative multiphonon (NMP) model, and demonstrate that the temperature dependence is governed predominantly by effective phonons with large phonon wavefunction overlap and high thermal occupation. The effective phonons are strongly correlated with lattice relaxation.The neglect of this correlation in existing DLTS models introduces substantial errors when they are used to fit DLTS-measured emission rates. Our comparison for 21 different defects in 12 semiconductors, including Si, SiC and Ga$_2$O$_3$, shows that the Henry-Lang model gives a completely different temperature dependence of carrier capture cross section from that obtained using the rigorous NMP model, with errors reaching up to six orders of magnitude at room temperature. Our study highlights the necessity of revisiting previous DLTS analysis studies using the rigorous NMP model.

</details>


### [129] [One-dimensional self-organization of water molecules in proton conducting Andersson-Wadsley titanates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24239)
*Mathilde Arnaud,Guillaume Benas,Narimane Meziani,Armel Descamps-Mandine,Claudie Josse,Sophia Akkari,Thierry Douillard,Sofia de Sousa Coutinho,Mélanie de Vos,Stéphane Holé,Gwenaëlle Rousse,Rémi Federicci,Sylvain Franger,Paola Giura,Fabio Finocchi,Brigitte Leridon*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文研究了M₂Ti₂O₅型层状碱金属钛酸盐（M=K,Rb）中水分子嵌入引发的超离子导电行为，发现水分子沿b轴自组织形成一维双链，并不断水化导致自发剥落形成（001）表面；结合第一性原理计算与实验观测，指出这些水链通过类似Grotthuss机制驱动了各向异性的快速质子传导，沿b轴室温下电导率达3 mS/cm。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索属于Andersson-Wadsley型钙钛矿的M₂Ti₂O₅层状化合物（MTO）在水分子自发嵌入后表现出的超离子导电性（superionic conductivity）的微观机制，理解水分子排列与质子传导行为之间的关联。

Method: 利用扫描电子显微镜（SEM）观测不同水化程度下材料表面的形貌演化；采用密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）模拟水分子在Rb₂Ti₂O₅中的有序排列与氢键网络；结合红外光谱（infrared spectroscopy）对水链结构进行验证，并测量不同晶向上的质子电导率。

Result: 低水化程度下，水分子沿b轴自组装形成一维有序双链，并呈现沿b方向的一维异质图案；进一步水化后，材料自发剥落形成（001）表面，表面由密集排列的水链构成；Rb₂Ti₂O₅沿b方向表现出超离子导电性，室温下电导率高达3 mS/cm，且质子导电具有高度各向异性。

Conclusion: 水分子形成的自组织一维链是快速质子传导的结构根源，其传导机制很可能基于Grotthuss机制（Grotthuss-like mechanism）；这些发现为设计新型超离子导体提供了微观结构层面的理解。

Abstract: Layered alkali titanates with M 2 Ti 2 O 5 chemical formula (MTO, M=K,Rb) belonging to the Andersson-Wadsley perovskite family spontaneously incorporate water to form MTO.(H 2 O) x compounds, which exhibit superionic conductivity. At very low hydration x, scanning electron microscopy evidences one-dimensional heterogeneous patterns oriented along ___ b that are arranged in an orderly manner. At higher hydration, the material is observed to spontaneously exfoliate by creating (001) surfaces. Simulations carried out using Density Functional Theory reveal an ordered arrangement of the guest water molecules in Rb 2 Ti 2 O 5 , with strong hydrogen bonds between the water molecules and the apical oxygen of the host crystal. At low hydration x, the water molecules form self-organized one dimensional (1D) double chains along ___ b. Further increase of the water content leads to the creation of hydrated (001)-surfaces that are made of densely packed water chains in agreement with the infrared spectroscopy measurements. Rb 2 Ti 2 O 5 exhibits highly anisotropic proton conductivity, with respect to the crystal orientation, with super-ionic conductivity along ___ b reaching 3 mS/cm at room temperature after hydration. The combined observations and simulations suggest that these water chains are thus at the root of fast proton conduction, which is likely powered by a Grotthuss-like mechanism.

Conclusion: 建立了一种可迁移的工作流，用于二维范德华异质结（van der Waals heterostructures）中的近邻调控磁性（proximity-controlled magnetism）。

Abstract: Magnetic anisotropy controls the orientation and thermal stability of two-dimensional magnetic order. Predicting proximity-induced changes in anisotropy requires linking the electronic structure to microscopic magnetic interactions and finite-temperature behavior. Here we study monolayer CrI$_3$ on hexagonal WTe$_2$ using a first-principles-to-finite-temperature workflow centered on relativistic spin-Hamiltonian mapping. We find that WTe$_2$ reorients the CrI$_3$ magnetization from out-of-plane to in-plane and substantially enhances the magnetic ordering scale within the extracted spin models. Analysis of the extracted spin Hamiltonians shows that the reorientation is driven by a substrate-induced change in the balance between symmetric anisotropic exchange and onsite anisotropy. ### [131] [Quintic-Anharmonicity-Assisted Three-Phonon Scattering: A Previously Overlooked Same-Order Channel to Four-Phonon Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24409)
*Yi Xia*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现了一种被此前忽视的、与四声子散射同阶但由三阶与五阶非简谐顶点耦合引起的新声子散射通道——五阶非简谐辅助的三声子散射（quintic-anharmonicity-assisted three-phonon scattering），并在第一性原理层面推导和实现了该贡献。该通道的能量守恒结构与常规三声子过程相同，但微扰阶次和温度依赖性与四声子过程相当。在Si中该通道散射率在宽频宽温范围内可与四声子散射相比拟，在强非简谐体系AgCl中甚至可在室温下与常规三声子散射相当。该结果表明，高温下热导率抑制不能唯一归因于四声子过程，并揭示了一个此前被忽略的同阶散射通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统三声子散射（three-phonon scattering）模型不能完全描述高温下的非简谐散射与晶格热输运，而四声子散射（four-phonon scattering）被认为是最主要的更高阶非简谐修正。然而，是否存在其他同阶但被忽略的散射通道尚不清楚。

Method: 基于图论微扰理论（diagrammatic perturbation theory）识别出与四声子过程同阶的新贡献，该贡献源于三阶非简谐顶点（cubic anharmonic vertex）与五阶非简谐顶点（quintic anharmonic vertex）的耦合。从第一性原理（first principles）出发推导并实现了该散射通道的公式化表达。

Result: 在Si中，该额外通道的声子散射率在宽频率和温度范围内与四声子散射相当，导致高温下晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity）出现类似的加速降低。在强非简谐材料AgCl中，该通道甚至在室温下就与常规三声子散射相当。

Conclusion: 高温下观测到的增强散射与热导率抑制不能唯一归因于四声子过程。该工作确立了一个此前被忽视的同阶散射通道——五阶非简谐辅助的三声子散射，为揭示隐藏的微观热输运机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Four-phonon scattering is widely regarded as the leading higher-order anharmonic correction to conventional three-phonon description of anharmonic scattering and lattice thermal transport. Here we show that diagrammatic perturbation theory contains another phonon linewidth contribution of the same perturbation order, arising from the coupling between cubic and quintic anharmonic vertices. We derive and implement this contribution from first principles and identify it as a quintic-anharmonicity-assisted three-phonon scattering channel. Although this process shares energy-conservation structure of the conventional three-phonon process, its perturbative order and temperature dependence resemble those of the conventional four-phonon process. For Si, we find that phonon scattering from this additional channel is comparable to four-phonon scattering over a broad frequency and temperature range, leading to a similar accelerated reduction of lattice thermal conductivity at high temperatures. We further show that in strongly anharmonic AgCl, this channel can become comparable to the ordinary three-phonon scattering even at room temperature. These results demonstrate that the commonly observed high-temperature enhanced scattering and suppression of lattice thermal conductivity might not be attributed uniquely to four-phonon process, and establish quintic-anharmonicity-assisted three-phonon scattering as a previously overlooked same-order channel in anharmonic lattice dynamics, which may be leveraged to uncover hidden microscopic thermal transport mechanisms.

</details>


### [132] [Dimensional Confinement Driven Scattering Inversion in NaCrTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24478)
*Himanshu Sharma,Bhawna Sahni,Tanusri Saha-Dasgupta,Aftab Alam*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算结合超越恒定弛豫时间近似的玻尔兹曼输运方程，研究了反铁磁半导体NaCrTe₂中维度降低引发的磁结构重构，发现从块体到单层时主导散射机制从极性光学声子（POP）散射转变为声学形变势（ADP）散射，并阐明了介电屏蔽、晶格刚度与能带拓扑如何共同调控低维磁性半导体的输运性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管维度降低已被证明是调控范德华材料（van der Waals materials）电子和磁性质的有效途径，但其对电子输运的影响因量子限域（quantum confinement）和散射机制改变之间的竞争效应而仍然复杂，亟需澄清这一相互作用机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合超越恒定弛豫时间近似（constant relaxation time approximation）的玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation），对反铁磁半导体NaCrTe₂进行研究。

Result: 单层极限诱导了耦合的磁结构重构（magnetostructural reconstruction），使带隙从块体的0.44 eV降至单层的0.15 eV，并显著增强了静态介电常数（static dielectric constant）。这一演变触发了根本性的散射反转：块体中以极性光学声子（POP）散射为主，而单层中转为声学形变势（ADP）散射主导。

Conclusion: 该散射交叉源于介电屏蔽增强对弗洛利希相互作用（Fröhlich interaction）的抑制与晶格软化对声学散射的放大之间的竞争。这些结果阐明了介电屏蔽、晶格刚度与能带拓扑如何共同调控低维磁性半导体的输运行为，为优化其电子性能提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Dimensionality reduction provides a powerful route to tune the electronic and magnetic properties of van der Waals materials, yet its influence on electronic transport remains complex due to competing effects from quantum confinement and modified scattering mechanisms. Here, we investigate this interplay in an antiferromagnetic semiconductor $\text{NaCrTe}_2$ using first-principles calculations combined with the Boltzmann transport equation beyond the constant relaxation time approximation. Our results show that the monolayer limit induces a coupled magnetostructural reconstruction, reducing the band gap from $0.44$ eV (bulk) to $0.15$ eV (monolayer) and significantly enhancing the static dielectric constant. This evolution triggers a fundamental scattering inversion: whereas bulk transport is limited by polar optical phonon (POP) scattering, the monolayer becomes dominated by acoustic deformation potential (ADP) scattering. We show that this crossover originates from the simultaneous suppression of the Fröhlich interaction through enhanced dielectric screening and the amplification of acoustic scattering due to pronounced lattice softening. These results clarify how the interplay between dielectric screening, lattice stiffness, and band topology governs transport in low-dimensional magnetic semiconductors, providing a framework to optimize their electronic performance.

Conclusion: 作者指出了数据标准化、界面复杂性和可重复性方面的挑战，并提出了构建固态电池材料自主实验室（autonomous laboratories）的设计原则。

Abstract: Solid electrolytes (SEs) are central to next-generation metal batteries, yet their discovery remains constrained by fragmented data, limited transferability of simulations, and slow experimental iteration. Unlike catalysis, where surface reactivity dominates, SEs require simultaneous optimization of bulk ion transport, defect chemistry, mechanical integrity, and interfacial stability. Here, we outline a framework for autonomous SE discovery enabled by large artificial intelligence (AI) models, including machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) and large language models (LLMs). We discuss the evolution from static materials databases to dynamic, self-updating knowledge systems, the role of MLIPs in bridging density functional theory (DFT) and long-timescale ion migration, and the emergence of LLMs as engines for literature mining, hypothesis generation, and scientific reasoning. We further describe a closed-loop architecture integrating AI-driven candidate design, multiscale simulation, uncertainty-aware selection, and experimental validation. Such systems shift SE research from intuition-guided exploration to data-informed, self-improving cycles. We conclude by highlighting challenges in data standardization, interfacial complexity, and reproducibility, and we propose design principles for building autonomous laboratories for solid-state battery materials.

### [135] [Fractional Magnonic Frequency Combs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24673)
*Qian-Nan Huang,Zhiping Xue,Xudong Wang,Yanmeng Lei,Lihui Bai,Ke Xia,Gerrit E. W. Bauer,Tao Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了在高质量磁性球体中发现的分数量子磁振子频率梳（fractional magnonic frequency combs），通过添加低功率失谐微波将频率间距压缩为原始梳齿的有理数分数，产生数百条谱线的高密度频谱网格。理论分析表明，参量三磁振子散射（parametric three-magnon scattering）是主导非线性过程，该机制为磁系统特有，在精密计量领域具有应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统整数磁振子频率梳（integer MFCs）的频率间距固定且相等，限制了频谱密度和灵敏度。本文旨在探索如何通过低功率失谐微波驱动，在磁性体系中实现更高密度的频率梳，从而突破整数梳的局限性。

Method: 实验上，在高质量磁性球体中使用主驱动微波外加一个低功率精确失谐的辅助微波，产生分数量子磁振子频率梳（fractional MFCs）。理论上，通过分析发现参量三磁振子散射（parametric three-magnon scattering）是主导非线性过程，该机制能够很好地复现实验观测结果。

Result: 实现了频率间距压缩为原始整数梳有理数分数的分数量子磁振子频率梳，生成包含数百条谱线的高密度频谱网格。该分数量子磁振子频率梳（fractional MFCs）的灵敏度显著高于传统整数磁振子频率梳（integer MFCs）。

Conclusion: 分数量子磁振子频率梳（fractional MFCs）的工作机制——参量三磁振子散射（parametric three-magnon scattering）——是磁系统独有的非线性过程，在光力学系统（optomechanical system）中不存在。该平台可作为频率“游标卡尺”（vernier caliper），在精密计量（precision metrology）领域具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Magnonic frequency combs (MFCs) are spectacular phenomena in microwave-driven high-quality magnets. Like the equally spaced prongs in a comb, conventional \textit{integer} MFCs are sharp resonances with an equal and constant frequency difference. Here we report \textit{fractional} MFCs in a high-quality magnetic sphere that emerges when adding a low-power, precisely detuned microwave to the main drive that compresses the frequency spacings to a rational fraction of the original comb, generating high-density spectral grids with hundreds of lines. The theoretical analysis finds that parametric three-magnon scattering is the dominant non-linear process that reproduces the observation well. This mechanism is unique to magnets: it does not exist in an optomechanical system, where the Kerr and optical nonlinearities govern comb formation at a much higher power input. Since our platform operates as a frequency ``vernier caliper" with much higher sensitivity than integer MFCs, it has application potential in precision metrology.

### [136] [Mechanism of Band Gap Formation in Beam Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24860)
*Kwangmin Lee,Charles Emmett Maher,Katherine A. Newhall,Ryan C. Hurley*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的带隙形成机制——几何诱导的变形模式耦合（geometry-induced coupling between deformation modes），解释了梁网络（beam networks）中带隙（band gap）的形成：带隙起始源于节点处的轴向-弯曲耦合（axial-bending coupling）并与一维周期性梁的轴向截止频率（axial cutoff frequency）成比例，带隙终止主要由与梁几何相关的高频旋转分支（high-frequency rotational branches）决定。该机制对周期性和无序梁网络均成立，为梁网络材料的带隙物理起源提供了统一解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管带隙通常归因于布拉格散射（Bragg scattering）或局域共振（local resonance），但这些机制是否主导梁网络中的带隙形成尚不清楚。本文旨在阐明梁网络中带隙形成的物理机制。

Method: 通过理论分析提出几何诱导的变形模式耦合作为新机制，分别考察周期性晶格和无序网络中该机制的具体表现形式：在周期性晶格中通过节点处的梁取向（beam orientations）体现，在无序网络中通过梁长度变化导致的短梁统计（short-beam statistics）体现。

Result: 带隙起始由轴向-弯曲耦合及轴向截止频率决定，带隙终止由梁几何相关的高频旋转分支主导。该机制同时适用于周期性和无序梁网络，但表现形态不同：周期性网络中体现为节点处的梁取向，无序网络中体现为梁长度变化引起的短梁统计效应。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了周期性和无序梁网络中带隙形成的统一机制，为梁网络材料中带隙的物理起源提供了新的认识。

Abstract: Band gaps are commonly attributed to Bragg scattering or local resonance, yet it remains unclear whether these mechanisms govern band gap formation in beam networks. In this work, we explain band gap formation in beam networks in terms of a new mechanism, geometry-induced coupling between deformation modes. Specifically, band gap onset arises from axial-bending coupling at lattice nodes and scales with the axial cutoff frequency of a one-dimensional periodic beam, whereas band gap termination is primarily governed by high-frequency rotational branches associated with beam geometry. This mechanism holds for both periodic and disordered beam networks. In periodic lattices, it manifests through beam orientations at lattice nodes, whereas in disordered networks it manifests through short-beam statistics arising from variations in beam length. Together, these results establish a unified mechanism for band gap formation across both periodic and disordered beam networks, providing new insight into the physical origin of band gaps in beam-network materials.

</details>

### [137] [Investigating causality between principal components in protein dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24283)
*Debarshi Banerjee,Ali Hassanali,Alessandro Laio*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究将一种因果发现框架（causal-discovery framework）应用于分子动力学（MD）模拟的主成分分析（PCA）结果，构建了主成分（PCs）之间的有向网络（directed networks），揭示了传统协方差分析无法捕获的因果不对称性（causal asymmetries），为蛋白质运动动力学组织提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主成分分析（PCA）广泛用于表征分子动力学（MD）模拟中的集体蛋白质运动，但PCA仅识别结构波动的主导模态，无法揭示不同主成分（PCs）之间是否存在因果性相互影响。

Method: 采用Del Tatto等人（PNAS, 2024）近期提出的因果发现框架，将其应用于两种蛋白质的长时标MD轨迹。通过分析PCs之间的关系，构建描述PCs跨时标相互影响的有向网络（directed networks）。

Result: 所发现的定向关系（directional relationships）是因果联系存在的必要条件，这些关系无法被基于协方差（covariance）的传统分析方法捕获，提供的信息与PCA及时滞独立成分分析（TICA）互补。

Conclusion: 该因果推断方法能够揭示蛋白质运动动力学组织中先前隐藏的特征，为这一广泛使用的集体变量（collective variables）类别提供了新的分析视角。

Abstract: Principal component analysis (PCA) is widely used to characterize collective protein motions from molecular dynamics (MD) simulations. While PCA identifies the dominant modes of structural fluctuation, it does not reveal whether different principal components (PCs) causally influence each other. Here, we investigate this question using a recently introduced causal-discovery framework [Del Tatto et al, PNAS 2024], which allows to infer putative causal asymmetries between high-dimensional time series. We apply this approach to long-timescale MD trajectories of two proteins. By analyzing relationships among PCs, we construct directed networks describing how PCs influence one another across time scales. These directional relationships, whose existence is a necessary condition for the presence of a causal link, are not captured by conventional covariance-based analyses and provide information that is complementary to PCA and Time-lagged Independent Component Analysis (TICA). Our results suggest that our causal inference approach can uncover previously hidden aspects of the dynamical organization of protein motions and offer a new perspective on this very popular class of collective variables.

</details>


### [138] [Quantum nuclear and band-dispersion effects recover near-UV absorption in short-hydrogen-bonded organic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24750)
*Jonas Hänseroth,Max Großmann,Malte Grunert,Ali Hassanali,Erich Runge,Christian Dreßler,Muhammad Nawaz Qaisrani*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过结合机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials）、量子核采样（quantum nuclear sampling）和混合泛函含时密度泛函理论（hybrid-functional time-dependent density functional theory），发现核量子效应（nuclear quantum effects, NQEs）和布里渊区采样（Brillouin-zone sampling）共同作用，才能解释L-焦谷氨酰胺铵（L-pyroglutamine ammonium）晶体中非芳香族近紫外光学吸收的实验值，二者分别提供0.5–0.8 eV和0.5–1.1 eV的红移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢键有机和生物分子材料中频繁观测到近紫外（near-UV）光学吸收，但其微观起源尚未明确，且电子结构计算通常高估实验吸收起始值（absorption onset），亟需解决这一理论与实验间的偏差。

Method: 以实验上具有明确短氢键和非芳香近紫外响应的L-焦谷氨酰胺铵晶体为模型体系，利用机器学习原子间势进行大规模经典和量子核采样，结合混合泛函含时密度泛函理论计算光学光谱；同时通过受控的计算机内离子替换改变氢键环境，并显式纳入布里渊区采样。

Result: 核量子效应稳定了经典模拟中强烈抑制的质子共享构型，使最低亮激子（bright excitation）红移0.5–0.8 eV，并将6 eV以下亮激子构型比例从约3%提升至约30%。显式布里渊区采样额外提供0.5–1.1 eV的机制不同的红移，反映适度的间接电子特性。仅当同时纳入这两种效应时，计算吸收起始值才与实验的3.8–4.5 eV范围吻合。

Conclusion: 量子质子涨落（quantum proton fluctuations）和倒易空间收敛（reciprocal-space convergence）是预测强氢键分子材料光学光谱所需的合作但物理上独立的两个要素。

Abstract: Near-UV optical absorption is increasingly reported in hydrogen-bonded organic and biomolecular materials lacking aromatic or extended pi-conjugated chromophores, yet its microscopic origin remains unresolved and electronic-structure calculations often overestimate experimental absorption onsets. Here, we combine machine-learned interatomic potentials for large-scale classical and quantum nuclear sampling with periodic excited-state calculations to address this discrepancy in L-pyroglutamine ammonium, an experimentally established glutamine-derived crystal containing a well-resolved short hydrogen bond and exhibiting non-aromatic near-UV optical response. Using controlled in silico ion substitutions that vary the surrounding hydrogen-bond environment while preserving this scaffold, we compute optical spectra from configurations sampled along classical and quantum nuclear trajectories using hybrid-functional time-dependent density functional theory. We show that nuclear quantum effects stabilise proton-sharing configurations that are strongly suppressed classically, redshifting the lowest bright excitations by 0.5-0.8 eV and raising the fraction of configurations with bright excitations below 6 eV from approximately 3% to approximately 30%. Explicit Brillouin-zone sampling provides a further, mechanistically distinct redshift of 0.5-1.1 eV, reflecting modest but significant indirect electronic character. Only when both effects are incorporated does the calculated onset recover the experimental 3.8-4.5 eV range. These results establish quantum proton fluctuations and reciprocal-space convergence as cooperative but physically distinct ingredients required for predictive optical spectroscopy of strongly hydrogen-bonded molecular materials.

</details>


### [139] [Polyatomic Thermal Radiative Dissociation in Microcavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24866)
*Enes Suyabatmaz,Tuan Nguyen,Raphael F. Ribeiro*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个态分辨主方程框架，研究多原子分子在平面Au/MgO多层微腔中的黑体红外解离（BIRD）现象，发现通过调控电磁态密度（DOS），特别是利用MgO表面声子极化激元的近场增强效应，可以显著改变反应动力学，并提出了Reststrahlen波段DOS工程作为控制红外微腔中多原子BIRD的实用策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑体红外解离（BIRD）过程依赖于环境热光子的吸收，其辐射跃迁速率受电磁态密度（DOS）影响。作者希望通过结构化红外环境（如微腔）来调控热单分子解离反应，探索利用腔量子电动力学（cavity QED）效应控制化学反应动力学的可能性。

Method: 建立了一个态分辨主方程（state-resolved master-equation）框架，研究对象为反应团簇(H₂O)₂Cl⁻，处于平面Au/MgO多层腔中。该框架考虑了非简谐基频、泛频和组合跃迁所采样的态密度（DOS），同时纳入了甲烷缓冲气体的碰撞效应，以分析BIRD与碰撞活化之间的竞争。

Result: MgO表面声子极化激元（surface phonon polaritons）在微腔中心真空气相反应区产生强烈的近场增强效应。短腔且具有较厚极性晶体层的结构由于增强了倏逝表面声子极化激元贡献，产生了最大的BIRD增强效应。腔DOS工程能够改变BIRD与碰撞活化的交叉区域。

Conclusion: Reststrahlen波段（Reststrahlen-band）DOS工程被确立为一种控制红外微腔中多原子BIRD的实用策略，为通过腔结构设计调控化学动力学提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Blackbody infrared radiative dissociation (BIRD) activates molecules through successive absorption of ambient thermal photons until the internal energy reaches a dissociation threshold. Because these radiative transition rates depend on the electromagnetic density of states (DOS), structured infrared environments provide a route to control thermal unimolecular dissociation. Here we develop a state-resolved master-equation framework for polyatomic BIRD in a planar Au/MgO multilayer cavity, where the reactive cluster $\mathrm{(H_2O)_2Cl^-}$ is studied. The cavity modifies the kinetics through the DOS sampled by anharmonic fundamental, overtone, and combination transitions. We show that MgO surface phonon polaritons produce strong near-field enhancements in the central vacuum reaction region of a microcavity. We find that short cavities with thick polar crystal layers yield the largest BIRD enhancements due to enhanced evanescent surface phonon polariton contributions. We further include collisions with a methane bath gas and show that cavity DOS engineering shifts the crossover between BIRD and collisional activation. These results establish Reststrahlen-band DOS engineering as a practical strategy for controlling polyatomic BIRD in infrared microcavities.

### [140] [Temperature distribution measurement on three-phase contact line in liquid nitrogen using two-color temperature-sensitive paint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24533)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低温相变现象在工程应用中至关重要，但三相接触线附近的温度分布因常规红外热成像在极低温下难以应用而缺乏直接测量手段。

Method: 采用双色温度敏感涂料（2C-TSP）技术，将温敏染料与温度不敏感的参比染料集成于单一涂层中，通过发光强度比补偿液-气界面折射与反射造成的光强变化，实现鲁棒的温度测量。

Result: 在110、430和900 W/m²三种热流条件下测得温度场，发现三相接触线处存在局部温度极小值；液体区域平均温度几乎恒定，气体区域温度随热流密度增加而上升，呈现非均匀热结构。

Conclusion: 2C-TSP技术是直接可视化低温三相接触线附近温度场的有效手段，为液氮相变现象研究提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Cryogenic phase-change phenomena play an important role in a wide range of engineering applications, including cryogenic cooling systems, superconducting technologies, and space propulsion systems. In particular, the three-phase contact line is recognized as a key region governing evaporation and heat transfer. However, direct measurements of temperature distributions near cryogenic three-phase contact lines remain limited because conventional infrared thermography becomes increasingly difficult at extremely low temperatures. In this study, a two-color temperature-sensitive paint (2C-TSP) technique was applied to visualize the temperature field around a liquid-nitrogen three-phase contact line. A temperature-sensitive dye and a temperature-insensitive reference dye were incorporated into a single coating, enabling robust temperature measurements based on luminescence intensity ratios by compensating for changes in optical intensity caused by refraction and reflection at the liquid-gas interface. Temperature distributions were measured under three heating conditions with heat fluxes of 110, 430, and 900 W/m2. The measured temperature fields revealed a localized temperature minimum at the observed three-phase contact line, suggesting localized cooling associated with phase change. Quantitative analysis showed that the average temperature in the liquid region remained nearly constant, whereas the temperature in the gas region increased with increasing heat flux. These observations reveal a non-uniform thermal structure around the cryogenic three-phase contact line. The present results demonstrate that 2C-TSP is a promising technique for direct visualization of temperature fields around cryogenic three-phase contact lines and provides new insights into phase-change phenomena in liquid nitrogen.

### [141] [The Physics of Topological Defects in Glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24376)
*Arabinda Bera,Peter Schall,Timothy W. Sirk,Vijayakumar Chikkadi,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本综述系统总结了玻璃态材料中拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的最新研究进展，涵盖理论概念、数值模拟与实验观测，并探讨了建立非晶固体塑性与力学失效统一拓扑描述的未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体材料中拓扑缺陷的力学行为已被广泛理解，而其在非晶固体（amorphous solids）中的相关性直到近年才被认识。该领域快速发展，亟需一次全面的综述来整合理论、计算与实验成果。

Method: 本文是一篇综述（review），通过梳理近年来理论、计算和实验研究，系统介绍了拓扑缺陷在玻璃中的存在证据（如振动本征模、非仿射位移场和变形诱导矢量场中的拓扑不变量），并讨论了Burgers矢量、非仿射塑性（non-affine plasticity）、振动模式（vibrational modes）和拓扑不变量（topological invariants）等核心概念。

Result: 研究表明，玻璃中的拓扑缺陷与软区（soft spots）、局域塑性重排（localized plastic rearrangements）、屈服（yielding）以及剪切带（shear-band）形成存在强关联，为无序材料塑性的微观起源提供了新视角。

Conclusion: 综述评估了当前领域的成就、局限和开放问题，指出了未来建立非晶固体塑性与力学失效统一拓扑描述的研究方向。

Abstract: Topological defects play a central role in the mechanical behavior of crystalline materials, yet their relevance to amorphous solids has only recently begun to emerge. Over the last few years, theoretical, computational, and experimental studies have revealed the presence of well-defined topological invariants in vibrational eigenmodes, non-affine displacement fields, and deformation-induced vector fields of glasses. These defects have been shown to correlate strongly with soft spots, localized plastic rearrangements, yielding, and shear-band formation, suggesting a new perspective on the microscopic origins of plasticity in disordered materials. In this review, we provide a comprehensive overview of recent developments in the rapidly growing field of topological defects in glasses. We discuss the underlying theoretical concepts, including Burgers vectors, non-affine plasticity, vibrational modes, and topological invariants, and review recent numerical and experimental advances. Finally, we assess the current achievements, limitations, and open questions, and discuss future directions toward a unified topological description of plasticity and mechanical failure in amorphous solids.

### [142] [Anderson localization on the Bethe lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24671)
*Dafne Prado Bandeira,Angelica Vecchiarelli,Marco Tarzia*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文对贝特晶格（Bethe lattice）上的安德森局域化（Anderson localization）提供了教学性综述，聚焦于格林函数（Green's function）形式和空穴方法（cavity approach），推导了自洽方程，讨论了局域化的诊断方法、临界行为及其与定向聚合物（directed polymers）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝特晶格上的安德森局域化是无限维极限下可解析处理的量子相变模型，同时为多体构型空间中的局域化提供了平均场（mean-field）描述，因此需要一套系统的教学框架来阐明其解析与数值方法。

Method: 采用减除函数（resolvent）/格林函数形式和空穴方法，推导了对角减除函数的空穴自洽方程；通过总体动力学（population dynamics）进行数值求解，并在大连接数极限下进行解析处理。

Result: 建立了局域态密度（local density of states）的全概率分布作为相变的自然序参量；获得了临界无序强度、临界行为、绝缘相中的局域化长度以及退局域相中的关联体积。

Conclusion: 该框架系统地揭示了贝特晶格上安德森局域化的统计特征，并与随机介质中的定向聚合物问题建立了联系，通过稀有的共振路径和冻结现象加以解释。

Abstract: Anderson localization is a paradigmatic disorder-driven quantum phase transition in which interference effects can completely suppress wave propagation. Its formulation on the Bethe lattice -- an infinite tree with fixed coordination number -- provides a unique setting in which the transition becomes analytically tractable. Owing to its exponential volume growth, the Bethe lattice realizes the infinite-dimensional limit of the Anderson problem and also serves as a useful mean-field-like description of localization in many-body configuration spaces.
  These lecture notes provide a pedagogical review of Anderson localization on the Bethe lattice, focusing on the resolvent (Green's function) formalism and the cavity approach. We discuss the main diagnostics of localization and show how they are encoded in the statistical properties of Green's functions, with the full probability distribution of the local density of states emerging as the natural order parameter of the transition. We derive the cavity self-consistent equations for the diagonal resolvent and review both their numerical solution by population dynamics and their analytical treatment in the large-connectivity limit. This framework gives access to the critical disorder and the critical behavior near the transition, including the localization length in the insulating phase and the correlation volume that controls the delocalized phase. We also discuss the connection with directed polymers in random media and its interpretation in terms of rare resonant paths and freezing phenomena.
  These notes originated from a series of lectures delivered by one of the authors at the Oropa Summer School on "Fundamental Problems in Statistical Physics XVI" (July 2025).

</details>


### [143] [On the localization transition from MAA to AA models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24720)
*Hangdong Qiu,Yunhua Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文构建了一种新的双准周期镶嵌Aubry-André（DMAA）模型，通过叠加两个准周期势场，揭示了从MAA模型到AA模型的局域化转变演化过程，发现了多重局域化-退局域化转变，并通过数值模拟和连续模型实验验证了其可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 镶嵌Aubry-André（MAA）模型允许迁移边（mobility edges）的存在，而Aubry-André（AA）模型则没有。为了揭示从MAA到AA模型的局域化转变（localization transition）演化过程，需要构建一个能够连接两者的新模型。

Method: 设计了一个双准周期MAA（DMAA）模型，由一个非零偶数位势的原始MAA模型和一个非零奇数位势且带有可调振幅因子的修正MAA模型叠加构成。通过逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）、归一化参与率（normalized participation ratio）、分形维数（fractal dimension）和实空间波函数分布等数值计算，以及连续模型中对实验极化激元（polariton）模式的模拟进行验证。

Result: DMAA模型中扩展态（extended states）、临界态（critical states）和局域态（localized states）之间的相互作用与竞争，在原有的单一局域化转变之外，产生了新的双重和多重局域化-退局域化转变。数值计算和连续模型模拟结果均一致，并验证了其实验可行性。

Conclusion: 构建的DMAA模型为研究两个相似准周期模型之间的局域化转变过程提供了一个新框架，并拓展了对安德森局域化（Anderson localization）的理解。

Abstract: Despite their potential similarity between the mosaic Aubry-André (MAA) and AA models, the MAA model allows mobility edges (MEs), whereas the AA model does not. Here we develop a new double quasiperiodic MAA (DMAA) model consisting of one primitive MAA with nonzero even-site potentials and the other modified one with both nonzero odd-site potentials and a tunable amplitude factor, to reveal how localization transitions evolve from MAA to AA models. Interplays and competitions among the extended, critical and localized states arising from superpositions of double quasi-periodic MAA potentials enable new twice and multiple localization-delocalization transitions besides the original single localization transition. Our numerical calculations on inverse participation ratio, normalized participation ratio, fractal dimension and real-space wavefunction distribution confirm such localization features. The continuum model simulations on the experimental polariton modes also yield consistent results and hence validate their experimental feasibility. The constructed DMAA model provides a new framework for studying the localization transition processes between two analogous quasiperiodic models and broadens the understanding of Anderson localization.

</details>

### [144] [Fermi surface change and $d$-wave superconductivity in the square lattice Kondo-Heisenberg model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23799)
*Alexander Nikolaenko,Riccardo Rende,Luciano Loris Viteritti,Subir Sachdev,Ya-Hui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 利用神经网络量子态（neural network quantum states）研究二维Kondo-Heisenberg模型在非半满导电电子条件下的基态相图，发现弱Kondo耦合下的Néel反铁磁序与仅包含导电电子的费米面（Fermi surface）、强耦合下的重费米液体（heavy Fermi liquid）与包含导电电子和自旋的费米面，以及过渡区的d_{x^2-y^2}超导电性，确立了费米体积（Fermi volume）变化和非传统超导作为该模型的本征特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二维Kondo-Heisenberg模型中Kondo耦合与Heisenberg耦合强度变化对基态相图的影响，特别是费米面（Fermi surface）体积变化和非传统超导电性（unconventional superconductivity）的起源。

Method: 采用神经网络量子态（neural network quantum states）作为变分波函数，在正方晶格（square lattice）上求解导电电子远离半满填充的二维Kondo-Heisenberg模型，并扫描Kondo耦合与Heisenberg耦合参数以映射基态相图。

Result: 弱Kondo耦合区出现反铁磁Néel序（antiferromagnetic Néel order），费米面包围面积仅计及导电电子且不受Néel序影响；强耦合区形成重费米液体（heavy Fermi liquid），费米面包围面积同时包含导电电子与自旋；过渡区观测到d_{x^2-y^2}超导电性，表现为配对关联中的离域长程序（off-diagonal long-range order）和与磁相共存的配对振幅穹顶（pairing-amplitude dome）。

Conclusion: 费米体积（Fermi volume）变化与非传统超导电性是二维Kondo-Heisenberg模型的本征特征，并非由晶格缺陷或其他外部因素引入。

Abstract: We study the two-dimensional Kondo-Heisenberg model on a square lattice, with the conduction electrons away from half-filling, using neural network quantum states. Mapping the ground-state phase diagram as a function of the Kondo and Heisenberg couplings, we identify (i) at weak Kondo coupling, antiferromagnetic Néel order with a Fermi surface whose enclosed area counts only the conduction electrons and is insensitive to the Néel order, and (ii) at strong coupling, a heavy Fermi liquid with a Fermi surface whose enclosed area counts both the conduction electrons and the spins. In the crossover between these regimes, we find $d_{x^2-y^2}$ superconductivity, evidenced by off-diagonal long-range order in the pair-pair correlations and a pairing-amplitude dome that coexists with the underlying magnetic phase. Our results establish Fermi volume change and unconventional superconductivity as intrinsic features of the two-dimensional Kondo-Heisenberg model.

</details>


### [145] [Topological lattice gauge theory enriched by non-invertible symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28688)

Method: 在量子双模型（quantum double model）中凝聚任意荷代数（algebra of charges），分析所得理论中的定域激发（localised excitations）范畴结构及其超群分次（hypergroup grading）性质，并利用Hopf幺半函子（Hopf monad）编码非可逆对称性的范畴作用。

Result: 证明了凝聚后理论的定域激发范畴构成一个超群分次扩展（hypergroup-graded extension）的去禁闭激发（deconfined excitations）范畴；每个超群元素对应的畴壁（domain wall）以其非可逆方式作用于定域激发，且该作用与幺半结构（monoidal structure）均与超群分次相容；规范操作（gauging）对应计算该Hopf幺半函子上的模范畴（category of modules）。

Conclusion: 所建立的框架可自然推广至由凝聚任意代数获得的更一般的弦网模型（string-net model）理论，为系统研究非可逆对称性富集的拓扑序提供了新的范畴论工具。

Abstract: We use finite group topological lattice gauge theory, also known as the quantum double model, as a lens to explore a notion of topological order enriched by a non-invertible symmetry. For invertible symmetry enriched topological order, there is an established axiomatisation in terms of a G-crossed braided fusion category. We lay the foundations for a generalisation of this notion. By condensing an arbitrary algebra of charges in a quantum double model, we demonstrate that the category of localised excitations in the resulting theory forms a hypergroup-graded extension of the category of deconfined excitations. For every element in the hypergroup, the associated domain wall acts in a typically non-invertible way on these localised excitations. Both this action and the monoidal structure are compatible with the hypergroup grading. The actual categorical action is encoded in a Hopf monad on the category of localised excitations, and gauging the non-invertible symmetry amounts to computing the category of modules over this Hopf monad. Finally, we outline how this framework naturally extends to theories obtained by condensing algebras in a generic string-net model.

### [146] [Domain-wall drift in a ferrimagnet induced by a linearly oscillating in-plane magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23831)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索线性振荡面内磁场能否驱动亚铁磁畴壁产生净运动，并阐明其背后的惯性自旋动力学（inertial spin dynamics）机制。

Method: 从包含场致动能贡献的亚铁磁拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）出发，推导畴壁位置和方位角的集体坐标（collective-coordinate）方程；随后通过微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulations）验证解析预测。

Result: 在振荡面内磁场与弱静态面外偏置磁场共同作用下，畴壁角的周期性切换可被整流为有限平均畴壁速度；低驱动频率下漂移速度正比于频率而非场幅值；高于截止频率后平均运动被抑制；漂移幅度和方向可由净自旋密度（net spin density）调控。

Abstract: We investigate ferrimagnetic domain-wall dynamics under linearly oscillating in-plane magnetic fields. Starting from a ferrimagnetic Lagrangian that retains the field-dependent contribution to the kinetic energy, we derive collective-coordinate equations for the domain-wall position and azimuthal angle. This formulation makes explicit the field-induced inertial terms, including Coriolis-, Euler-, and centrifugal-like contributions, and clarifies how they couple translational and azimuthal dynamics. For an oscillating in-plane field supplemented by a weak static out-of-plane bias field, we show that periodic switching of the wall angle can be rectified into a finite average domain-wall velocity. At low drive frequencies, where the wall angle follows the oscillating field, the induced drift is proportional to the drive frequency rather than the field amplitude, while above a cutoff frequency the wall angle can no longer follow the drive and the average motion is suppressed. Micromagnetic simulations confirm the analytical predictions and demonstrate that the magnitude and direction of the drift can be tuned by the net spin density. These results identify linearly oscillating fields as a mechanism for frequency-controlled domain-wall motion in ferrimagnets and highlight the role of inertial spin dynamics near magnetic compensation.

Abstract: Ruddlesden--Popper nickelates have emerged as a promising platform for high-temperature superconductivity, yet the role of lattice degrees of freedom in their correlated normal state remains largely unexplored. Here, we report the observation of a finite phonon thermal Hall effect in the trilayer nickelate La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ at ambient pressure. Remarkably, the thermal Hall response is strongly enhanced below the density-wave transition at $T^*\approx140$ K, exhibiting two distinct plateaus in the thermal Hall resistivity. The characteristic energy scale extracted from the thermal Hall response ($\sim4.1$ meV) closely matches the magnon--phonon crossing span energy ($\sim3.2$ meV), pointing to magnon--phonon hybridization as the primary mechanism enhancing the thermal Hall effect. ### [148] [Fluctuation exchange study on the electron-hole asymmetry of the superconductivity across 1/3 filling in the trilayer Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24126)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用涨落交换近似（fluctuation exchange approximation）分析三层哈伯德模型；考察小U和大U两种情况下能带填充接近1/3时的超导行为，并对比电子掺杂与空穴掺杂侧的差异。

Result: 当U较小时，超导电性呈现近似的电子-空穴对称性（electron-hole symmetric behavior），符合近半填充双能带系统的预期。当U增大时，出现不对称性，空穴掺杂侧（hole-doped regime）更有利于超导；该不对称性源于大U下成键（bonding）、非成键（nonbonding）和反成键（antibonding）能带的非对称重整化（asymmetric renormalization）。

Conclusion: 三层哈伯德模型中的超导电性在弱关联（小U）时具有电子-空穴对称性，而在强关联（大U）时对称性破缺，空穴掺杂更有利于超导，其物理机制是不同能带在大U下的重整化差异。

Abstract: We study within the fluctuation exchange approximation the trilayer Hubbard model where three layers of the Hubbard model are coupled by large interlayer hoppings so that the overlap of the bonding, nonbonding, and antibonding bands is relatively small. We pay special attention to the band fillings close to 1/3, for which the bonding and nonbonding bands as a whole are close to half filling. For relatively small values of the onsite $U$, superconductivity roughly exhibits electron-hole symmetric behavior, as expected for a nearly half-filled two-band system. By contrast, an asymmetry appears when $U$ becomes large, where superconductivity is more favored in the hole-doped regime, i.e., in the regime where electrons are removed from 1/3 filling. We attribute this asymmetry to the asymmetric renormalization of the bonding, nonbonding, and antibonding bands when $U$ is large.

Abstract: We investigate the electronic and magnetic properties of the polar $\sqrt{3}\times\sqrt{3}$ charge-density-wave (CDW) phase of CrSe$_2$ using ab initio calculations. The CDW introduces a polar distortion out of the van der Waals plane that couples to the spin-polarized Cr d states resulting in a remarkably flat electronic band exactly at the Fermi level. We provide a microscopic understanding of the origin of the flat band by analyzing in detail the structural reconstruction, the effects of orbital hybridization, crystal-field splittings, spin-orbit coupling and electronic correlations. Our calculations show that due to the polar nature of the CDW distortion, an electric field can act as an external switch to induce the CDW phase, providing a way to manipulate strong correlations in the system.

### [150] [On Degeneracies of Density, Magnetic, and Pairing Responses: How Competing Orders Echo Underlying Symmetries in the Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24755)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用无阻挫二部哈伯德模型的赝自旋对称性，解析推导出电荷、自旋和配对磁化率对一般空间调制的相互关系；并结合双粒子（two-particle）数值模拟，研究二维情形下短程自旋涨落驱动的d波配对与d密度波（环流）不稳定性。

Result: 发现金属-绝缘体转变附近同时出现d波配对与d密度波（loop current）的不稳定性，这种简并由短程自旋涨落（short-ranged spin fluctuations）驱动；几何阻挫（geometric frustration）逐渐解除该简并并有利于超导。

Conclusion: 该研究为揭示关联电子系统中的对称性关系提供了一种通用工具，并在电荷/环流序、配对序及自旋序等相互交织的序之间建立了统一视角。

Abstract: Strongly correlated electron systems often display competing or even intertwined ordering tendencies, hinting to extremely close or degenerate many-electron energies. While degeneracies are directly rooted in the underlying symmetries of the problem under investigation, their multifaceted effects on different response functions and their mutual relations often remain elusive. Here we put this subject on a rigorous basis by investigating the degeneracies of charge, spin, and pairing susceptibilities for the unfrustrated, bipartite Hubbard model. Exploiting its pseudospin symmetry, we analytically derive the mutual relations between these response functions for generic spatial modulations, highly relevant, e.g., for the competition of stripe and superconducting orders. By means of two-particle numerical simulations we demonstrate the occurrence of a simultaneous $d$-wave pairing/$d$-density wave (loop current) instability in the vicinity of the metal-insulator transition, driven by short-ranged spin fluctuations for the two-dimensional case. We show how this degeneracy is gradually lifted by geometrical frustration, which favors superconductivity. Our study provides a general tool for revealing symmetry relations in correlated electron systems and establishes a unifying perspective on the nature of their intermingled charge/loop current, pairing, and spin orders.

Abstract: Charge order driven by electron-phonon coupling is well understood at equilibrium but pump-probe experiments raise a new question: how does this order melt and recover after strong photoexcitation? A pump pulse promotes carriers across the charge-order gap and creates a nonequilibrium high-energy electronic population. In a closed system the subsequent dynamics is constrained by energy conservation. In an `open system' - where the system is coupled to a thermal bath at some temperature $T_{\rm bath}$ - there are new fluctuation and dissipation processes at play. One can attempt a computational scheme that incorporates coupling of electrons to a laser pump, the coupling of system phonons to a thermal bath, and the Holstein interaction that couples electrons and phonons. We attempt an approximation where the pump induced electronic excitations are modeled by a slowly time varying `electron temperature', $T_{\rm el}(t)$, indicative of a quasi-equilibrium electronic state. We solve the problem for different combinations of $T_{\rm el}$ and $T_{\rm bath}$, probing the order parameter dynamics, the static properties and excitations in the long time `quasi steady state', and establish a `phase diagram' in terms of bath temperature and electron temperature.

### [152] [Introduction to matrix-product states and tensor networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24803)
*Grégoire Misguich*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文为2026年Les Houches暑期学校编写的讲义笔记，系统介绍了量子多体物理中的张量网络（tensor-network）方法，以矩阵乘积态（MPS）为核心，涵盖其基础语言、核心算法、高维推广（投影纠缠对态，PEPS）以及在混合态、量子信道和林德布拉德动力学（Lindblad dynamics）中的应用，并附有基于ITensor的Julia代码示例。

Method: 首先建立张量网络的基本语言，包括图形表示（graphical notation）、虚拟指标（virtual indices）、键维数（bond dimensions）、规范自由度（gauge freedom）、规范形式（canonical forms）以及QR分解和奇异值分解（singular-value decomposition），并阐述纠缠（entanglement）对表示效率的控制作用。随后介绍MPS的核心算法，包括收缩（contractions）、关联函数（correlation functions）、矩阵乘积算符（matrix-product operators）、密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）和时间演化方法。进一步讨论PEPS作为MPS的高维推广及其近似收缩的基本思路。最后将张量网络表示扩展到混合态（mixed states）、量子信道（quantum channels）和林德布拉德动力学，应用于热态（thermal states）和开放量子系统（open quantum systems）。讲义全程辅以基于ITensor、ITensorMPS和TensorMixedStates的短Julia代码示例。

Result: 本文未报告具体数值结果或性能比较。作为教学讲义，其成果体现在系统性地整合了从MPS基础到开放量子系统应用的完整知识体系，并提供了可执行的代码示例以增强可操作性。

Conclusion: 张量网络方法为量子多体系统的数值模拟提供了强大且统一的框架，MPS在处理一维强关联系统方面尤为高效，而PEPS等扩展则有望应用于更高维系统。该讲义为学习者提供了从基础理论到代码实现的全方位入门引导，有助于推动张量网络方法在开放量子系统等前沿领域的应用。

Abstract: These notes provide an introduction to tensor-network methods in quantum many-body physics, with an emphasis on matrix-product states (MPS). They develop the basic tensor-network language, including graphical notation, virtual indices, bond dimensions, gauge freedom, canonical forms, QR and singular-value decompositions, and the role of entanglement in controlling the efficiency of the representation. The main MPS algorithms are then introduced, including contractions, correlation functions, matrix-product operators, DMRG, and time-evolution methods. The notes also briefly discuss projected entangled-pair states (PEPS) as a higher-dimensional generalization of MPS, together with the basic ideas behind approximate PEPS contraction. Finally, tensor-network representations of mixed states, quantum channels, and Lindblad dynamics are presented, with applications to thermal states and open quantum systems. The presentation is accompanied by short Julia code examples based on ITensor, ITensorMPS, and TensorMixedStates. These notes were written for the 9th Les Houches Summer School on Computational Physics: Open Quantum Systems, held in June 2026.

</details>


### [153] [THz-induced phonon mode mixing and collective dynamics in a polar nanolattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24804)
*Elizabeth Skoropata,Peter M. Derlet,Hiroki Ueda,Roman Mankowsky,Mathias Sander,Henrik T. Lemke,Rafael T. Winkler,Yunpei Deng,Milan Radovic,Matteo Savoini,Biaolong Liu,Martina Basini,Vladimir Ovuka,Steven L. Johnson,Marta D. Rossell,Urs Staub*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过超快X射线衍射与分子动力学模拟，研究了SrTiO₃薄膜中纳米级有序界面位错网络在太赫兹激发下的动力学，发现跨尺度的对称性破缺可产生具有涡旋状位移的新型集体模式，为通过外延控制实空间拓扑以探索动态功能特性开辟了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的声子操控通常局限于通过应变、掺杂或光照等手段改变单胞（unit-cell）结构。本文旨在超越单胞尺度，探索更高阶结构（如有序界面位错网络）对波散射与干涉效应的控制，以发现新的动态响应与集体模式。

Method: 采用二维和三维时间分辨X射线衍射（time-resolved x-ray diffraction）与经典分子动力学模拟（classical molecular dynamics simulations），探测具有纳米级有序界面位错网络的SrTiO₃薄膜在太赫兹（THz）激发下的动力学行为。

Result: 研究发现，跨所有尺度的对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）是产生动态电极化（dynamical electric polarization）的有效途径，并能控制声子混合（phonon mixing），从而在太赫兹频段生成此前未报道的、具有环形涡旋状位移（circular vortex-like displacements）的集体模式。

Conclusion: 该工作开辟了一条通过外延（epitaxy）控制实空间拓扑（real-space topology）来探索动态功能性质的新路径，并可拓展至磁性、电学及铁电系统。

Abstract: Manipulating phonons through symmetry is a fundamental approach to alter the dynamic responses of materials. Most often new phases are sought through control of the unit-cell (e.g. via strain, doping, light, etc.). By comparison, there is vast potential to look beyond the unit-cell into higher-order architectures to control wave scattering and interference effects that remains less explored. We describe the THz-induced dynamics of an SrTiO$_{3}$ thin film with a nanoscale ordered interfacial dislocation network probed with 2- and 3-dimensional time-resolved x-ray diffraction and classical molecular dynamics simulations. We find that symmetry breaking at all scales is an effective approach to create a dynamical electric polarization and to control phonon mixing that generates previously unreported collective modes in the THz regime with circular vortex-like displacements. This work opens a new pathway to explore dynamical functional properties that can be extended to magnetic, electric, and ferroelectric systems by controlling the real-space topology via epitaxy.

### [154] [Zeta-regularization and natural boundaries: Sums and products of integers and primes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24536)
*P. L. Krapivsky,J. M. Luck*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文在超越素数ζ函数自然边界的基础上，首次实现了“所有素数之和”的正则化，并将整数与素数的正则化乘积推广至九个虚二次域（imaginary quadratic fields），建立了整数乘积与素数乘积之间的幂律关系（power-law relationship）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Euler通过zeta正则化（zeta-regularization）技巧给出了所有自然数乘积的有限值，但该方法因素数ζ函数（prime zeta function）沿虚轴存在自然边界（natural boundary）而无法用于所有素数之积。Muñoz García与Pérez-Marco虽通过自然边界上导数正则化得到素数积为$4π^2$，但如何正则化所有素数之和以及将此框架推广至更一般的数域仍是开放问题。

Method: 首先，借助在自然边界之外有限距离处的解析延拓（analytic continuation），对素数ζ函数在原点处的导数进行重新正则化，从而定义所有素数之和。其次，将这一正则化方法应用于九个虚二次域（包括高斯整数（Gauss integers）和艾森斯坦整数（Eisenstein integers）），分别计算域中整数与素数的正则化乘积，并推导二者间的幂律关系。

Result: 成功实现了所有素数之和的正则化，得到了有限且自洽的数值结果。在九个具有唯一因子分解性质的虚二次域中，分别确定了所有整数与所有素数的正则化乘积值，并建立了二者之间的通用幂律关系。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅扩展了正则化乘积在数论中的应用范围，还指出当相关zeta函数出现自然边界时，标准的zeta正则化技术在物理情境中也同样失效，因而本文方法具有超越数论的更广泛意义。

Abstract: Euler regularized the divergent product of all natural numbers and found beautiful formulas for regularized sums of integer powers of natural numbers. These derivations essentially relied on what is now called the zeta-regularization technique, although analytical continuation had not yet been invented. This classic method is however not applicable to the product of all primes, as the prime zeta function has a natural boundary along the imaginary axis. Muñoz García and Pérez-Marco overcame this obstacle and evaluated the product of all primes to $4π^2$ by finding an appropriately regularized value of the derivative of the prime zeta function at the origin, lying on the natural boundary. We extend their approach in two novel directions. First, we show how to make sense of the sum of all primes. This regularization requires going a finite distance beyond the natural boundary. Second, we determine the regularized products of integers and primes in the nine imaginary quadratic fields where integers have a unique factorization into primes, and establish a general power-law relationship between products of integers and primes. Two well-known examples are Gauss and Eisenstein integers. The interest in this approach goes beyond number theory. In a variety of physical situations, the zeta-regularization technique is indeed not applicable because the relevant zeta function has a natural boundary.

</details>

### [155] [Modern tidal interaction models for rapid binary population synthesis: II. Binary black hole formation, mergers, and spins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23773)
*Veome Kapil,Ilya Mandel,Jeff Riley,Evgeni Grishin,Jim Fuller,Emanuele Berti*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 利用双星快速布居合成代码COMPAS并结合自洽的潮汐耗散新模型，对孤立双星演化形成的双黑洞并合率及有效自旋（χ_eff）分布进行了预测。研究表明，第二代黑洞的自旋显著依赖于潮汐耗散效率与质量传递历史，且高χ_eff双星优先在高红移处并合，当前引力波探测器观测到的自旋分布被严重偏向低χ_eff，但随着探测器灵敏度向高红移拓展，高χ_eff系统比例将上升至约15%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确预测双黑洞（binary black holes, BBHs）的并合率和有效自旋（χ_eff）分布，对于理解孤立双星演化通道的物理机制以及指导当前及未来引力波（gravitational wave, GW）探测器的观测策略具有重要意义。

Method: 采用快速双星布居合成代码COMPAS，引入一种新型的自洽潮汐耗散（tidal dissipation）实现方案，对孤立双星演化过程进行大规模数值模拟，从而预测双黑洞系统的并合率与χ_eff分布。

Result: 大部分第一代黑洞（black holes, BHs）以零自旋形成（化学均匀演化通道除外）；第二代黑洞的自旋强烈依赖于潮汐耗散效率和质量传递历史，且并非总与前超新星同步化一致。高χ_eff双星因形成时双星间距小、并合时间短而在高红移优先并合。当前探测器下，本征自旋分布严重偏向低χ_eff，约三分之一系统χ_eff<0.05，仅约3%系统的χ_eff>0.5；但当探测器灵敏度提升至可探测更高红移源时，χ_eff>0.5的系统比例可上升至约15%。

Conclusion: 孤立双星演化形成的双黑洞本征自旋分布具有显著的低χ_eff偏向，而当前引力波探测器观测到的偏向更为明显；随着探测器对高红移源的敏感性增强，未来观测到的χ_eff分布将向高值方向移动，从而为检验潮汐耗散模型和双星演化通道提供关键约束。

Abstract: We present predictions for the merger rates and effective spin ($χ_{\rm eff}$) distribution of binary black holes (BBHs) from isolated binary evolution, using a new self-consistent tidal dissipation implementation in the rapid binary population synthesis code COMPAS. Most of the first-born black holes (BHs) in our simulated merging BBHs are formed with zero spins, with the exception of BBHs formed from chemically homogeneous evolution. The spins of the second-born BHs with the new model depend significantly on the efficiency of tidal dissipation and mass transfer history, and crucially, are not always consistent with pre-supernova synchronization. High-$χ_{\rm eff}$ binaries preferentially merge at high redshift due to smaller binary separations at BBH formation and shorter coalescence times, thus rendering them largely inaccessible to current gravitational wave (GW) detectors. We expect the intrinsic spin distribution of merging BBHs formed from isolated evolution to be strongly biased toward low $χ_{\rm eff}$ with current detectors, with a third of systems having $χ_{\rm eff} < 0.05$ and only $\sim 3\%$ with $χ_{\rm eff}>0.5$. However, $χ_{\rm eff}$ will increase as GW detectors become sensitive to higher redshift sources, with up to $\sim 15\%$ of systems having $χ_{\rm eff}>0.5$.

### [156] [A Collapsar-Disk Origin for GW190814](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23786)
*Vishal Baibhav,Brian D. Metzger,Lam Hui*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出GW190814引力波事件源自坍缩星盘（collapsar disk）碎裂形成的致密天体与中心黑洞合并，并预测该事件前应存在剥离包层超新星（stripped-envelope supernova），候选体为SN2019npv；同时探讨了三体相互作用导致的长时标合并延迟及其电磁对应体与宇宙学应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW190814事件的极端质量比（~23 M☉黑洞与2.6 M☉致密天体）难以通过标准孤立双星或动力学形成通道解释，因此需要新的形成机制来描述该事件起源。

Method: 基于中微子冷却的坍缩星盘（neutrino-cooled collapsar disk）引力不稳定碎裂模型，提出盘碎片与中心黑洞合并产生GW190814；通过三体相互作用（three-body interactions）解释碎片轨道激发与长时标合并延迟，并与候选超新星SN2019npv的时间关联进行分析。

Result: 识别出SN2019npv（Ib型超新星候选体）位于GW190814的置信体积内，在并合前约60天发生；三体相互作用可产生数周至数月的合并延迟；若将SN2019npv作为宿主，GW190814可作为标准汽笛（standard siren）给出H0 = 70.5 (+9.2, -6.4) km/s/Mpc。

Conclusion: GW190814可能由坍缩星盘碎片与中心黑洞合并产生，该通道可预测与超新星的时间关联，并为未来引力波事件的电磁对应体搜寻和哈勃常数测量提供新途径。

Abstract: GW190814 was a remarkable gravitational-wave (GW) event: a merger between a 23 solar-mass black hole (BH) and a 2.6 solar-mass compact object, with an extreme mass ratio that is difficult to reproduce through standard isolated-binary or dynamical formation channels. Recent work has shown that neutrino-cooled collapsar disks can become gravitationally unstable and fragment, producing neutron stars (NSs) or low-mass BHs in orbit around the newly formed central BH. These fragments may subsequently interact, scatter, merge with one another, or inspiral into the central remnant. We propose that GW190814 originated from such a collapsar-disk fragment merging with the central BH. A key prediction of this scenario is a temporal association with a stripped-envelope supernova preceding the GW event, and we identify the Type Ib supernova candidate SN2019npv, which occurred inside the GW190814 credible volume approximately 60 days before coalescence, as a possible electromagnetic precursor. Although this delay is too long for a conventional kilonova counterpart, we show that three-body interactions among disk fragments can excite some compact objects to wide orbits and naturally produce merger delays of weeks to months. While GW190814 itself was not expected to produce detectable tidal-disruption-powered emission, future delayed mergers in this channel could generate luminous transients through either reprocessed kilonova heating or shocks driven as merger ejecta collide with the preceding supernova ejecta. Finally, treating SN2019npv as the host makes GW190814 a bright standard siren and yields H_0 = 70.5 (+9.2, -6.4) km/s/Mpc.

</details>
