### [157] [Yielding versus random organization: convex absorbing transitions in soft matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23914)
*Tristan Jocteur,Kirsten Martens,Eric Bertin,Romain Mari*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过比较广义随机组织模型（ROM）和弹塑性模型，发现两者在吸收相变中共享一种非局部活性产生机制，均表现出凸相变（β>1），并通过长程相互作用的衰减指数α揭示了从凹相变到凸相变的平滑交叉，最终在参数化表示中与长程守恒定向逾渗类和Hébraud-Lequeux型平均场行为相联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解软物质系统中两种不同模型（随机组织模型与弹塑性模型）在吸收相变（absorbing phase transition）行为上的共性与差异，尤其是长程相互作用如何影响临界性质。

Method: 比较广义随机组织模型（描述循环剪切悬浮液的频闪动力学）和弹塑性模型（描述屈服应力流体在施加应力下的介观动力学），分析两者在不同长程相互作用衰减指数α下的临界性质，包括活性均值与涨落、雪崩统计（avalanche statistics）和低波数结构因子（structure factor）。

Result: 两种模型均表现出凸相变（凸性指数β>1），与通常的凹相变（β<1）形成鲜明对比。随α变化观察到从短程相互作用的凹相变（涨落发散、雪崩紧凑）到长程相互作用的凸相变（涨落消失、雪崩非紧凑）的平滑交叉。两种模型在将临界指数作为β的函数进行参数化绘图时表现出良好的一致性。

Conclusion: 凹相变区域与长程守恒定向逾渗（Long-Range Conserved Directed Percolation）类一致；凸相变区域可由基于Hébraud-Lequeux屈服转变模型的平均场图像（含反常扩散）解释。

Abstract: We compare two different soft matter models, a generalized Random Organization Model (ROM) describing the stroboscopic dynamics of cyclically sheared suspensions, and an elastoplastic model describing the mesoscale dynamics of a yield-stress fluid under imposed stress. Both show absorbing phase transitions, sharing a peculiar mechanism: activity induces an internal noise which is transmitted over large distances by long-ranged mediated interactions, either hydrodynamic or elastic, which results in non-local creation of activity. They also both show convex transitions (i.e., the exponent $β>1$), in stark contrast with usual absorbing phase transitions, like (Conserved) Directed Percolation, which are concave ($β<1$). We further compare the dependence of the critical properties (activity mean value and fluctuations, avalanche statistics, low-wavenumber structure factor) on the decay exponent $α$ of long-range interactions in both models, finding a qualitatively similar scenario. A smooth crossover is observed as a function of $α$ between a concave transition regime for short-range interactions, with diverging fluctuations and compact avalanches, and a convex transition regime, with vanishing fluctuations and non-compact avalanches, for longer-range interactions. Although for a given range exponent $α$, the values of critical exponents for both models differ, a good agreement between the models is found by parametrically plotting the different critical exponents as a function of the exponent $β$ of the mean activity. In this parametric representation, the concave regime is consistent with the behavior of the Long-Range Conserved Directed Percolation class, while the convex regime can be accounted for by a mean-field-type scenario with anomalous diffusion close to an absorbing boundary, inspired by the Hébraud-Lequeux model for the yielding transition.

</details>


### [158] [Flexibility Controls Active-Filament Transport in Crowded Landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23921)
*Qingyi Di,Mohammad Fazelzadeh,Sara Jabbari-Farouji*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模布朗动力学模拟，系统探究了主动柔性细丝（active polymer）在有序与无序障碍物阵列中的长时扩散行为。研究发现，细丝柔性对输运的影响取决于介质结构：无序环境中中等柔性优化输运，有序密阵中半柔性细丝通过沿周期性通道的定向运动增强迁移。研究识别出三种输运机制，并揭示长时扩散受限于细丝构象与重取向动力学的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管主动细丝是可变形的活性物质（deformable active matter）的典型范例，但其柔性如何与环境异质性相互作用、进而控制其在拥挤环境中的输运机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用大规模布朗动力学模拟，对切向驱动的主动聚合物在有序与无序障碍物阵列中运动进行模拟，系统扫描障碍物密度和细丝柔性对长时扩散的影响。

Result: 柔性既可增强也可阻碍输运，取决于介质结构。无序环境中中等柔性实现最优输运，高度柔性与半柔性细丝均扩散较慢；有序密阵则促进半柔性细丝沿周期性通道定向运动。识别出三种输运机制：高度柔性细丝的曲折控制扩散、中等柔性细丝的受限辅助输运、半柔性细丝的持续运动控制输运。

Conclusion: 结合理论与模拟表明，长时扩散受限于障碍物导致的细丝构象与重取向动力学改变。该工作揭示了变形活性体在异质环境中的通用输运原理，为主动细丝在复杂多孔景观中的导航提供了预测性框架。

Abstract: Active filaments, ranging from motor-driven biopolymers to elongated bacteria and worms, are paradigmatic examples of deformable active matter. How filament flexibility interacts with environmental heterogeneity to control their transport in crowded environments, however, remains poorly understood. Here, we perform large-scale Brownian dynamics simulations of tangentially driven active polymers moving through ordered and disordered obstacle arrays to map the long-time diffusion as a function of obstacle density and filament flexibility. We find that flexibility can either enhance or hinder transport depending on the structure of the medium. In disordered environments, transport is optimized at intermediate filament flexibility, whereas both highly flexible and semiflexible filaments diffuse more slowly. In contrast, dense ordered arrays enhance the mobility of semiflexible filaments by promoting directed motion along periodic channels. We identify three distinct transport regimes: (i) tortuosity-controlled diffusion of highly flexible filaments, characterized by trapping-and-hopping dynamics; (ii) confinement-assisted transport of moderately flexible filaments, which enhances diffusion in dense media; and (iii) persistence-controlled transport of semiflexible filaments, which facilitates diffusion in dense ordered media, but suppresses it in disordered media. Combining theory and simulations, we show that long-time diffusion is governed by confinement-induced changes in filament conformation and reorientation dynamics. Our work uncovers general transport principles for deformable active agents in heterogeneous environments and provides a predictive framework for active-filament navigation in complex porous landscapes.

</details>


### [159] [Stress-Boundary-Memory Feedback Drives Vortical-Polar Transitions in Softly Confined Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23923)
*Haosheng Wen,P. B. Sunil Kumar,Mohamed Laradji*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本论文通过计算模拟研究活性物质的环境敏感性与软约束（soft confinement）之间的相互作用如何塑造集体动力学。模型将活性组分表示为自推进粒子（self-propelled particles, SPPs），即具有向列序（nematic order）且运动方向可反向的环形聚合物。粗粒化分子动力学模拟揭示出活性应力、边界弹性（boundary elasticity）和粒子级记忆三者之间的三路反馈（three-way feedback）驱动集体行为。随着驱动力（driving force, FD）增大，系统依次经历热涨落主导、相干涡旋运动伴随间歇性反转、持续单向涡旋运动，以及极性态（polar state）——SPPs呈现强烈向列有序、腔体形状对称性破缺，并产生持久的弹道推进（ballistic propulsion）。结果表明边界弹性可作为控制涡旋与弹道动力学平衡的关键参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究活性物质的环境敏感性如何与软约束共同作用，以塑造集体动力学行为。活性物质通常处于软性、可形变的环境中，但这一软约束如何调节集体态尚未被充分理解。

Method: 活性组分建模为向列型、不相交的环形聚合物，即自推进粒子（SPPs），运动方向可无翻滚（tumbling）地反转。采用粗粒化分子动力学（coarse-grained molecular dynamics）模拟，系统考察不同驱动力（FD）下的动力学行为。

Result: 随着FD增加，系统依次出现四个动力学区：热涨落主导区（低FD）；相干涡旋运动伴间歇性反转（中FD）；持续单向涡旋运动（高FD）；极性态（极高FD），表现为SPPs强向列有序、腔体形状对称性破缺、活性粒子聚集于前缘产生弹道推进。

Conclusion: 环境敏感性与软约束共同调控活性物质涌现的集体态，边界弹性（boundary elasticity）可作为控制参数，调节涡旋动力学与弹道动力学之间的平衡。

Abstract: We computationally investigate how environmental sensitivity of active matter interacts with soft confinement to shape collective dynamics. In our model, the active constituents are represented as self-propelled particles (SPPs), implemented as nematic, disjoint ring polymers whose direction of motion can reverse without tumbling. Coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations reveal that collective dynamics arise from a three-way feedback between active stresses, boundary elasticity, and particle-level memory. With increasing driving force, FD, this feedback generates a sequence of collective dynamical regimes. At low FD, SPP motion is dominated by thermal fluctuations. At intermediate FD, coherent vortical motion emerges with intermittent, noise-driven reversals. With further increase in FD, reversals are suppressed, yielding sustained unidirectional vortical motion. At sufficiently high FD, the system transitions to a polar state characterized by strong nematic ordering of the SPPs, symmetry breaking of the enclosure shape, and persistent polar collective motion. In this regime, the SPPs accumulate at the leading edge of the enclosure, driving sustained ballistic propulsion. These results demonstrate how environmental sensitivity and soft confinement jointly regulate emergent collective states and identify boundary elasticity as a control parameter governing the balance between vortical and ballistic dynamics.

</details>


### [160] [Broadband molecular dynamics simulation of fluid inertial effects in confined Brownian motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24291)
*Quentin Thomas,Clara Mefo Sop,Maxime Lavaud,Yacine Amarouchene,Thomas Salez,Pascal Damman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过分子动力学（molecular-dynamics）模拟，研究受限条件下布朗粒子（Brownian particle）的流体动力学记忆效应（hydrodynamic memory），发现靠近刚性壁时速度自相关函数（velocity autocorrelation function）出现各向异性、代数尾修正以及有效附加质量（effective added mass）的显著增强，从而在零频率迁移率（zero-frequency mobility）与高频惯性行为（high-frequency inertial behaviour）之间建立桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然束缚引起的布朗扩散修正已得到充分研究，但束缚如何改变完整的流体动力学响应（hydrodynamic response）仍未被充分探索。

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular-dynamics）模拟，对处于显式溶剂（explicit solvent）中的中性浮力胶体粒子（neutrally buoyant colloidal particle）的速度自相关函数（velocity autocorrelation function）进行宽谱分析。

Result: 在体相（bulk）中，模拟无需可调参数即复现了可压缩性（compressibility）、附加质量（added mass）、流体动力学长时尾（hydrodynamic long-time tail）以及斯托克斯-爱因斯坦扩散（Stokes-Einstein diffusion）。靠近刚性壁时，速度关联呈现各向异性（anisotropic），代数尾（algebraic tails）发生修正，扩散系数降低；最重要的是，短时动力学显示有效附加质量随趋近壁面而显著增强。

Conclusion: 速度自相关函数可作为连接受限布朗粒子零频率迁移率与高频惯性行为的核心物理量。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic memory governs Brownian motion over a broad range of timescales, from acoustic wave propagation at short times to diffusive relaxation at long times. While confinement-induced corrections to Brownian diffusion are well established, how confinement modifies the full hydrodynamic response remains less explored. In this Letter, we use molecular-dynamics simulations of a neutrally buoyant colloidal particle in an explicit solvent to resolve the velocity autocorrelation function across a broad hydrodynamic spectrum. In the bulk, the simulations recover compressibility, added mass, the hydrodynamic long-time tail, and Stokes-Einstein diffusion without adjustable parameters. Near a rigid wall, the velocity correlations become anisotropic, their algebraic tails are modified, and the diffusion coefficients are reduced. Most importantly, the short-time dynamics reveals a pronounced enhancement of the effective added mass as the wall is approached. As such, the velocity autocorrelation function appears as a central quantity to bridge the zero-frequency mobility and the high-frequency inertial behaviour of a confined Brownian particle.

</details>


### [161] [Dynamics and stability of inertial flexible chains under follower activity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24614)
*Sattwik Sadhu,Nitin Kriplani,Raghunath Chelakkot*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟和理论推导，研究了惯性不可忽略条件下受追随活性驱动的柔性可伸展活性粒子链的复杂动力学，揭示了链长、段质量和活性对周期性运动的影响，并分别在短链和长链极限下推导了键长与键角的近似表达式及稳定性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要聚焦于过阻尼极限（overdamped limit）下柔性活性链的动力学行为，而惯性显著条件下的动力学机制尚不清晰。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统研究惯性（inertia）对活性链周期性运动及其稳定性的影响。

Method: 采用数值模拟量化链动力学随链长 N、段质量和活性的变化；同时针对短链（N=3）和长链（N≫1）两种极限情况发展理论描述，推导键长和键角沿链轮廓的近似表达式，并分析周期性运动的稳定性条件。

Result: 短链和长链极限下推导的键长与键角近似表达式与数值结果高度吻合；确定了短链中周期性运动关于段质量和活性的稳定性条件；发现了长链中圆形周期性解（circular, periodic solution）结构失稳的参数区间。

Conclusion: 本文的理论与数值分析揭示了活性链中有序和周期性行为涌现的机制，为理解受追随活性驱动的柔性链在惯性显著条件下的非平衡动力学提供了重要理论框架。

Abstract: The dynamics of flexible polymers and chains under follower activity is known to produce diverse nonequilibrium states. A prominent feature of such systems is the emergence of periodic motion arising from the coupling between internal activity and chain conformation. Recently, it has been shown that flexible and extensible chains of active particles exhibit rich dynamical patterns in the overdamped limit, where inertia is negligible. Here, we study the complex dynamics of a flexible and extensible chain of active particles under follower activity when inertia is significant. Using numerical simulations, we quantify the chain dynamics as a function of chain length ($N$), segment mass, and activity. To rationalize the numerical results, we develop theoretical descriptions in the limit of short chains ($N=3$) and long chains ($N \gg 1$). In both these limits, we derive approximate expressions for the bond lengths and bond angles along the contour, which show excellent agreement with the numerical results. In addition, for short chains, we derive the stability conditions for a periodic motion as a function of segment mass and activity. For long chains ($N\gg1$) we identify parameter regime in which the circular, periodic solution becomes structurally unstable. Our theoretical and numerical analysis provides insights into the emergence of ordered and periodic behaviour in active chains.

### [162] [Limited surface mobility inhibits stable glass formation for 2-ethyl-1-hexanol](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24657)
*M. Tylinski,M. S. Beasley,Y. Z. Chua,C. Schick,M. D. Ediger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过气相沉积（vapor-deposition）制备2-乙基-1-己醇（2-ethyl-1-hexanol）玻璃，发现其动力学稳定性（kinetic stability）高度依赖于沉积速率，且在相同制备时间内远优于液态冷却老化玻璃，支持了表面迁移率（surface mobility）受限是抑制该分子形成高稳定玻璃的关键因素的假说。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明气相沉积可制备具有极高动力学稳定性的有机玻璃，但近期发现部分分子在预期可形成稳定玻璃的条件下仅能获得有限稳定性。本工作旨在探究2-乙基-1-己醇无法在常规沉积条件下形成高稳定玻璃的原因。

Method: 在宽泛的沉积速率范围内气相沉积2-乙基-1-己醇玻璃，测量其等温转变时间（isothermal transformation times）以量化动力学稳定性，并与乙基环己烷（ethylcyclohexane）的沉积速率实验进行对比分析。

Result: 在Tsubstrate = 0.90 Tg条件下，当沉积速率从0.2 nm/s降至0.005 nm/s时，动力学稳定性提升约3个数量级。相同制备时间内，气相沉积玻璃的动力学稳定性远高于液态冷却老化玻璃。2-乙基-1-己醇的表面迁移率在0.85 Tg条件下比乙基环己烷低4个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 2-乙基-1-己醇形成高稳定玻璃受到表面迁移率有限的抑制，沉积速率是决定其动力学稳定性的关键因素。

Abstract: Previous work has shown that vapor-deposition can prepare organic glasses with extremely high kinetic stabilities and other properties that would be expected from liquid-cooled glasses only after aging for thousands of years or more. However, recent reports have shown that some molecules form vapor-deposited glasses with only limited kinetic stability when prepared using conditions expected to yield a stable glass. In this work, we vapor deposit glasses of 2-ethyl-1-hexanol over a wide range of deposition rates and test several hypotheses for why this molecule does not form highly stable glasses under normal deposition conditions. The kinetic stability of 2-ethyl-1-hexanol glasses is found to be highly dependent on the deposition rate. For deposition at Tsubstrate = 0.90 Tg, the kinetic stability increases by 3 orders of magnitude (as measured by isothermal transformation times) when the deposition rate is decreased from 0.2 nm/s to 0.005 nm/s. We also find that, for the same preparation time, a vapor-deposited glass has much more kinetic stability than an aged liquid-cooled glass. Our results support the hypothesis that the formation of highly stable 2-ethyl-1-hexanol glasses is inhibited by limited surface mobility. We compare our deposition rate experiments to similar ones performed with ethylcyclohexane (which readily forms glasses of high kinetic stability); we estimate that the surface mobility of 2-ethyl-1-hexanol is more than 4 orders of magnitude less than that of ethylcyclohexane at 0.85 Tg.

### [163] [Thermal stability of vapor-deposited stable glasses of an organic semiconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24674)
*Diane M. Walters,Ranko Richert,M. D. Ediger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过光谱椭偏仪（spectroscopic ellipsometry）和介电谱（dielectric spectroscopy）等实验手段，研究气相沉积有机玻璃TPD在退火过程中的转化前沿（transformation front）动力学，发现前沿速度随基底温度变化一个数量级以上，而活化能保持不变，表明液体的迁移率和玻璃的结构是控制热稳定性的独立因素，并暗示该类行为具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气相沉积有机玻璃相较于液冷玻璃具有更高的动力学稳定性（kinetic stability），但退火后以恒定速度传播的前沿（propagating fronts）转变为过冷液体（supercooled liquid）。已有研究针对模型玻璃形成体（model glassformers），但对有机半导体材料的转化前沿动力学尚缺乏系统理解，这限制了其在有机电子器件中的应用。

Method: 采用光谱椭偏仪（spectroscopic ellipsometry）和一种新的高通量退火协议（high-throughput annealing protocol），测量了以不同基底温度（0.63至0.96 Tg）制备的TPD玻璃在多个退火温度下的转化前沿速度；同时使用介电谱（dielectric spectroscopy）测量过冷TPD的结构弛豫时间（structural relaxation time）。

Result: 转化前沿速度随基底温度（TSubstrate）变化超过一个数量级，但活化能（activation energy）保持不变；液体的迁移率（mobility）与玻璃的结构（structure）是控制TPD薄膜热稳定性的两个独立因素；与模型玻璃形成体相比，TPD的转化前沿具有相似的速度和基底温度依赖性。

Conclusion: TPD气相沉积玻璃的转化行为与模型玻璃形成体类似，暗示该类动力学稳定玻璃的转化前沿传播具有普适性（universal behavior）。该研究结果有助于设计具有更高热稳定性的有机电子器件活性层（active layers）。

Abstract: Vapor-deposited organic glasses can show enhanced kinetic stability relative to liquid-cooled glasses. When such stable glasses of model glassformers are annealed above the glass transition temperature Tg, they lose their thermal stability and transform into the supercooled liquid via constant velocity propagating fronts. In this work, we show that vapor-deposited glasses of an organic semiconductor, N,N-bis(3-methylphenyl)-N,N-diphenylbenzidine (TPD), also transform via propagating fronts. Using spectroscopic ellipsometry and a new high-throughput annealing protocol, we measure transformation front velocities for TPD glasses prepared with substrate temperatures (TSubstrate) from 0.63 to 0.96 Tg, at many different annealing temperatures. We observe that the front velocity varies by over an order of magnitude with TSubstrate, while the activation energy remains constant. Using dielectric spectroscopy, we measure the structural relaxation time of supercooled TPD. We find that the mobility of the liquid and the structure of the glass are independent factors in controlling the thermal stability of TPD films. In comparison to model glassformers, the transformation fronts of TPD have similar velocities and a similar dependence on TSubstrate, suggesting universal behavior. These results may aid in designing active layers in organic electronic devices with improved thermal stability.

</details>


### [164] [Optical mapping of phases and phase boundaries in nanoconfined fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24809)
*Lauriane Pierrot Deseilligny,Susan Perkin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于表面力平衡法（surface force balance, SFB）的非侵入式方法，实现对受限液体中纳米级成分分布（composition mapping）的测量。通过将传统SFB的顶点测量扩展为折射率分布（refractive index profiles）的空间分辨重构，该方法能够直接获取纳米受限流体界面的位置与几何结构。研究通过空气测量和正庚烷液滴动态蒸发两个模型场景验证了方法的精度与适用范围，并观察到弯液面几何结构从表面张力主导向受限主导的交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在受限空间中，额外的热力学变量会导致流体偏离体相结构（bulk structure）和性质，表面相互作用引起的成分变化可能诱导新相的出现并改变相变行为。因此，亟需一种能够对纳米尺度受限液体进行成分分布表征的非侵入式方法。

Method: 利用表面力平衡法（SFB），将传统SFB分析从顶点测量（apex measurements）扩展为受限流体内部折射率分布（refractive index profiles）的空间分辨重构。当多相共存时，折射率分布可直接揭示纳米受限流体界面的位置与几何形态。研究通过空气测量和受限正庚烷液滴动态蒸发两个模型场景对干涉图分析方法进行详细描述并验证其有效性。

Result: 在空气中测量验证了该方法的高精度，并成功检测到纳米级润湿毛细管（wetting capillary）。在对受限正庚烷液滴动态蒸发的分析中，实现了低至0.1皮升（pL）体积的弯液面几何结构时间分辨重构。尽管蒸发持续驱动系统远离平衡态，弯液面在高度约80 nm以上仍符合悬链面（catenoidal geometry）几何描述；在更小分离距离处，弯液面出现系统性地偏离悬链面轮廓，标志着从表面张力主导（surface tension-dominated regime）向受限主导（confinement-dominated regime）的交叉。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了成分分布分析（composition profiling）作为一种分析框架，可用于分析受限诱导的成分变化（confinement-induced composition variations），并在纳米尺度上定量表征界面热力学效应。该方法为非侵入性研究纳米受限流体中的相行为和界面现象提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: In confined space, deviations from bulk structure and properties are expected due to additional thermodynamic variables. In particular, composition variations arising from surface interactions may lead to additional phases and altered phase transitions. Here, we introduce a non-invasive method for nanoscale composition mapping in confined liquids using the surface force balance (SFB). The method extends conventional SFB analysis from apex measurements to spatially resolved reconstruction of refractive index profiles within confined fluids. When multiple phases are present, the refractive index profiles provide direct access to the position and geometry of the nanoconfined fluid interfaces. We describe the interferogram analysis in detail and establish its range of validity through two model scenarios. First, measurements in air demonstrate the precision of the method and allow detection of a nanometric wetting capillary. Second, we analyse dynamic evaporation of a confined heptane droplet down to 0.1 pL volume. The method provides a time-resolved reconstruction of the meniscus geometry throughout the evaporation process. Although evaporation continuously drives the system out of equilibrium, the meniscus remains well described by a catenoidal geometry down to heights of approximately 80 nm. At smaller separations, systematic deviations from the catenoidal profile emerge, indicating a crossover from a surface tension-dominated regime to a confinement-dominated regime. Overall, we demonstrate composition profiling as a framework to analyse confinement-induced composition variations and to quantify interfacial thermodynamic effects at the nanoscale.

</details>

### [165] [Late-Time Oscillating Quintessence in Light of DESI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24221)
*Jun-Qian Jiang,Mustafa A. Amin,Arman Shafieloo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究一种能在近期（红移z≈0.1）开始振荡的早期哈勃冻结（Hubble frozen）精质场（quintessence）暗能量模型，该模型相比ΛCDM可将拟合优度提升Δχ²≈-9，且其扰动增长和积分 Sachs-Wolfe（ISW）贡献在最佳拟合区保持较小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DESI重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）测量结合Ia型超新星和宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据，暗示暗能量（dark energy）可能存在低红移动力学行为，亟需简单且物理透明的模型来刻画此类动力学。

Method: 采用一个在宇宙历史大部分时期被哈勃冻结、近期（z≈0.1）才开始在其势能最小值附近振荡的精质场模型；该类模型要求精质场势能在远离最小值处坡度平缓、靠近最小值处坡度变陡。

Result: 该振荡精质场（oscillating quintessence）模型相比ΛCDM可将拟合优度改进Δχ²≈-9，在与相同参数数量的常见唯象暗能量参数化（phenomenological dark energy parameterization）对比时仍具竞争力；该偏好主要来自背景膨胀历史（background expansion history），且在最佳拟合区附近精质场扰动的共振增长及相关的ISW贡献均较小。

Conclusion: 更精确的低红移距离测量以及ISW效应和引力透镜（lensing）等晚期探针，有助于区分该振荡精质场模型与其他形式的晚期暗能量动力学。

Abstract: Recent DESI baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, especially when combined with Type Ia supernova and CMB data, sharpen the case for possible low-redshift dynamics in the dark energy sector. We study a simple and physically transparent realization of such dynamics: a quintessence field that is Hubble frozen for most of cosmic history and starts to oscillate around its minimum recently (at a redshift $z\approx 0.1$). This late onset of oscillations can occur in a broad class of models where the quintessence potentials have a shallow slope away from the minimum and steepen near it. This class of models can improve the fit relative to $Λ$CDM, with $Δχ^2\simeq -9$, while remaining competitive with common phenomenological dark energy parameterizations with the same number of parameters. The preference is driven mainly by the background expansion history, and near the best-fit region the resonant growth of quintessence perturbations and the associated Integrated Sachs-Wolfe (ISW) contribution remain small. More precise low-redshift distance measurements, together with late-time probes such as the ISW effect and lensing, may help distinguish this oscillating quintessence scenario from other forms of late-time dark energy dynamics.

### [166] [Minimal Extensions of the $α$-Starobinsky Model: Reconciling ACT DR6 and Reheating Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24131)
*Nehla Shobcha,Norma Sidik Risdianto,Romy Hanang Setya Budhi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 针对ACT、Planck和DESI联合数据揭示的标准α-Starobinsky暴胀模型预测的标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）n_s与观测值之间约2σ的偏差，本文提出两类最小修正方案（指数型和多项式型），均通过单一小参数δ调控，成功将n_s移入1σ置信区间，同时满足张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）上限r<0.038，并给出可行的参数空间和再加热温度（reheating temperature）T_re ~ 10^9 GeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联合数据分析表明，标准α-Starobinsky暴胀模型预测的标量谱指数n_s与最新观测值之间存在约2σ的偏差，亟需对模型进行最小修正以消除这一张力。

Method: 在保持原模型平台结构与吸引子性质的前提下，引入两类由单一小参数δ>0调控的修正：乘法指数型修改和加法多项式型变形。解析推导慢滚参数及暴胀可观测量至δ的二阶，并结合一致性方程（consistency equation）整合再加热动力学。

Result: δ项有效将n_s移入P-ACT-LB-BK18联合数据集的1σ置信区间，且不违反张标比上限r<0.038。指数型模型在1σ下要求α≲35、δ~O(10^{-2})；加法型模型在p=1时要求δ~O(10^{-3})，p=2时δ~O(10^{-4})。所有可行方案对应的再加热温度T_re ~ 10^9 GeV，高于大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, BBN）下限且低于引力子超产生上限。

Conclusion: 两类最小修正均可有效缓解标准α-Starobinsky暴胀模型与最新宇宙学观测之间的张力，且理论上自洽、参数空间合理，为后续精细检验提供了明确的理论候选。

Abstract: The latest combined data from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) DR6, Planck, and DESI yields a scalar spectral index $n_s = 0.9743 \pm 0.0034$, which lies approximately $2σ$ above the prediction of the standard $α$-Starobinsky inflation model. To address this tension, we propose two minimal extensions that preserve the model's plateau structure and attractor properties: a multiplicative exponential modification and an additive polynomial deformation, both governed by a single small perturbative parameter $δ>0$. We analytically derive the slow-roll parameters and inflationary observables up to second order in $δ$ and integrate them with reheating dynamics via the consistency equation. It is shown that the $δ$ term effectively shifts $n_s$ into the $1σ$ confidence region of the joint P-ACT-LB-BK18 dataset without violating the tensor-to-scalar ratio bound ($r < 0.038$). The viable parameter space at $1σ$ requires $α\lesssim 35$ with $δ\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-2})$ for the exponential model, while the additive model requires $δ\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$ for $p=1$ and $δ\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$ for $p=2$. For the e-folding range $N_k \in [50, 65]$, the relevant reheating equation of state is $0<ω_{\mathrm{re}}\le1$. All viable scenarios yield a reheating temperature $T_{\mathrm{re}} \sim 10^9$ GeV, which is safely above the Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) bound and below the gravitino overproduction limit.

</details>


### [167] [The Topology of the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24886)
*Craig J. Copi,Deyan P. Mihaylov,Anna Negro,Amirhossein Samandar,Glenn D. Starkman,Yashar Akrami,George Alestas,Stefano Anselmi,Javier Carrón Duque,Fernando Cornet-Gomez,Linn Htat Lu,Andrew H. Jaffe,Arthur Kosowsky,Mikel Martin Barandiaran,Thiago S. Pereira,Catherine Petretti,Andrius Tamosiunas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文综述了利用宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）和物质三维分布探测宇宙非平凡拓扑（non-trivial cosmic topology）的研究进展。尽管WMAP和Planck等任务至今未发现确凿证据，但近期理论进展表明，即使拓扑尺度大于可见宇宙，仍可能存在可探测信号。未来LiteBIRD、Taurus等CMB实验以及高精度星系巡天有望进一步拓展可探测参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙在最大尺度上是否无限且各向同性？非平凡宇宙拓扑会破坏统计各向同性（statistical isotropy）乃至均匀性（homogeneity），从而留下可观测印记。检测这些印记是唯一能够确定宇宙整体拓扑结构的途径，具有根本性的宇宙学意义。

Method: 综述了多种搜索方法，包括寻找匹配圆对（matched circle pairs）以及基于拓扑相关协方差矩阵（topology-dependent covariance matrices）的全贝叶斯似然分析（full Bayesian likelihood analysis）。数据来源涵盖WMAP和Planck等空间任务的CMB观测，以及未来计划中的LiteBIRD、Taurus实验和高精度星系巡天及谱线强度映射巡天（line intensity-mapping surveys）。

Result: 迄今为止的搜索未发现非平凡拓扑的确凿证据；当前约束仅排除了部分拓扑、参数范围和观测者位置。然而，近期理论进展表明，即使拓扑尺度超过可见宇宙大小，可探测信号仍可能存在。未来实验可通过利用偏振数据（polarisation data）和探索所有可及红移处的拓扑诱导关联来扩展可探测参数空间。

Conclusion: 宇宙拓扑是否可观测仍不确定，但当前和未来的观测数据为探测宇宙整体结构提供了前所未有的机遇。

Abstract: Is the Universe infinite in all directions? The only way to know is to look. A non-trivial cosmic topology would imprint subtle signatures on the cosmic microwave background (CMB) and on the three-dimensional distribution of matter, breaking statistical isotropy and, potentially, homogeneity at the largest scales. If the topology scale is small enough, these signatures would be observable. Over the past three decades, successive space missions, most notably WMAP and $\textit{Planck}$, have enabled sophisticated searches for these signatures, using methods ranging from looking for matched circle pairs to full Bayesian likelihood analysis based on topology-dependent covariance matrices. Although these searches have yielded no definitive evidence for non-trivial topology, current constraints exclude only some topologies, parameter ranges, and observer positions. Recent advances show that detectable signals may persist even when the topology scale exceeds the size of the visible Universe. Planned CMB experiments, including LiteBIRD and $\textit{Taurus}$, and high-precision galaxy and line intensity-mapping surveys, could expand the detectable parameter space by exploiting polarisation data, and by exploring topology-induced correlations at all accessible redshifts. Whether cosmic topology is observable remains uncertain, but current and future data offer an unprecedented opportunity to probe the global structure of the Universe.

</details>

### [168] [Brane quantization of $A_n$-resolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24249)
*Yat-Hin Suen,Yutung Yau*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文通过SYZ镜像对称（SYZ mirror symmetry）扩展了膜量子化（brane quantization）在奇异纤维上的研究，在$A_n$奇点的双有理分辨（crepant resolution）中构造了空间填充的共轭A-膜（coisotropic A-brane）及其镜像B-膜（mirror B-brane），并通过壁穿越公式（wall-crossing formulas）粘合解析量子环面（analytic quantum tori）建立了两者内射代数之间的镜像同构（mirror isomorphism）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将半平坦情形下基于SYZ镜像对称的膜量子化方法推广到奇异纤维情形，以处理具有奇点结构的镜像对。

Method: 以$A_n$奇点$\mathbb{C}^2/\mathbb{Z}_{n+1}$的双有理分辨$X$为对象，其镜像$\check{X}$也被实现为同一空间的分辨；对每个正整数$k$，构造空间填充的共轭A-膜$\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)}$，并通过纤维逐点几何量子化（fiberwise geometric quantization）确定其镜像B-膜$\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)}$；随后利用壁穿越公式粘合解析量子环面，定义A-膜内射代数$Hom_A(\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)},\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)})$。

Result: 建立了A-膜内射代数$Hom_A(\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)},\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)})$与B-膜内射代数$Hom_B(\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)},\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)})$之间的镜像同构。

Conclusion: 论文成功将膜量子化方法从半平坦情形推广至$A_n$奇点奇异纤维情形，验证了对应镜像对之间内射代数的同构性。

Abstract: We extend the study of brane quantization via SYZ mirror symmetry to the setting of singular fibers, building on recent joint work with Chan, Leung, and Li in the semi-flat case. We consider a crepant resolution $X\to\mathbb{C}^2/\mathbb{Z}_{n+1}$ of the $A_n$-singularity, whose mirror $\check{X}$ is also realized as a resolution of $\mathbb{C}^2/\mathbb{Z}_{n+1}$. For each level $k\in\mathbb{Z}_{>0}$, we construct a space filling coisotropic A-brane $\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)}$ of $(X,kω)$ and determine its mirror B-brane $\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)}$ via fiberwise geometric quantization. We then define the endomorphism algebra $Hom_A(\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)},\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)})$ by gluing analytic quantum tori using wall-crossing formulas and establish a mirror isomorphism $Hom_A(\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)},\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)})\cong Hom_B(\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)},\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)})$.

</details>


### [169] [$p$-adic integrable systems: from biquadratic equations to local models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24363)
*Luis Crespo,Álvaro Pelayo*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文针对$p$进解析可积系统$F=(f_1,\ldots,f_n):(M,ω)\to(\mathbb{Q}_p)^n$的局部规范形（local normal form）计算问题，引入新技术（几乎特征向量与对齐辛坐标）以显式求解四维情形下的双二次方程，并展示了该方法在$p$耦合角动量研究中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解$p$进解析可积系统（$p$-adic analytic integrable systems）的局部规范形对于掌握其几何与动力学性质至关重要，但在某些情形（如四维）下显式确定这些规范形仍具挑战性。本文旨在引入能够计算这些局部规范形信息的技术。

Method: 本文引入两种新概念——几乎特征向量（almost eigenvectors）和对齐辛坐标（aligned symplectic coordinates）——作为技术工具。所提方法覆盖四维空间中的所有情形，核心步骤是求解双二次方程（biquadratic equations）。证明过程结合了解析估计（analytic estimates）与$p$进扩张域的伽罗瓦理论（Galois theory of $p$-adic extension fields），并利用了作者此前对规范形的分类结果。

Result: 所提出的技术能够有效计算四维$p$进解析可积系统的局部规范形信息，并成功应用于研究$p$耦合角动量（$p$-coupled angular momentum）。新定义的几乎特征向量与对齐辛坐标不仅服务于证明，本身也具有独立的研究价值。

Conclusion: 本文的主要结论陈述自包含（self-contained），不要求读者预先掌握$p$进可积系统或$p$进辛几何的背景知识，便于更广泛的数学研究者理解和使用。

Abstract: Let $p$ be a prime number and $n$ a positive integer. The study of normal forms of $p$-adic analytic integrable systems $F=(f_1,\ldots,f_n):(M,ω)\to(\mathbb{Q}_p)^n$ is essential to understand their geometrical and dynamical properties. Even though in some cases, such as dimension $4$, there is a classification of the local normal forms, it can be a challenge to determine them explicitly. Our goal in this paper is to introduce techniques to compute information about these local normal forms. We then explain how this is useful for instance to study the $p$-coupled angular momentum. The techniques we introduce cover all cases in dimension $4$ and require solving biquadratic equations. Along the way we define two new notions: almost eigenvectors and aligned symplectic coordinates. They are useful to prove our results but also of independent interest. The proofs use our previous classification of normal forms and rely on a combination of analytic estimates and Galois theory of $p$-adic extension fields. However, the statements of the main results are essentially self-contained and do not require prior knowledge of $p$-adic integrable systems or $p$-adic symplectic geometry.

</details>

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [170] [Bode-Fano Limits to Broadband Absorption by Small Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24658)
*Emanuele Corsaro,Andrea Alù,Carlo Forestiere*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 通过将亚波长物体的电磁散射严格映射为等效阻抗匹配问题，推导出无源、因果、线性、时间色散亚波长物体的基本吸收带宽极限，为宽带光收集和耗散提供了根本性限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管亚波长纳米结构可以在谐振时高效吸收光，但因果性（causality）和无源性（passivity）从根本上限制了其维持强吸收的带宽，现有理论尚未给出这类物体的普适性吸收带宽上限。

Method: 将电磁散射（electromagnetic scattering）问题严格重构为等效阻抗匹配（impedance-matching）问题，从而应用Bode-Fano型约束（Bode-Fano-type constraints）来推导无源、因果、线性、时间色散亚波长物体的吸收带宽极限。

Result: 得到了光学吸收的Bode-Fano型约束条件，并给出了可逼近这些极限的无源纳米颗粒材料色散（material dispersion）的理性合成指南。

Conclusion: 该结果阐明了宽带光收集和耗散的终极极限，对太阳能转换（solar-energy conversion）、光热热疗（photothermal hyperthermia）、热管理（thermal management）及相关纳米光子技术具有重要启示。

Abstract: Nanostructures can be designed to absorb light efficiently at resonance despite their subwavelength footprint, but causality and passivity fundamentally limit the bandwidth over which strong absorption can be maintained. Here we derive fundamental absorption-bandwidth limits for passive, causal, linear, and temporally dispersive subwavelength objects by rigorously casting electromagnetic scattering as an equivalent impedance-matching problem. This mapping yields ultimate Bode-Fano-type constraints for optical absorption and provides rational synthesis guidelines for the material dispersion of passive nanoparticles that can approach the bounds. Our results clarify the ultimate limits for broadband light harvesting and dissipation, with implications for solar-energy conversion, photothermal hyperthermia, thermal management, and related nanophotonic technologies.

</details>
